# Skyrim:Fire Mage

## Overview

**Fire Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Fire Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of fire mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level fire mages even at high levels, but boss-level fire mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Fire Mages

A Novice Fire Mage attacks with a blast of flame

Fire mages rely on their devastating fire-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, fire mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, fire mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers have the same gear as lower-level fire mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Fire Mage Bosses

Apprentice Fire Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level fire mages listed above. Fire Mage Adepts, Fire Mages, Fire Wizards and Pyromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers listed above, with the exception that Fire Mage Adepts and Fire Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts") rather than a Staff of Fireballs.

## Named Fire Mages

| Name | Location | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") | [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") | A representative of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") serving as an advisor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") | Wilderness | A pilgrim on her way to see the restored [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [The Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller") | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") | The elemental mage leader of the mages found in the keep (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") | [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage") | A hostile elemental mage living south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo") | [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") | A Thalmor agent working for Ancano |
| [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") | [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") | A master wizard at the College of Winterhold, reporting directly to the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") |
| [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked") | [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") | An Altmer experimenting with magic on live subjects within the fort |
| [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") | [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") | A Nord elemental mage performing sadistic experiments within the ruin |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic fire mages that are Dark Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means fire mages are slightly more likely to be Dark Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Fire Mage

## Overview

**Fire Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Fire Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of fire mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level fire mages even at high levels, but boss-level fire mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Fire Mages

A Novice Fire Mage attacks with a blast of flame

Fire mages rely on their devastating fire-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, fire mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, fire mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers have the same gear as lower-level fire mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Fire Mage Bosses

Apprentice Fire Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level fire mages listed above. Fire Mage Adepts, Fire Mages, Fire Wizards and Pyromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers listed above, with the exception that Fire Mage Adepts and Fire Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts") rather than a Staff of Fireballs.

## Named Fire Mages

| Name | Location | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") | [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") | A representative of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") serving as an advisor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") | Wilderness | A pilgrim on her way to see the restored [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [The Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller") | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") | The elemental mage leader of the mages found in the keep (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") | [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage") | A hostile elemental mage living south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo") | [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") | A Thalmor agent working for Ancano |
| [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") | [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") | A master wizard at the College of Winterhold, reporting directly to the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") |
| [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked") | [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") | An Altmer experimenting with magic on live subjects within the fort |
| [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") | [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") | A Nord elemental mage performing sadistic experiments within the ruin |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic fire mages that are Dark Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means fire mages are slightly more likely to be Dark Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Fire Mage

## Overview

**Fire Mages** are enemy spellcasters who specialize in the [Fire Damage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Damage "Skyrim:Fire Damage") branch of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") magic. They are typically found in a few caves, keeps, and ruins across [Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyrim "Skyrim:Skyrim") known as [warlock lairs](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock_Lairs "Category:Skyrim-Places-Warlock Lairs"). Like other elemental mages ([ice mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") and [storm mages](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")), they belong to the [Fire/Frost/Shock Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock_Mage "Skyrim:Fire/Frost/Shock Mage") [NPC](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs "Skyrim:NPCs") class.

The type of fire mage you encounter depends on your level. You will continue to meet low-level fire mages even at high levels, but boss-level fire mages will always be at the highest possible level.

### Fire Mages

A Novice Fire Mage attacks with a blast of flame

Fire mages rely on their devastating fire-based spells in combat, and carry a leveled dagger in case of close-quarters fighting ([iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), [steel](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), [orcish](/wiki/Skyrim:Orcish_Dagger "Skyrim:Orcish Dagger"), [dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Dagger "Skyrim:Dwarven Dagger"), [elven](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Dagger "Skyrim:Elven Dagger"), [glass](/wiki/Skyrim:Glass_Dagger "Skyrim:Glass Dagger"), or an enchanted dagger of any quality from iron to [Daedric](/wiki/Skyrim:Daedric "Skyrim:Daedric")). They also have a 10% chance to carry a leveled [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") or Destruction staff.

They wear a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000c5d12 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), [hooded black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Black Mage Robes"), robes of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Alteration "Skyrim:Fortify Alteration"), robes of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Destruction "Skyrim:Fortify Destruction"), robes of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Restoration "Skyrim:Fortify Restoration"), or robes of [Fortify Magicka Rate](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka_Rate "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka Rate").

In addition to the gear listed above, fire mages have a small chance to carry [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), Novice or Apprentice level [spell tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") (common, uncommon, or rare), [recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Recipes "Skyrim:Recipes"), and a small amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). They also have [atronach forge recipes](/wiki/Skyrim:Atronach_Forge_Recipe "Skyrim:Atronach Forge Recipe") in their inventories, but their chance of appearing in-game is set at 0%.

On death, fire mages have a 10% chance to drop potions and poisons, and a 5% chance to drop one of the following scrolls:

- **Alteration:** [Scroll of Mass Paralysis](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mass_Paralysis "Skyrim:Scroll of Mass Paralysis")
- **Conjuration:** [Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Storm_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Storm Atronach"), [Scroll of Dread Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Dread_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Dread Zombie")
- **Destruction:**[Scroll of Blizzard](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Blizzard "Skyrim:Scroll of Blizzard"), [Scroll of Fire Storm](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Fire_Storm "Skyrim:Scroll of Fire Storm")
- **Illusion:** [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms"), [Scroll of Harmony](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Harmony "Skyrim:Scroll of Harmony"), [Scroll of Hysteria](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Hysteria "Skyrim:Scroll of Hysteria"), [Scroll of Mayhem](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Mayhem "Skyrim:Scroll of Mayhem")
- **Restoration:** [Scroll of Bane of the Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Bane_of_the_Undead "Skyrim:Scroll of Bane of the Undead"), [Scroll of Guardian Circle](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Guardian_Circle "Skyrim:Scroll of Guardian Circle")

Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers have the same gear as lower-level fire mages, but have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Fireballs](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Fireballs "Skyrim:Staff of Fireballs") and do not have the leveled lists for atronach forge recipes.

### Fire Mage Bosses

Apprentice Fire Mage bosses have the same inventory as the lower-level fire mages listed above. Fire Mage Adepts, Fire Mages, Fire Wizards and Pyromancer bosses have the same inventory as the Pyromancers and Arch Pyromancers listed above, with the exception that Fire Mage Adepts and Fire Mages have a 50% chance to carry a [Staff of Firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts") rather than a Staff of Fireballs.

## Named Fire Mages

| Name | Location | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Ancano](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancano "Skyrim:Ancano") | [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements") | A representative of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor") serving as an advisor at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| [Ardwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Ardwen "Skyrim:Ardwen") | Wilderness | A pilgrim on her way to see the restored [Gildergreen](/wiki/Lore:Gildergreen "Lore:Gildergreen") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [The Caller](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Caller "Skyrim:The Caller") | [Fellglow Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellglow_Keep "Skyrim:Fellglow Keep") | The elemental mage leader of the mages found in the keep (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Drelas](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas "Skyrim:Drelas") | [Drelas' Cottage](/wiki/Skyrim:Drelas%27_Cottage "Skyrim:Drelas' Cottage") | A hostile elemental mage living south of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") (can also be an [ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Mage "Skyrim:Ice Mage") or [storm mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Storm_Mage "Skyrim:Storm Mage")) |
| [Estormo](/wiki/Skyrim:Estormo "Skyrim:Estormo") | [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") | A Thalmor agent working for Ancano |
| [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine") | [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment") | A master wizard at the College of Winterhold, reporting directly to the [Arch-Mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Savos_Aren "Skyrim:Savos Aren") |
| [Naris the Wicked](/wiki/Skyrim:Naris_the_Wicked "Skyrim:Naris the Wicked") | [Morvunskar](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvunskar "Skyrim:Morvunskar") | An Altmer experimenting with magic on live subjects within the fort |
| [Sild the Warlock](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") | [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast") | A Nord elemental mage performing sadistic experiments within the ruin |

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

### World Interactions

- **[Wizard Duel](/wiki/Skyrim:World_Interactions#Wizard_Duel "Skyrim:World Interactions")**

## Dialogue

All members of the Warlock faction share a set of generic dialogue which they will use when in combat:

*"You cannot even conceive of the power I wield..."*

*"Fire, frost, or lightning - you will suffer at my hands!"*

*"Don't you see? I am master of the arcane!"*

*"Behold my power!"*

*"The elements are mine to command!"*

## Notes

- All the generic fire mages that are Dark Elves are listed twice in the leveled lists, which means fire mages are slightly more likely to be Dark Elves than one of the other races.

# Skyrim:Fire Spirit

## Overview

| Fire Spirit (RefID: 000F82BD) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Fire_Spirit "Lore:Fire Spirit")) | | | |

| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000F82BD | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000F82BC |
| Other Information | | | |

| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction")**, [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), [Sneak](/wiki/Skyrim:Sneak "Skyrim:Sneak") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [DraugrFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DraugrFaction "Skyrim:DraugrFaction") | | |

Fire Spirit

The **Fire Spirit** will be encountered in [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian") during the quest [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus"). It is found inside a chamber with a flaming sealed door. Approaching the door will spawn the spirit.

The Fire Spirit wears an unobtainable set of [ancient Nord armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Armor "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Armor") and wields two leveled [ancient Nord swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Sword "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Sword"), which may be up to [honed](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Ancient_Nord_Sword "Skyrim:Honed Ancient Nord Sword") in quality. It also knows the [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") and [Wall of Flames](/wiki/Skyrim:Wall_of_Flames "Skyrim:Wall of Flames") spells. The Fire Spirit also has a special passive ability that gives it its flaming appearance, as well as providing a 33 percent [resistance to fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Resist Fire") at the cost of a 33 percent [weakness to frost](/wiki/Skyrim:Weakness_to_Frost "Skyrim:Weakness to Frost").

## Related Quests

- **[The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus")**: Retrieve the [Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:Staff of Magnus").

# Skyrim:Firir

## Overview

| Firir (RefID: 0007B703) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Chillwind Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillwind_Depths "Skyrim:Chillwind Depths") | | |
| Race | [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0007B703 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000976FB |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| Voice Type | [FemaleCommoner](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner "Category:Skyrim-Voice-FemaleCommoner") | | |

Firir's body in a Falmer cage

**Firir** is a [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [farmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Farmer_(class) "Skyrim:Farmer (class)") found dead in [Chillwind Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Chillwind_Depths "Skyrim:Chillwind Depths") after chasing a lead on a brutal assault on a merchant caravan. He wears only a [roughspun tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Roughspun_Tunic "Skyrim:Roughspun Tunic") with no shoes, and carries at least 25 gold.

## Notes

- A [torn note](/wiki/Skyrim:Torn_Note "Skyrim:Torn Note") is found on his body in the cave, apologizing for his death to his love, "Eydis". It is unclear if this is the [Eydis](/wiki/Skyrim:Eydis "Skyrim:Eydis") at [Old Hroldan Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Hroldan_Inn "Skyrim:Old Hroldan Inn"), as her "missing" husband is claimed to be a soldier and not named at any point. Additionally, bringing the note to Eydis has no effect.

## Bugs

- Firir has the `FemaleCommoner` voice type. This results in a female voice if the body is [resurrected](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate "Skyrim:Reanimate").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:First Edition

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Locate an important [folio](/wiki/Skyrim:Lusty_Argonian_Maid_Folio "Skyrim:Lusty Argonian Maid Folio") for [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano") |
| Location(s): | [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") |
| Reward: | Leveled enchanted jewelry |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1([Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano")) |
| ID: | DLC2RRFavor07 |
| Suggested Level: | 10 |

The Strident Squall

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
2. Retrieve the *[Lusty Argonian Maid Folio](/wiki/Skyrim:Lusty_Argonian_Maid_Folio "Skyrim:Lusty Argonian Maid Folio")*.
3. Return the folio to Cindiri.

### A Precious Heirloom

The biggest bookstore in [Cyrodiil](/wiki/Lore:Cyrodiil "Lore:Cyrodiil") is called [First Edition](/wiki/Oblivion:First_Edition "Oblivion:First Edition") and is located in the [Market District](/wiki/Oblivion:Market_District "Oblivion:Market District") of the capital of Cyrodiil, the [Imperial City](/wiki/Oblivion:Imperial_City "Oblivion:Imperial City"). The bookstore is famous for its various limited editions of numerous rare books and also delivers to citizens outside of Cyrodiil, for example to [Cindiri Arano](/wiki/Skyrim:Cindiri_Arano "Skyrim:Cindiri Arano") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"). Once you have [freed Cindiri](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_the_Stones "Skyrim:Cleansing the Stones") from [Miraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Miraak_(person) "Skyrim:Miraak (person)")'s spell, she will greet you with: *"You look able enough to venture outside of town. Perhaps you could help me recover something precious that was lost?"* When asked to elaborate she will explain that she had an important folio rebound at the First Edition bookstore. Unfortunately, the folio never made its way back to Raven Rock. When you ask her if it was aboard a ship she will say: *"Yes, the "Strident Squall" or something like that. The damn thing sunk right off the coast of Solstheim. Can you imagine?"* She then explains that one of the sailors managed to crawl back to Raven Rock and tell the [guards](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard "Skyrim:Redoran Guard") about the wreckage. When you offer to locate the folio for her, she will be grateful and even refer to it as a 'precious heirloom' to the family.

### The Strident Squall

You will not receive a map marker, nor will any citizens help you find the wreck. However, the [Wreck of the Strident Squall](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Strident_Squall "Skyrim:Wreck of the Strident Squall") is clearly visible on your map, at the southeastern tip of Solstheim. Travel to the wreck and fight five leveled [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver"), including a Reaver Lord; one sits on a chair on the ground while the remaining four will shoot at you from the deck. When the coast is clear examine the ship for several valuable items, including an East Empire Company strongbox containing an [East Empire Pendant](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") on some shelves below deck. Go behind the stairs you came down on and turn so that they are on your right. There will be a chest slightly to the right of a large hole in the hull which contains the folio, a [special edition](/wiki/Skyrim:Lusty_Argonian_Maid_Folio "Skyrim:Lusty Argonian Maid Folio") of the naughty tome *[The Lusty Argonian Maid](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid")*.

Return to Raven Rock and locate Cindiri Arano. When you hand her the missing folio she will be ecstatic: *"You have no idea what this means to me... to my family. Reclamations bless you! Well, you've certainly proven your worth around here to me. Please, accept this gift as a token of my appreciation!"* She will then hand you the reward, a leveled and enchanted ring, necklace, or circlet.

## Notes

- If you find the folio at the shipwreck before initiating the quest, you can simply speak to her, return it, and receive your reward all at once.

## Quest Stages

| First Edition (DLC2RRFavor07) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Locate Cindiri's Folio from the wreck of the Strident Squall |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Return the Folio to Cindiri Arano in Raven Rock |
| 200 | ☑ |  |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2RRFavor07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2RRFavor07`.

# Skyrim:First Lessons

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-College of Winterhold.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-College_of_Winterhold.png) | **Join the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location(s): | [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") |
| Reward: | Membership, [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward") spell |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | 0→1 ([Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir")) |
| ID: | MG01 |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | |  | **Next →** [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | → Next | [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") | | |

Faralda at the entrance bridge

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Approach the bridge to [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").
2. Speak to [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda").
3. Prove your ability *or* persuade her, provided you have a high enough Speech skill.
4. Cross the bridge and enter the courtyard.
5. (Optional) Speak to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine").
6. Enter the [Hall of the Elements](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Elements "Skyrim:Hall of the Elements").
7. Listen to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir")'s lecture and participate.

### Entrance Exam

Before heading to [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") to start this quest, you may want to check whether you have enough [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") to complete the quest's first challenge—you may need as much as 135 magicka. With the [novice hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Novice_Hood "Skyrim:Novice Hood") found in [Helgen Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen_Keep "Skyrim:Helgen Keep") during [Unbound](/wiki/Skyrim:Unbound "Skyrim:Unbound"), even new level-one characters will have 130 magicka. If you do not have other [Fortify Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Fortify_Magicka "Skyrim:Fortify Magicka") apparel or potions, one option available to everyone is to visit the [Temple of the Divines](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_the_Divines "Skyrim:Temple of the Divines") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") and activate the shrine of Julianos to obtain 25 more magicka from the [Blessing of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Blessing_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Blessing of Julianos"). If you have the [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") add-on installed, you may choose the power [Secret of Arcana](/wiki/Skyrim:Secret_of_Arcana "Skyrim:Secret of Arcana") from the black book *[Filament and Filigree](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Book:_Filament_and_Filigree_(quest) "Skyrim:Black Book: Filament and Filigree (quest)")* and all your spells will cost no magicka for 30 seconds.

Once in Winterhold, follow the main road west through town, and approach the prominent bridge connecting the town to the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). Standing at the approach of the bridge is [Faralda](/wiki/Skyrim:Faralda "Skyrim:Faralda"). She will ask you about your intentions and what you expect to find on entering the college. Several options would be available for you.

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| I want to use the power of ice and fire to destroy any who oppose me. | I see. That power certainly exists, I assure you. Wield it faithfully, and few can withstand you. |
| I desire to bend the will of those around me. | Yes, the school of Illusion can be quite influential. Kings have risen to power because of it, and empires have been razed with it. |
| I want to unravel the mysteries of Aetherius. | Ah, the immortal plane. It is said to be the source of all magic. This is a noble goal, indeed. |
| I seek the knowledge of the Elder Scrolls.[†](#intnote_.E2.80.A0) | Do you? It is true there are some here who have spent years studying the accumulated knowledge of the scrolls. But what you seek does not come easily, and can destroy those without a strong will. |
| I just wanted to see what it looks like inside. | Ha! Humor is often in short supply here. But I sense that perhaps you're after more than just that. |

[†](#note_.E2.80.A0)Only available during the quests [Elder Knowledge](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder_Knowledge "Skyrim:Elder Knowledge") and [Scroll Scouting](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_Scouting "Skyrim:Scroll Scouting")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") or if you have completed those quests without speaking to Faralda previously.

Regardless of the dialogue options you choose, she will ultimately decide that you need a lesson and will say that you must take a small test to show that you have some degree of skill with magic.

If you agree, she will randomly select one spell from any one of the five schools of magic for you to cast. This may be:

- Casting a [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") at the eye-shaped seal next to her.
- [Conjuring a Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach") on the seal.
- Casting [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Fear_(spell) "Skyrim:Fear (spell)") at the seal.
- Casting [Healing Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_Hands "Skyrim:Healing Hands") on her.
- Casting [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight") at the seal.

If you do not have the spell she asks of you, she will offer to teach it to you for 30 gold. This is an easy and cheap way to learn any one of the above spells.

You must cast the spell at the circular impression in the floor behind her. Casting the spell in any other location will not progress the quest. However, if she asks you to conjure a Flame Atronach, and you already have a Flame Thrall summoned, simply exiting the conversation and speaking to her again will successfully progress the dialogue.

Alternatively, you can attempt to persuade her and avoid this test. In order to persuade her, you will need a Speech skill of 100 (70 with the [Persuasion](/wiki/Skyrim:Persuasion "Skyrim:Persuasion") perk) or the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation"). If you are on the quest Elder Knowledge you can also mention that you are [Dragonborn](/wiki/Skyrim:Dovahkiin "Skyrim:Dovahkiin"). She will then ask to see a [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"). Either of these will get you in without needing to cast a spell.

Regardless of which path you take, Faralda will allow you across the bridge and direct you to [Mirabelle Ervine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirabelle_Ervine "Skyrim:Mirabelle Ervine").

### College Orientation Day

After you speak to Mirabelle Ervine, she will want to give you a tour of the facilities. Before that, however, she will give you three items to wear (although wearing them is not mandatory for membership): a Novice Hood (+30 to Magicka), a Novice Robes of Destruction (-12% to Destruction Spell Magicka Cost, Magicka regenerates 50% faster) and College Boots (unenchanted).

As you follow her around the college, she will point and explain the few areas and what their purpose is.

She will lead you to your new quarters, which is an Apprentice room in the [Hall of Attainment](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_Attainment "Skyrim:Hall of Attainment"), a circular chamber with five rooms total. One room is assigned to each of the apprentices, and one to Tolfdir. Your room is the first on the right, and includes a bed, several furniture containers, and some starting items such as a few [soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"). The furniture containers (wardrobes, end tables, and drawer) are safe for storage, but the food barrels respawn and are unsafe.

### Join the Lecture

*"Welcome, welcome! We were just beginning. Please, stay and listen."*

Upon completing the tour, Mirabelle will ask you to join Tolfdir's lecture in the lecture hall. Tolfdir will begin the lesson, addressing you and three of your peers. The other students will badger the professor to teach them a practical application of magic instead of lecturing about the importance of mitigating the damages. Eventually, Tolfdir will ask you what you think. Whatever your response, Tolfdir will ask you to perform a [Ward spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Ward_(spells) "Skyrim:Ward (spells)"). If you do not have this spell, he will give it to you freely. You will be asked to cast the spell and fend off his attack with it.

After you successfully defend yourself from one of his fire balls, the quest is finished, and Tolfdir will suggest a [school field trip](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") and you are off on the next quest.

### Achievements

One [achievement](/wiki/Skyrim:Achievements "Skyrim:Achievements") is unlocked during this quest, when Faralda allows you across the bridge:

-  **Gatekeeper** (10 points/Bronze)

## Notes

- You can buy the [Healing Hands](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing_Hands "Skyrim:Healing Hands"), [Magelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Magelight "Skyrim:Magelight"), [Fear](/wiki/Skyrim:Fear_(spell) "Skyrim:Fear (spell)"), [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach"), or [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt") spell from Faralda (depending on which is required for your test) for cheaper than the tome is offered in stores. If you want to purchase a specific spell cheaply, you can save before initiating the quest and reload to try again. You will also learn the [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration_Spells "Skyrim:Restoration Spells") spell while listening to [Tolfdir](/wiki/Skyrim:Tolfdir "Skyrim:Tolfdir").
- If one of the three students die by any means, Tolfdir will cancel the ward training and immediately start the next quest.
- Without enough Magicka or spent Perks in Restoration, it may be difficult for some characters to maintain a Ward long enough for Tolfdir to even throw a firebolt. This can be bypassed by using Fortify Magicka potions, or more efficiently, either the [Spellbreaker](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellbreaker "Skyrim:Spellbreaker") shield or the [Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki_(item) "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki (item)") and their respective Ward effects.
- Several of the [college's optional quests](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(faction)#Optional_Quests "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (faction)") become available once First Lessons has been started, namely [Out of Balance](/wiki/Skyrim:Out_of_Balance "Skyrim:Out of Balance"), [Enchanting Pick-Up](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting_Pick-Up "Skyrim:Enchanting Pick-Up"), and [Restocking Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Restocking_Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Restocking Soul Gems"), [Fetch me that Book!](/wiki/Skyrim:Fetch_me_that_Book! "Skyrim:Fetch me that Book!"), and [Shalidor's Insights](/wiki/Skyrim:Shalidor%27s_Insights "Skyrim:Shalidor's Insights"). Another quest, [Filling Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Filling_Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Filling Soul Gems"), was supposed to be available following First Lessons, but was left unfinished and cannot be started. Most of the other optional quests do not become available until after the next quest, [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal"), has been completed.
- If you want to skip the tour, you can talk to Mirabelle Ervine and select the 'I was told to come see you' dialogue, then tell her 'I'm not ready to start the tour yet' and simply go into the Hall of Elements. The quest will progress normally once you start listening to Tolfdir's lecture.
- At the end of the lecture in this quest, Tolfdir's relationship with you is upgraded to friend.

## Bugs

- If you step in front of Faralda as she casts the spells during the walk up to the college, it will show up as a light spell on your character and will never light the podium.
- If interrupted during the tour (such as by a dragon), Mirabelle Ervine will not continue, saying only "after I have finished showing you the grounds we can talk". However, if you proceed to the Hall of Elements, Tolfdir will begin his lecture and you can complete the quest as if you had finished the tour. Mirabelle seems to return to normal behavior after this point.
- If you miss the first chance to defend yourself from Tolfdir's fireball, he may not throw another one at you, stalling the quest indefinitely.
  - Tolfdir will start firing the spell at you but will immediately stop. This can be solved by simply moving around for a bit on the spot, then start casting the Lesser Ward spell again.
  - It can also be solved by killing one of the students, running away to someplace outside of Winterhold, then paying up the 1000 gold bounty to the guards. That way Tolfdir will skip the training part, and start the [Under Saarthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Under_Saarthal "Skyrim:Under Saarthal") quest.
- If you dismiss a follower during the demonstration of wards there is a chance that the entire class and any faculty present will attack the follower. Since an essential follower stands up after kneeling for a bit, this results in a loop without a sufficient delay to continue the lesson.
  - Permanently killing the follower or reloading a previous save will successfully address this issue.
  - If you cast 'calm' on your follower, they will stop attacking Tolfdir and the students and you can then rehire them.
- Mirabelle can end up talking to herself if the scene between her and Ancano is interrupted.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- Oddly, since the [Jarl's Longhouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl%27s_Longhouse_(Winterhold) "Skyrim:Jarl's Longhouse (Winterhold)") is marked as being owned by the Winterhold crime faction, once you finish the quest, you will have helped someone in the hold, allowing you take things from the longhouse without it being considered theft.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, addresses this issue. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19319)) A new faction was created specifically for the residents of the longhouse in order to set ownership correctly.

## Quest Stages

| First Lessons (MG01) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've found the College of Winterhold, where mages study the arcane arts in Skyrim. If I want to learn more about magic, I'll need to join their ranks. *Objective 10:* Join the College of Winterhold |
| 20 |  | In order to join the College of Winterhold, I need to show I'm capable of simple magic by casting a Magelight spell.. *Objective 20:* Cast a Mage Light spell |
| 21 |  | In order to join the College of Winterhold, I need to show I'm capable of simple magic by summoning a Flame Atronach. *Objective 21:* Summon a Flame Atronach |
| 22 |  | In order to join the College of Winterhold, I need to show I'm capable of simple magic by casting a Firebolt spell. *Objective 22:* Cast a Firebolt spell |

| 200 | ☑ | After joining the College of Winterhold and speaking with Tolfdir, I've learned a bit about wards and will be accompanying some of the others on an expedition. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 3.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage MG01 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest MG01`.

# Skyrim:First Mate

## Overview

| First Mate (RefID: 000E5F36) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") | Gender | Male |
| Level | Radiant (1-25) | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000E5F36 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000E5F37 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 35-489 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 70-246 | | |
| Primary [Skills](/wiki/Skyrim:Skills "Skyrim:Skills") | **[One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed")**, **[Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed")**, [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block"), [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") | Unaggressive |
| Voice Type | [MaleOrc](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleOrc "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleOrc") | | |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFaction "Skyrim:BanditFaction") | | |

First Mate

The **First Mate**, an [Orc](/wiki/Skyrim:Orc "Skyrim:Orc") [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)"), is the second-in-command of a gang of [corsairs](/wiki/Skyrim:Corsair "Skyrim:Corsair") aboard the [Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload"), a ship tied up southwest of [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"). He spends all of his days aboard ship.

The first mate wears a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes#00086991 "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and a matching pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots#00086993 "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), and wields a leveled [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") of the best possible quality. He also carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload_Footlocker_Key "Skyrim:Dainty Sload Footlocker Key") to his footlocker and between 20 and 56 gold coins

## Related Quests

- **[The Dainty Sload](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:The Dainty Sload")**: Frame a [ship's](/wiki/Skyrim:Dainty_Sload "Skyrim:Dainty Sload") captain to get revenge for a [jilted merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur").

# Skyrim:Fisherman

## Overview

| Fisherman | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") | Gender | Radiant |
| Level | PC×0.5 (range=5-15) | Class | [Bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_(class) "Skyrim:Bandit (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | N/A | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00097976 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 35+(PC-2)×5.5 | | |
| [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 25 | | |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 25+(PC-2)×2 | | |
| [Morality](/wiki/Skyrim:Morality "Skyrim:Morality") | No Crime | [Aggression](/wiki/Skyrim:Aggression "Skyrim:Aggression") |  |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Fisherman Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Fisherman_Faction "Skyrim:Fisherman Faction"); [Crime Faction so crimes against created actors are registered](/wiki/Skyrim:Crime_Faction_so_crimes_against_created_actors_are_registered "Skyrim:Crime Faction so crimes against created actors are registered") | | |

A Fisherman found at [Crabber's Shanty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crabber%27s_Shanty "Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty")

.jpg)

The dead Fisherman at the Wreck of the Winter War (with [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") installed)

Four **Fishermen** can be found in various locations. They can be male or female of any race, and each one wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") with farm [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), and carries an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, they will be wearing [fishing apparel](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Items#Apparel "Skyrim:Fishing Items") instead and carry fishing rods. Unlike most hunters, fishermen do not offer trades.

## Dialogue

They have the same dialogue as generic [hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") encountered in the wilderness:

:   *"I've been hunting and fishing in these parts for years."*
:   *"It's not like my poaching is hurting anyone. The Jarl can hardly eat every deer now can he?"*
:   *"There's enough for all of us if you aren't greedy."*

## Locations

- [Crabber's Shanty](/wiki/Skyrim:Crabber%27s_Shanty "Skyrim:Crabber's Shanty"), a small shack on the River Hjaal.
- An [unmarked camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places#Hunter.2C_Fishermen_and_Other_Camps "Skyrim:Unmarked Places") south of [South Brittleshin Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:South_Brittleshin_Pass "Skyrim:South Brittleshin Pass") on an island on [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta"). [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-19784&y=-62304&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- An unmarked camp east of [Moss Mother Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Moss_Mother_Cavern "Skyrim:Moss Mother Cavern") on the northwest corner of Lake Ilinalta. [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?x=-46304&y=-46736&zoom=17&legacy=true)
- [Wreck of the Winter War](/wiki/Skyrim:Wreck_of_the_Winter_War "Skyrim:Wreck of the Winter War"), lying dead in a cage.

# Skyrim:Fishing Legend

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Catch rare fish.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water") |
| Location(s): | [Riften Fishery](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Fishery "Skyrim:Riften Fishery") |
| Reward: | [Fang of Haynekhtnamet](/wiki/Skyrim:Fang_of_Haynekhtnamet "Skyrim:Fang of Haynekhtnamet") |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ5 |
| Added by: | [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") |
| --- | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | **← Previous** [Darkest Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Depths "Skyrim:Darkest Depths") |  | | |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | ← Previous | [Darkest Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Depths "Skyrim:Darkest Depths") | | |

[File:SR-quest-Fishing Legend.jpg](/w/index.php?title=Special:Upload&wpDestFile=SR-quest-Fishing_Legend.jpg "File:SR-quest-Fishing Legend.jpg")

Fishing Legend

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water").
2. Read the [List of Rare Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Rare_Fish "Skyrim:List of Rare Fish").
3. Obtain an Angelfish.
4. Obtain an Angler.
5. Obtain a Lyretail Anthias.
6. Obtain a Scorpion Fish.
7. Return to Swims-In-Deep-Water.

## Detailed Walkthrough

Speak to [Swims-In-Deep-Water](/wiki/Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water "Skyrim:Swims-In-Deep-Water"):

:   **I'm ready for the next fishing challenge.**
:   *"Of course. It's all in this note."*
:   **I'll return with these rare catches soon.** / **This looks like it'll be a real challenge. I'll do my best.**
:   *"My thanks to you."*

He will then hand you a [list of rare fish](/wiki/Skyrim:List_of_Rare_Fish "Skyrim:List of Rare Fish") to catch

- [Angelfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Angelfish "Skyrim:Angelfish") - Angelfish are rare and can only be caught when fishing with an Alik'r Fishing Rod in temperate lakes. Two guaranteed Angelfish can be found in a pool within [Ancestor Glade](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestor_Glade "Skyrim:Ancestor Glade") and can be caught without a fishing rod.
- [Angler](/wiki/Skyrim:Angler "Skyrim:Angler") - Can only be caught in freezing waters while using the Argonian Fishing Rod. A lone Angler can be found at [Pilgrim's Trench](/wiki/Skyrim:Pilgrim%27s_Trench "Skyrim:Pilgrim's Trench") in a small rocky cove on the ocean floor (there are clams to the left and right of the mouth of the cove, and more on top of it), just to the west of the sunken ships, no fishing necessary. This is found in the Food section of Items.
- [Lyretail Anthias](/wiki/Skyrim:Lyretail_Anthias "Skyrim:Lyretail Anthias")- Can only be caught in temperate streams while using an Alik'r fishing rod. Three guaranteed Lyretails can be found in the waters of [Evergreen Grove](/wiki/Skyrim:Evergreen_Grove "Skyrim:Evergreen Grove").
- [Scorpion Fish](/wiki/Skyrim:Scorpion_Fish "Skyrim:Scorpion Fish") - Can only be caught in underground fishing spots while using the Argonian Fishing Rod. They can also be found in [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave"). This is found in the Food section of Items.

Return to Swims:

:   **It wasn't easy, but here are the fish you asked for.**
:   *"You are like my brood to me. Here. A token."*
:   **Are there any more fishing challenges you can give me?**
:   *"You've already learned all I can teach you."*

He will then reward you with the [Fang of Haynekhtnamet](/wiki/Skyrim:Fang_of_Haynekhtnamet "Skyrim:Fang of Haynekhtnamet").

## Bugs

Sometimes the fish you can pick up (not caught by fishing) mentioned above aren't there. If this happens, you can zone and zone back to get them to spawn. (For Ancestor Glade, leave the cave and zone back in. For Pilgrim's Trench, zone into nearby Ysgramor's Tomb and back out.)

## Quest Stages

| Fishing Legend (ccBGSSSE001\_Fish\_MQ5) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | Swims-In-Deep-Water has given me another fishing challenge. I should read the list he gave me to see what I will need to catch. |
| 20 |  | For my final challenge, the fish I am to catch are both rare and found in locations all over Skyrim. The fifth volume of Fishing Mastery has details on where, and how, to catch them. I should return them to Swims-In-Deep-Water once I've caught them all. |
| 21 |  | For my final challenge, the fish I am to catch are both rare and found in locations all over Skyrim. Angelfish can be found in temperate lakes, and can only be caught with an Alik'r fishing rod. The lyretail anthias can be caught in temperate streams with the Alik'r rod as well. Anglers are only caught in freezing waters using the Argonian fishing rod. Finally, scorpion fish are found underground. Like the angler, scorpion fish can only be caught by using the Argonian fishing rod. |
| 200 | ☑ | I've completed Swims-In-Deep-Water's final fishing challenge, designating me a legendary fisherman. He granted me the Fang of Haynekhtnamet, an exquisite Argonian dagger, as a reward. |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ5 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE001_Fish_MQ5`.

# Skyrim:Fit for a Jarl

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Model some clothes for [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie") |
| Location(s): | [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment") |
| Reward: | [Leveled gold](#A_Job_Well_Done) and [Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment_Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes") |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | =1 ([Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie"), if Unofficial Skyrim Patch since v2.1.3 are installed) |
| ID: | SolitudeFreeform02 |

Taarie has fashion advice and a job for you.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie").
2. Put on [Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment_Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes").
3. Introduce [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment") to [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair").
4. Return to Taarie.

### You're Going to Wear That ?

If you meet up with [Taarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Taarie "Skyrim:Taarie") in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), she will comment on your outfit: *"If you're heading to the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"), you might want to rethink that outfit."* You may ask her for some suggestions on what to wear to meet the jarl. Taarie's abrasive attitude toward you will change immediately. She will regard your meeting in the Blue Palace as an opportunity to introduce [Radiant Raiment](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment") to [Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"). Taarie offers to pay you to wear one of Radiant Raiment's outfits when you speak to the jarl. She'll let you keep the clothes as well.
You may be skeptical of Taarie's sudden wellspring of good will; maybe she wants to make you look silly in front of the jarl. Taarie assures you that you cannot possibly look any sillier than you do right now, so go ahead and accept the offer.

### Does This Make My Rear-End Look Big?

The [Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant_Raiment_Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Radiant Raiment Fine Clothes") are added to your inventory with instructions from Taarie: *"Try to get Elisif's opinion on it and if she likes it mention it's from Radiant Raiment."* Equip the clothes and go speak with Elisif. Depending on your business at the Blue Palace, the conversation starter about your apparel can seem awkward. Yet, Elisif has an eye for fashion, even in the midst of turmoil. You may ask for her opinion on your outfit and she will tell you, *"It's quite fetching actually. The craftsmanship is excellent."* Tell her it was made by Radiant Raiment. She will be glad to put in a request for a few dresses quite soon.

### A Job Well Done

Return to Taarie and tell her that Elisif loved the outfit and that she'll be placing an order soon. Taarie will be quite happy with the result: *"That's wonderful. You've done us a great service."* You can keep the outfit as she promised and she will also give you some gold for your trouble.

| Levels | Reward |
| --- | --- |
| 1–9 | 250 |
| 10–19 | 400 |
| 20–29 | 500 |
| 30–39 | 600 |
| 40+ | 750 |

## Bugs

- After you finish the quest, Taarie's disposition will not get raised as expected.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.3, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=19403))
- It is possible to steal the outfit prior to actually receiving the quest, which would then leave the outfit permanently flagged as stolen even though you're supposed to be given the outfit freely.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Fit for a Jarl (SolitudeFreeform02) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Speak to Elisif with Taarie's outfit on. |
| 20 |  | *Objective 20:* Tell Taarie what Elisif said about the outfit. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 30, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage SolitudeFreeform02 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest SolitudeFreeform02`.

# Skyrim:Fjori

## Overview

| Fjori (RefID: 0003D726) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Fjori "Lore:Fjori")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Ansilvund Burial Chambers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Burial_Chambers "Skyrim:Ansilvund Burial Chambers") | | |

Ghost of Fjori

|  |
| --- |
| **This article could benefit from an image**. See [Help:Images](/wiki/Help:Images "Help:Images") for information on how to upload images. Please remove this template from the page when finished. |

| Fjori (RefID: 000a222a) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Fjori "Lore:Fjori")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Ansilvund Burial Chambers](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_Burial_Chambers "Skyrim:Ansilvund Burial Chambers") | | |
| Species | [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") | [Soul](/wiki/Skyrim:Souls "Skyrim:Souls") | Radiant |
| Level | 1-30 | Type | [Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Undead "Skyrim:Undead") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000a222a | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000a222b |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 50-1000 | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 0-10 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 80-575 | | |
| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Creature Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Creature_Faction "Skyrim:Creature Faction"); [DunAnsilvundSpecialDraugrFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:DunAnsilvundSpecialDraugrFaction "Skyrim:DunAnsilvundSpecialDraugrFaction") | | |

**Fjori** was a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") huntress. When she was 29 years old, she fell in love with the warlord [Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Holgeir "Skyrim:Holgeir") on the field of battle, where they fought until her sword broke his axe and his shield dulled her blade. With Fjori and Holgeir united, there came a time of peace for the clans of the forest. When Holgeir was bitten by a poisonous snake, Fjori journeyed to obtain a cure from the [Akavir](/w/index.php?title=Skyrim:Akavir&action=edit&redlink=1 "Skyrim:Akavir (page does not exist)") which instantly cured him. However, then Fjori too was bitten by a snake, she died immediately due to exhaustion from her journey. Holgeir had a [great tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund") built, and after its completion, he took his own life, hoping to rejoin her in [Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:Sovngarde_(place) "Skyrim:Sovngarde (place)").

During the quest [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)"), a conjurer named [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven"), distraught over the loss of her husband Saeel Al-Skaven, is raising an army of [Draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") which includes both Fjori (as a Draugr) and Holgeir (as a Draugr or Dragon Priest) in its ranks.

## Related Quests

- **[Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund_(quest) "Skyrim:Ansilvund (quest)")**: Kill [Lu'ah Al-Skaven](/wiki/Skyrim:Lu%27ah_Al-Skaven "Skyrim:Lu'ah Al-Skaven") in [Ansilvund](/wiki/Skyrim:Ansilvund "Skyrim:Ansilvund").

## Quest-Related Events

When the curse is finally broken, the ghosts of the two lovers will emerge behind the altar:

:   **Fjori**: *"Thank you for releasing us from her spell."*
:   **Holgeir**: *"Now we can rest in peace once again. Come Fjori, my love..."*
:   **Fjori**: *"Take this with our gratitude."*

Fjotra

**Fjotra** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") who is initially found in [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt"). She has been kidnapped by a group of [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") and imprisoned in their redoubt. She is the daughter of [Enmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Enmon "Skyrim:Enmon") and [Mena](/wiki/Skyrim:Mena "Skyrim:Mena") from [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten").

She is the new sybil of Dibella, and you will be tasked with bringing her back to the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").

Fjotra wears red colored [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") and a pair of [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing").

## Related Quests

- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new Sybil for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

### The Heart of Dibella

When first spoken to:

:   *"Are you one of them? Please don't hurt me."*
:   **I'm here to bring you to the Temple in Markarth.**
:   *"Then it is true what they said? I am touched by the gods?"*
:   **You're going to be the Sybil of Dibella.**
:   *"I've heard stories about the wonders of the great Temple in Markarth. But I never dreamed that I would even get to see it. I am honored to be called for this duty. Please, lead on."*

When spoken to while she's following you:

:   *"Please, let's hurry to the Temple before the Forsworn find me again."*
:   *"I can't wait to learn from the priestesses."*
:   *"I hope we reach Markarth soon."*

## Conversations

If Enmon is with you and you go to Karthwasten with Fjotra, this conversation will occur:

:   **Fjotra**: *"Father!"*
:   **Enmon**: *"Fjotra, dear. Did they hurt you?"*
:   **Fjotra**: *"Of course not. My spirit remains strong."*
:   **Enmon**: *"My little girl. Always strong. Do you know where you have to go?"*
:   **Fjotra**: *"I'm to go to the temple in Markarth. I... I'll have to leave you and mother."*
:   **Enmon**: *"It's our honor to have you there. This man is going to take you to Markarth. Are you ready?"*
:   **Fjotra**: *"Of course."*

## Notes

- Although both her mother and father are [Bretons](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton"), Fjotra is a Nord, suggesting that she was adopted. According to the [Prima Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide") she is a Reachwoman.[[1]](#cite_note-TESVSPOGG-1):332
- Fjotra is the only child [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") in the game. As a child, she is invulnerable to attacks, making her useful as bait in a fight.

## Bugs

- When brought to [Harmugstahl](/wiki/Skyrim:Harmugstahl "Skyrim:Harmugstahl"), she may be attacked by the [Adventurer](/wiki/Skyrim:Adventurer#Adventurer1 "Skyrim:Adventurer") you meet at the entrance. **?**

# Skyrim:Fletcher (place)

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
