Unknown Book, Vol. I

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Find an Ancient Falmer Tome.
2. Bring it to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").

## Detailed Walkthrough

After finding an Ancient Falmer Tome, take it to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") in [The Arcanaeum](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcanaeum "Skyrim:The Arcanaeum") at the [College of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)"). He will purchase the book from you for 1000 gold, and give you a translated copy.

| Unknown Books | Translated Copies |
| --- | --- |
| [Unknown Book, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. I")  [Unknown Book, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. II")  [Unknown Book, Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. III")  [Unknown Book, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. IV") | [The Betrayed](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Betrayed "Skyrim:The Betrayed")  [Journal of Mirtil Angoth](/wiki/Skyrim:Journal_of_Mirtil_Angoth "Skyrim:Journal of Mirtil Angoth")  [Diary of Faire Agarwen](/wiki/Skyrim:Diary_of_Faire_Agarwen "Skyrim:Diary of Faire Agarwen")  [Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky_(book) "Skyrim:Touching the Sky (book)") |

### Unknown Book, Vol. I

Between the Wayshrine of Learning and the Wayshrine of Sight. If you are approaching the book from the Wayshrine of Sight, simply head southwest until you come across a path in the middle of a ridge. At the top there will be several [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). Head down the other side. Among the ruins to the right there will be a skeleton clutching a chest. The book is next to the chest. If you are approaching from the Wayshrine of Learning, go to your right along the frozen lake and you will see the ruins.

### Unknown Book, Vol. II

Most easily accessed with the [Emerald Paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon"), which is located on the body of a [Frost Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Giant "Skyrim:Frost Giant") in the [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") village. Once you have the Emerald Paragon, travel to the [Paragon Platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") (detailed directions to the platform are on its page) and place the Emerald Paragon in the Paragon Socket. A portal will open to the [Forgotten Vale Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Overlook "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Overlook"). Turn to your right (north) and make your way down the rocky river. The book is a short way down, just after the two broken pillars. It is next to the chest on the right-hand edge of the waterfall, by another broken pillar. You can also jump from the Inner Sanctum Balcony to the south and make your way along the cliffs. Make sure you have at least 450 health, or use [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal"), to survive the jump.

### Unknown Book, Vol. III

South, near the [Glacial Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Crevice "Skyrim:Glacial Crevice"). Travel upriver, toward the entrance of Glacial Crevice, but do not enter. At the fence entrance, turn around to face North. You will see two rock pathways. One on the right, that leads up along the mountain side and one on the left that goes over the river. Take the rock bridge pathway on the left that crosses the river and continue to cross over one more rock bridge. You will reach a fork, to the left is a Falmer bridge (made of [chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Chitin "Skyrim:Chaurus Chitin")) and to the right is a rocky pathway leading up into the mountains. Take the Falmer bridge to the left. Upon crossing the Falmer bridge, turn right to cross another rock bridge going down towards an Eastern lone Falmer tent. The book will be inside on a table.

### Unknown Book, Vol. IV

This book is on the table in the last hut before entering the tunnel leading to the Shrine of Radiance (the last Shrine after exiting the Glacial Crevice). There's a fire brazier outside the entrance to the tunnel and the hut is elevated directly above it.

### Gallery

- 

  Unknown Book, Vol. I
- 

  Unknown Book, Vol. II
- 

  Unknown Book, Vol. III
- 

  Unknown Book, Vol. IV

## Notes

- [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") will give 1,000 gold per Ancient Falmer Tome (Unknown Book), for a total of 4,000 gold. He takes them all if all four tomes are in your inventory, and it will appear that he only gave you 1,000 gold; however, he indeed gives 4,000 gold. This can be verified by checking your total gold before and after giving him the Falmer Tomes.
- This quest will remain in your available quest list until all four tomes have been given to Urag gro-Shub.
- Urag will not enter a conversation during the quest "[The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus")", and the tomes cannot be sold until after the quest is completed.

## Quest Stages

| Forgotten Vale Books Quest (DLC1VQFVBooks) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring Ancient Falmer Tome to Urag-gro Shub *[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]* |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 10, 30, 200.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC1VQFVBooks stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC1VQFVBooks`.

# Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Cave: Forgotten Vale Cave | | |
| Added by | [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 18 |
| Occupants | |
| [Chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Chaurus Hunters](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter"), [Shellbug](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC1zFalmerValley03 | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") | |

Forgotten Vale Cave

**Forgotten Vale Cave** is a small cave in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") containing [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") and one of the rare [shellbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug"). It contains only one zone, *[Forgotten Vale Cave](#Forgotten_Vale_Cave)*.

### Exterior

The exterior of this cave is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). The entrance is in the first section of the vale along the east wall of the valley, and is guarded by a [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"). A [gleamblossom](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleamblossom "Skyrim:Gleamblossom") plant is to the left of the entrance.

### Forgotten Vale Cave

Main chamber

The entrance leads into a passage with [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling. A gated pen to the north contains a [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), a [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter"), two unoccupied [chaurus cocoons](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon"), seven chaurus egg sacs, and five [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom") on the walls. The path splits to the west, with the left side rising along a ledge to a rope release that opens a concealed door in the northwest wall of the main chamber, and the right side descending past a Falmer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the floor of the chamber. The chamber features six [Falmer hives](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive") and five cocoons, but only one of each is occupied by a chaurus hunter.

The passage behind the concealed door on the northwest ledge of the chamber descends into another chamber containing another rope release that operates the door, a few glowing mushrooms, an unoccupied cocoon, and one of the rare [shellbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug"). In order to obtain their [chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug_Chitin "Skyrim:Shellbug Chitin"), these creatures must be [mined](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") with a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"); the material cannot be obtained through killing the creatures by conventional means. Shellbugs are also not detected by the [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") spell.

## Bugs

- You may be unable to mine the shellbug after it respawns. Leaving and reentering the cave will enable the shellbug, allowing you to mine it normally.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.0, fixes this bug.

## Maps

Forgotten Vale Cave

  The shellbug

  Mined and dead

## Overview

Forgotten Vale Forest

**Forgotten Vale Forest** is a small grove in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), which can only be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [ruby paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Paragon "Skyrim:Ruby Paragon"). It is the location of [Auriel's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Auriel's Shield").

### Exterior

The exterior to this grove is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). It can only be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [ruby paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Paragon "Skyrim:Ruby Paragon").

### Forgotten Vale Forest

The paragon portal teleports you to a small forested valley far north of the main areas of the vale. The broken stone arch forming the portal allows you to return directly to the paragon platform. There doesn't seem to be a proper path through the trees, and due to the density of the snow and trees it can be difficult to see any [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll") as you approach; the [Detect Life](/wiki/Skyrim:Detect_Life_(spell) "Skyrim:Detect Life (spell)") spell or the [Aura Whisper](/wiki/Skyrim:Aura_Whisper "Skyrim:Aura Whisper") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") may therefore be useful. There are up to six frost trolls in the area. Eventually you will encounter a [Falmer Warmonger](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Warmonger "Skyrim:Falmer Warmonger"), either battling some of the trolls or having defeated them, wandering near an unlocked stone [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). The Falmer carries the unique [Auriel's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Auriel's Shield"), and will attack as soon you are spotted. The chest is on a rise near the southwest wall by the remains of another arch, with a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") lying on the ground in front. North of the chest is an overhanging section of the valley wall, where you may find one or two frost trolls. The only other items of note in the forest are three [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bushes and some broken masonry.

Forgotten Vale Overlook

**Forgotten Vale Overlook** is a small river valley in the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"), which can be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [emerald paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon"). It is the location of *[Unknown Book, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. II")*.

### Exterior

The exterior to this river valley is the [Forgotten Vale](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale"). It can be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [emerald paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon"), or by using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") when standing on one of the icebergs outside [Temple Balcony](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale)#Auriel.27s_Chapel "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)").

### Forgotten Vale Overlook

The paragon portal teleports you to the eastern bank of a turbulent river in the isolated river valley above the waterfall at the southern end of the frozen lake. The broken stone arch forming the portal allows you to return directly to the paragon platform. There are no enemies here. The river is fairly wide, with rapids among the many rocks in the water, and both of the riverbanks are cluttered with broken masonry and fallen trees. Head downstream by proceeding north along the eastern bank. Just to the right of where the waterfall cascades into the lake below is a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") lying next to an unlocked stone [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with an enchanted [elven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Elven Greatsword"), a quiver of [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"), a random enchanted [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), and *[Unknown Book, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. II")* on the ground in front of the chest. Looking up towards the northwest, you'll see the balcony of the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)") on the cliffs above.

Forgotten Vale

The **Forgotten Vale** is an isolated region in northwestern Skyrim once inhabited by the [Snow Elves](/wiki/Lore:Snow_Elf "Lore:Snow Elf") worshipping the god [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El"). It is initially only accessible after traversing both [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave") and [Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage"), and allows access (via standard entrances and the [paragon platform](#Paragon_Platform)) to eight distinct locations: [Darkfall Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Grotto "Skyrim:Darkfall Grotto"), Darkfall Passage, [Forgotten Vale Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Cave "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Cave"), [Forgotten Vale Forest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Forest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Forest"), [Forgotten Vale Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Overlook "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Overlook"), the [Glacial Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Crevice "Skyrim:Glacial Crevice"), the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)"), and [Sharpslope Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharpslope_Cave "Skyrim:Sharpslope Cave").

The vale is now inhabited by the brutish, corrupted [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") and a variety of indigenous creatures: [frost giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Giant "Skyrim:Frost Giant"), [frost trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Troll "Skyrim:Frost Troll"), [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [ice wraiths](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wraith "Skyrim:Ice Wraith"), [Vale sabre cats](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Sabre_Cat "Skyrim:Vale Sabre Cat"), and [Vale deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Deer "Skyrim:Vale Deer"). You will visit it during the *[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard")* add-on's main questline, either as a [Vampire Lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Lord "Skyrim:Vampire Lord") or as a member of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). The [temple](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Chapel "Skyrim:Auriel's Chapel") built by the Snow Elves in honor of Auri-El (displayed as "Temple Balcony" at the wayshrine portals once the final wayshrine is raised at the end of the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")) is accessed through the Inner Sanctum. In the middle of a frozen lake near the Inner Sanctum is a [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaching part of the [Drain Vitality](/wiki/Skyrim:Drain_Vitality "Skyrim:Drain Vitality") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), which is guarded by the twin [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") [Naaslaarum](/wiki/Skyrim:Naaslaarum "Skyrim:Naaslaarum") and [Voslaarum](/wiki/Skyrim:Voslaarum "Skyrim:Voslaarum") after completion of the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising").

## Related Quests

- **[Forgotten Vale Books Quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Books_Quest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Books Quest")**: Bring the Ancient Falmer Tome to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub").
- **[Touching the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Touching_the_Sky "Skyrim:Touching the Sky")**: Find and retrieve [Auriel's Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Bow "Skyrim:Auriel's Bow").

## Locations

- **[Darkfall Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Grotto "Skyrim:Darkfall Grotto")** — A small cave in the Forgotten Vale.
- **[Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage")** — A small cave only accessible through [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave") serving as the only access to the Forgotten Vale.
- **[Forgotten Vale Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Cave "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Cave")** — A small cave in the Forgotten Vale containing [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus") and one of the rare [shellbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug").
- **[Forgotten Vale Forest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Forest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Forest")** — A small grove in the Forgotten Vale, which can only be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [ruby paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Paragon "Skyrim:Ruby Paragon").
- **[Forgotten Vale Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Overlook "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Overlook")** — A small river valley in the Forgotten Vale, which can be accessed by using the [paragon platform](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale#Paragon_Platform "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale") with the [emerald paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon").
- **[Glacial Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Crevice "Skyrim:Glacial Crevice")** — A small cave in the Forgotten Vale, which must be traversed to reach the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)").
- **[Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)")** — A relatively well-preserved portion of the Chantry of [Auri-El](/wiki/Lore:Auri-El "Lore:Auri-El") in the Forgotten Vale.
- **[Sharpslope Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharpslope_Cave "Skyrim:Sharpslope Cave")** — A small cave in the Forgotten Vale containing [chaurus](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus "Skyrim:Chaurus"), [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer"), and one of the rare [shellbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug").

### Wayshrine of Sight

Auriel's Chapel balcony

From [Darkfall Passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Passage "Skyrim:Darkfall Passage"), you are transported via the portal in the Wayshrine of Illumination to a cave area with a path winding away and up to the surface. There are six [gleamblossom](/wiki/Skyrim:Gleamblossom "Skyrim:Gleamblossom") plants in the cave area. You emerge high in the mountains overlooking the vale. There are many gleamblossom plants found throughout the first area of the vale and many [torchbugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug "Skyrim:Torchbug") flying around at night. Off to the west, up an incline you will encounter a frost troll in its lair, which contains the bodies of a dead Vale deer and Vale sabre cat. To the right is a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein"). Two more silver ore veins can be found above the first, to the northwest; they can be reached by heading to the right of the troll's lair. A fourth vein can be found by heading north from the lair. It is on the ground to the northwest of a pointed stone arch.

Heading north from where you exit the cave area, another rock overhang is being used as a lair by a Vale sabre cat. Just to the north is a silver ore vein and farther north is a Falmer guarding the entrance to [Forgotten Vale Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Cave "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Cave"). Northwest from the entrance you will encounter [Prelate Athring](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Athring "Skyrim:Prelate Athring") in front of the Wayshrine of Sight. Speaking with him will cause him to raise the wayshrine containing the second basin you need to draw water from. The wayshrine will also contain portals to each of the wayshrines you have visited and caused the prelates to raise. North of the shrine is a [gold ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein"). From the vein, head south past the shrine to find another silver ore vein near several gleamblossom plants to the right of a hill. West from that vein is another gold ore vein against a rock face. Follow the rock wall south until you reach the main path, then proceed west under a stone arch. As the path starts to climb, ahead are three frostbite spiders. Once they are dealt with, backtrack slightly to just before a broken pillar on the left of the path, and climb to the south to find another gold ore vein, the last in this part of the vale.

Just past the three spiders, hanging from an rock overhang by some webbing is a [dessicated corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Dessicated_Corpse "Skyrim:Dessicated Corpse") that can be shot down with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") or ranged magic. There are [egg sacs](/wiki/Skyrim:Egg_Sac "Skyrim:Egg Sac") on either side of you as you enter the pass, and a [giant frostbite spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Giant Frostbite Spider") will descend from above and attack. On your right is a gold ore vein. The pass descends into the next valley, where you can see a large waterfall to the west and a wide river ahead. There are no more gleamblossom plants in the rest of the vale.

As you descend, you will see a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") on the right lying across a stone [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). On the ground beside the chest is a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a book titled *[Unknown Book, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._I "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. I")*. As soon as you pick up this book, a [miscellaneous quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Books_Quest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Books Quest") is added directing you to bring this tome to [Urag gro-Shub](/wiki/Skyrim:Urag_gro-Shub "Skyrim:Urag gro-Shub") at the [College in Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)").

### Wayshrine of Learning

There is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") bush by the riverbank, and a [quicksilver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore Vein") on the ground to the southeast. Following the riverbank south, you will soon reach [Prelate Celegriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Celegriath "Skyrim:Prelate Celegriath") by the Wayshrine of Learning. Speaking with him will cause him to raise the wayshrine containing the third basin you need to draw water from.

Dropping down to the riverbank and following it to the far southern end, you'll see a waterfall disappearing underground. You can use this to enter [Darkfall Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Grotto "Skyrim:Darkfall Grotto"); however, using the [amethyst paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Paragon "Skyrim:Amethyst Paragon") at the [paragon platform](#Paragon_Platform) to enter the grotto will allow you to collect all of the grotto's treasure.

West of the waterfall is a slope with a [malachite ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Malachite_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Malachite Ore Vein") partway up. Staying on the west side of the river and following it back north, you will pass some broken stone pillars.

A short distance before the next waterfall is an ice wraith guarding an apprentice-locked stone chest, with skeletal remains, a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), and a random [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Generic_Magic_Weapons "Skyrim:Generic Magic Weapons") [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") beside it. Just north of the waterfall is a malachite ore vein. Continuing along the riverbank and just before reaching the bottom of the next waterfall, a gap in the ice contains an ice wraith guarding a novice-locked chest, with a lootable skeleton and a satchel beside it. The satchel contains two random potions, including one of [waterbreathing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Waterbreathing "Skyrim:Potion of Waterbreathing"), and other loot. There is another malachite ore vein just north of the waterfall, and one more vein on the rock face west of a tall snow-clogged tree on the next landmass to the northwest. After the next waterfall is a snowberry bush.

Crossing back to the eastern riverbank and heading south a few paces to another snowberry bush, another malachite ore vein is to the northeast. Continue southeast for a hundred paces or so for one last malachite ore vein, before returning north. Continuing north along the bank, a frost giant is carrying the amethyst paragon. There are two more snowberry bushes nearby. The river at this end is partially frozen, enabling you to cross to the west side of the large waterfall, where you will find another malachite ore vein on the wall with a small piece of ice for you to stand on while mining.

A few paces back to the south on the western riverbank is a path heading north up a series of stairs. Partway up the stairs, once you are level with the top of the large waterfall, head northeast. On the near shore by the wide rapids, to the left is a pair of broken pillars that are part of a stone arch, with a pedestal holding a paragon socket at the base of the right pillar. This is all that remains of the paragon platform. With the corresponding paragon, the platform gives you access to several otherwise inaccessible areas in the Forgotten Vale as [listed below](#Paragon_Platform). On the eastern bank under an icy overhang is another frost giant, this one carrying the [sapphire paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Paragon "Skyrim:Sapphire Paragon"). A malachite ore vein and a snowberry bush are to the right of its lair.

### Wayshrine of Resolution

Wayshrine of Resolution

Word wall

Returning southwest to the path and stairs, follow them to the top and across into the next valley. The path turns north, following the riverbank, where a natural stone bridge crosses over to the western side. On the far side, to the south is the Wayshrine of Resolution, with [Prelate Nirilor](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Nirilor "Skyrim:Prelate Nirilor") standing beside it. Speaking with him will cause him to raise the wayshrine containing the fourth basin you need to draw water from. Beside the wayshrine is a snowberry bush. From here, you can either head southwest toward the frozen lake, or return to the bridge and head north.

Heading southwest leads to a stone arch, with stairs rising from the lake toward the wayshrine. Under the arch is a lootable skeleton, with two random [potions of resist fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire") beside it. Heading southwest from the arch and following the western edge of the lake will lead you to a total of three [moonstone ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore Vein"). The last vein is just past a small copse of trees and some broken masonry near the lake. From this vein, if you head due east toward the word wall and have completed Dragon Rising, two named dragons, Naaslaarum and Voslaarum, will burst from beneath the ice of the lake and simultaneously attack you. During the battle, they may dive back through the ice before smashing more holes in the ice when they emerge again. Stairs lead up to the word wall, which teaches a word for the Drain Vitality shout. To the right of the word wall is an unlocked stone chest, and beside the chest is a lootable skeleton, a leveled [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and two random potions of resist fire.

There are also three chests under the ice in the lake, with their locations noted on the [map](#Map) below. Any character that isn't an [Argonian](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") will require potions of waterbreathing or preferably a corresponding [enchanted](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(effect) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (effect)") item or [spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Waterbreathing_(spell) "Skyrim:Waterbreathing (spell)") to recover the loot from these chests. A [light](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlelight "Skyrim:Candlelight") staff or spell would also be desirable if you don't have [night vision](/wiki/Skyrim:Night_Eye_(effect) "Skyrim:Night Eye (effect)"). [Vampire's Sight](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Sight "Skyrim:Vampire's Sight") is ideal, as you can recast it as often as you like, even underwater, unlike spells. The first submerged chest is below the large waterfall at the south end of the lake. Proceeding south along the western side of the lake, you will reach a large section of fallen masonry in front of a snowbank. An ice wraith will emerge from the snow and attack as you approach. A moonstone ore vein is against the rock face behind the snowbank. A second vein is at the top of a slope a short distance east of the waterfall, nearly level with the bottom level of the waterfall. To find the first submerged chest, enter the water directly beneath the waterfall and dive down to the chest near some sunken masonry, then return to the surface. Next, head north-northeast from the waterfall until you reach a hole made by the dragons. Dive here and face south, and you should see two broken pillars very close to the hole. Between the pillars is the second chest atop skeletal remains. Back on the surface, head southeast from the hole toward a stone arch. Nearby on the frozen lake are two sets of skeletal remains with an [elven sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Sword "Skyrim:Elven Sword") and two random potions of resist fire.

Heading north along the eastern side of the lake, you will pass another moonstone ore vein near where the rocks end. From there, return to the word wall and dive into one of the holes made by the dragons to the west to find the third submerged chest near two broken pillars. Still underwater, a short distance to the southeast are two satchels among a large collection of skeletal remains. Back on the surface, return to the bridge north of the Wayshrine of Resolution and cross back to the north. Once across, the path descends, following the riverbank northwest. You'll eventually reach a small deserted Falmer settlement consisting of two Falmer tents with a campfire between them. The first tent contains a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") on the ground and a [Vale deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Vale Deer Hide") in a large leather pouch. The second tent has a chitin table holding two random potions of healing, a [pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl"), a [small pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl"), a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), and a [fox pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Fox_Pelt "Skyrim:Fox Pelt"). Beside the table is another large leather pouch holding a [Falmer war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_War_Axe "Skyrim:Falmer War Axe").

Continuing along the river heading southwest, you will reach a group of five [chaurus cocoons](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Cocoon "Skyrim:Chaurus Cocoon"), two of which are occupied, with two [orichalcum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore Vein") among them. A short distance farther is the lower entrance to [Sharpslope Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Sharpslope_Cave "Skyrim:Sharpslope Cave"). A second, upper entrance to the cave places you closer to the rare [shellbug](/wiki/Skyrim:Shellbug "Skyrim:Shellbug") inside; see the next paragraph for details. There are three more occupied chaurus cocoons and four more orichalcum ore veins along the river, with the first vein immediately south of the lower entrance, and the last vein in the corner on the opposite bank.

Returning to the small deserted Falmer settlement, just to the northeast is an unlocked gate across a path that zigzags up the side of the mountain. After a couple of switchbacks, a natural stone bridge crosses south over the river. Before crossing the bridge, at the top of the path to the north is a Falmer tent guarded by a Falmer magic-user. The tent contains a Falmer chest and another leather pouch holding a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd") and a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"). The bridge is guarded by a Falmer, with any fighting likely to alert several more Falmer to your presence. Across the bridge, the path continues to follow the riverbank far below. As it reaches another bridge, this one made by the Falmer, on the left are two leather pouches, one holding a quiver of [Falmer arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Arrow "Skyrim:Falmer Arrow") and a [Falmer sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Falmer Sword"), and the other holding two [rock warbler eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg"). Across the bridge is a Falmer archer standing on a ledge overlooking the river below. The path ascends west over a large natural stone arch, which is marked by two strange posts on the far side. The path continues to the west, with the upper entrance to Sharpslope Cave marked by a tattered banner fluttering overhead.

The path continues past the entrance to an area beneath the natural stone arch, where three leather pouches are on a flat rock next to a gold ore vein. The leather pouches contain four pieces of [gold ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore "Skyrim:Gold Ore"), three rock warbler eggs, and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"). The path continues to the south, leading to another Falmer-built bridge which crosses to the east. On the far side is a Falmer tent containing a table holding two random potions of healing and a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), as well as a leather pouch holding five [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"). As the path rises to the east, on the far side of the stone spire ahead is a Falmer chest. The path keeps rising and turns southeast, passing a gate near another Falmer. The area beyond the gate contains a frost giant carrying the [emerald paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon") along with two dead Falmer, a dead chaurus, and a dead [chaurus hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Hunter "Skyrim:Chaurus Hunter"), all of which are leveled and appear to have been killed fighting the giant. Scattered on the ground nearby are several Falmer [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons") and [shields](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Shield "Skyrim:Falmer Shield") along with many bones, suggesting the battle has continued for some time.

The path continues to circle the tall stone spire past a Falmer chest on a ledge to a Falmer-built platform. It is possible to climb to the top of the spire for a magnificent view and a snowberry bush, with a partially buried skeleton among the branches holding a [gold sapphire ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Sapphire_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Sapphire Ring"). From the platform, a collapsed Falmer bridge originally led north, while an intact Falmer bridge crosses to the southwest. This leads to another platform with a leather pouch holding a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") and four samples of [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers"). Another natural stone arch crosses to the west to a Falmer tent guarded by a leveled Falmer. A second Falmer patrols the next Falmer bridge to the south. Two leather pouches on the right after crossing the natural stone arch contain two racks of [dog meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog_Meat "Skyrim:Dog Meat"), a joint of raw [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat"), and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"). The tent is larger and more ornate than most Falmer dwellings, and contains a chest with quality loot and a leather pouch to the right holding a joint of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") and a set of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"). A large rock behind the tent holds a [goat hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide"), a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), a set of [large antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Antlers "Skyrim:Large Antlers"), a [Falmer bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Bow "Skyrim:Falmer Bow"), and a leather pouch holding a piece of [moonstone ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") and a piece of [chaurus chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Chitin "Skyrim:Chaurus Chitin"). Against the south side of the tent is another leather pouch holding a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull").

The next Falmer bridge heads south to a pair of tents facing each other on a slanted platform. The western tent contains a Vale deer hide, a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"), two haunches of raw venison, and a Falmer war axe on a wooden chopping block. The eastern tent contains two leather pouches; one holds two racks of dog meat, and the other holds a sample of hawk feathers, two pearls, and three small pearls. A large rock behind the eastern tent holds an altar of sorts made from a goat hide that can't be interacted with laid flat on a leather pouch. On top of the hide are two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), a [ruby](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby"), and a troll skull.

The path heads southwest to the next ledge and east across another Falmer bridge to a larger area, with a haunch of raw venison in a leather pouch on your right as you leave the bridge. Ahead is a large rock with a Falmer sword and a [skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Skull "Skyrim:Skull") on top and a leather pouch to the right holding a piece of chaurus chitin. A Falmer tent is up a ramp to the north, with deer skulls and antlers stuck to posts flanking the entrance. The tent contains a Falmer chest, with leather pouches holding six loose Falmer arrows and a random empty soul gem on either side. Under the tent is a gated storage area containing two haunches of raw venison, a set of large antlers, three cabbages, and a gourd. Returning south, a ramp descends to another ledge guarded by a leveled Falmer. On the south side of the ledge are two more leather pouches holding a piece of chaurus chitin, two chaurus eggs, and a goat hide. From the ledge, a natural stone bridge heads southwest, and a Falmer-built bridge heads west.

The path across the Falmer bridge leads down to a Falmer tent, with a mammoth skull attached above the entrance. The tent contains a table holding *[Unknown Book, Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._III "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. III")*, two random potions of healing, and three pearls, as well as a leather pouch holding a Vale deer hide. Head across the stone bridge to the southwest and then back across another nautral stone bridge heading southeast to an upper section of the river, with a stone ramp descending to the north. At the bottom, on the opposite bank are three chaurus cocoons, but only one is occupied. Two final orichalcum ore veins are also along the river nearby. Returning up the ramp to the upper section of the river above the waterfall, to the east is a path up to a small pass leading to three moonstone ore veins: two are on the ground, and one is on the side of the rock face to the south. Return again to the upper section of the river and head south to where some Falmer fencing is stretched in front of the headwater. Beyond the fence, two leveled Falmer guard the entrance to the [Glacial Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Crevice "Skyrim:Glacial Crevice").

### Falmer Fissure

Falmer Fissure

Once you have passed through the Glacial Crevice, you will emerge again outside in the isolated southwest area of the Forgotten Vale. There are two paths. The first path continues ahead under a walkway that links two raised Falmer tents and continues to more Falmer settlements. The second path, to your immediate left, heads north, with a string of [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") stretched across the path. Beyond the chimes, two Falmer patrol in front of a gate that blocks an area containing a frost giant. There is a Falmer chest to the right of the gate, and a dead Falmer lying on a large rock just beyond them. Farther northwest are two more dead Falmer, the occasional weapon, and many scattered bones including mammoth skulls and rib cages. The frost giant's lair is under a rock overhang, and contains the bodies of two chaurus, a chaurus hunter, and another Falmer, along with a Falmer bow and a Falmer sword. The frost giant carries the [diamond paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond_Paragon "Skyrim:Diamond Paragon"), which enables you to use the paragon platform to teleport to a unique area in the Glacial Crevice. There is a quicksilver ore vein at either end of the lair, and two more to the south, with one near the top of a rise, and the other a short distance beyond.

Returning to the exit from the Glacial Crevice, the two raised Falmer tents are accessed by a curved ramp. In the first tent is a central campfire with a Falmer sword and a rack of dog meat on either side, and a second Falmer sword, a Vale deer hide, a deer pelt, a piece of chaurus chitin, a haunch of raw venison, and a gourd either on benches or in a leather pouch against the wall. A short walkway crosses to the second tent, which contains a Falmer chest and a leather pouch holding a pine thrush egg, a rock warbler egg, and two pieces of [honeycomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Honeycomb "Skyrim:Honeycomb"). Under the second tent is a string of bone chimes.

Following the path east at ground level, another tent on the left contains two legs of goat, three gourds, and a set of large antlers among straw scattered on the floor. The next section of the path is trapped with a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") at either end, each triggering separate [claw traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Claw "Skyrim:Claw"), while above is a lookout point with a Falmer on guard. Past the second tripwire are two ramps. The ramp on the left leads back up to the lookout point and a raised tent, which has a central campfire and a troll skull on a bench. A second Falmer, a magic-user, is in the middle of the path at ground level beyond the start of the ramp on the right. Any fighting with either Falmer is likely to alert several more Falmer in the settlements beyond. On the north wall of the path near the second Falmer is a leather pouch behind some fencing holding a piece of [silver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore "Skyrim:Silver Ore") and two pieces of [quicksilver ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Quicksilver_Ore "Skyrim:Quicksilver Ore"), with another piece of quicksilver ore on the ground beside it. The ramp on the right has another tent built under it opposite the fenced leather pouch, containing another leather pouch holding a rack of dog meat and a leg of goat. The ramp ascends to the east, passing a smoky campfire to a set of elevated walkways that crisscross the settlement and link several tents on different levels. Take care, as there is another Falmer patrolling a walkway farther ahead, and a Falmer magic-user in the first tent on the left. Before reaching the junction for that tent, you will pass the top of another tent on a lower level. In the raised tent on the left are three samples of hawk feathers, a [hawk beak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Beak "Skyrim:Hawk Beak"), a [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), two bowls of [powdered mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Powdered_Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Powdered Mammoth Tusk"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a set of small antlers, and three loose chaurus eggs, all on a bench or in two leather pouches. There is also an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") built into a table, with two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") beside it.

The main walkway continues, passing a raised platform with an open wooden box filled with water containing three living [clams](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam "Skyrim:Clam") that can be harvested. The walkway then passes between the side of a tent and a tall rock, with a string of bone chimes hanging down, and continues past another junction with a branch to the left all the way to a rock wall at the back before turning left and continuing through a gap between two walls to another area. The walkway branching to the left passes another tent on the same level to the right, which contains a table holding a fox pelt, a random filled soul gem, two chaurus eggs, and two random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina (see [bugs](#Bugs)). Opposite the tent is a curved ramp leading up and around the tall rock to the tent beside the clams, which contains a Falmer chest and two [mammoth tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") in a leather pouch. As the walkway descends past the previous tent, it takes a couple of turns and passes more bone chimes, then passes the entrance to the empty tent you previously passed above. The next tent along the walkway contains an [ice wolf pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Ice_Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Ice Wolf Pelt") on the floor, two [Vale sabre cat hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Vale_Sabre_Cat_Hide "Skyrim:Vale Sabre Cat Hide") and two pieces of quicksilver ore on top of a straw bale, and an open crate holding a pickaxe, two more pieces of quicksilver ore, two [amethysts](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst "Skyrim:Amethyst"), and an [emerald](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald "Skyrim:Emerald"). The walkway finally descends to ground level, where two quicksilver ore veins, three loose pieces of quicksilver ore, and two pickaxes are found.

Passing through the gap between the rock walls to the next area leads to more raised tents, with the walkway continuing between them. The tent on the right contains two gourds and a leg of goat on the floor, while the tent on the left contains a table holding two chaurus eggs, two pieces of chaurus chitin, and a [honed Falmer sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Honed_Falmer_Sword "Skyrim:Honed Falmer Sword"). Past the second tent, two Falmer patrol the walkway, and three more tents are on the left. The first tent is below you, after a switchback in the path. Next to it is the second tent containing two legs of goat and two rock warbler eggs in a leather pouch. The third tent is off a junction and is tilted on its side, with a [beehive](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive "Skyrim:Beehive") hanging from the ceiling containing a [bee](/wiki/Skyrim:Bee "Skyrim:Bee"), a piece of honeycomb, and a [beehive husk](/wiki/Skyrim:Beehive_Husk "Skyrim:Beehive Husk"). The walkway continues past the three tents up to a tent that is larger and more ornate, which contains a Falmer chest, a bench, a table, and a leather pouch holding a sample of hawk feathers, a set of small antlers, a bird nest containing a rock warbler egg, two random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina, a random poison, *[Unknown Book, Vol. IV](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._IV "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. IV")*, a beehive husk, and a piece of honeycomb. Return along the walkway and take the switchback past the first of the previous three tents, which contains a bench with a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), a pearl, and a garnet. The walkway continues to descend past an alcove with three chaurus cocoons, two of which are occupied. The walkway finally skirts around a fire before reaching ground level. Nearby under the last tent is a storage area containing four pieces of chaurus chitin. The path leads east to a gate, with another fire to the left.

Beyond the gate, the path turns south to enter a wide tunnel and starts to rise. A lookout point and a quicksilver ore vein are on the left partway up, and several glowing mushrooms grow on the walls. The tunnel continues past an empty Falmer tent, turning west and continuing to rise even more steeply. The path passes between two Falmer-built ledges near an empty [Falmer hive](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer_Hive "Skyrim:Falmer Hive"), followed by another quicksilver ore vein on the left. Farther up the rise, on the left is a second Falmer-built ledge and another empty Falmer hive. The path then passes through a narrow gap with a tripwire across the front that triggers a large [rockfall](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") from farther up on a raised platform, with the platform just beyond an occupied Falmer hive opposite another quicksilver ore vein. At the top, a final quicksilver ore vein is on the left just before the path emerges from the tunnel and continues northwest.

### Wayshrine of Radiance

More Falmer tents are on several levels, and ahead is [Prelate Edhelbor](/wiki/Skyrim:Prelate_Edhelbor "Skyrim:Prelate Edhelbor") in front of the Wayshrine of Radiance. Speaking with him will cause him to raise the wayshrine containing the fifth and final basin you need to draw water from.

A ramp to the left of the wayshrine leads up to a Falmer tent, which contains three leather pouches holding two bowls of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a bowl of powdered mammoth tusk, a leg of goat, a gourd, and a mammoth tusk. The walkway continues up past another tent containing a goat hide, a piece of honeycomb, a troll skull, and a normal [deer hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Hide "Skyrim:Deer Hide"). The third tent contains two quivers of Falmer arrows and two pieces of chaurus chitin, with one of the quivers on the floor beside the leather pouches which hold the remaining items. The walkway now crosses to the right side of the wayshrine, passing the empty lower level of a two-level tent, with a ramp spiraling up to the upper level. The tent's upper level has open sides for use as lookout points. Inside are three leather pouches holding a haunch of raw horse meat, a [leek](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), and a haunch of raw venison. The walkway continues along a stone wall before spiraling up to yet another tent, which contains a table holding three random potions of healing and three random potions of magicka. To either side of the table are leather pouches holding two [orange dartwings](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), a [blue dartwing](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Dartwing "Skyrim:Blue Dartwing"), a [luna moth wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Luna_Moth_Wing "Skyrim:Luna Moth Wing"), two [blue butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), a sample of [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), four pearls, and two small pearls.

### Inner Sanctum

Returning to ground level, the path heads northeast toward a large stone arch and a stone bridge that crosses to the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)"). Before the bridge, another quicksilver ore vein is to the left, on the west rock wall. Under the bridge, to the right are three loose [elven arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Arrow "Skyrim:Elven Arrow"). Far below this point to the east is a ledge that can only be reached by careful rock climbing or by using the [Become Ethereal](/wiki/Skyrim:Become_Ethereal "Skyrim:Become Ethereal") shout and dropping from under the bridge. On the ledge is a gold ore vein with some skeletal remains, a pickaxe, a [gold ruby necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ruby_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Ruby Necklace"), a Falmer weapon, a bowl of powdered mammoth tusk, two pieces of gold ore, a [diamond](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond "Skyrim:Diamond"), two [flawless diamonds](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Diamond "Skyrim:Flawless Diamond"), and a bird nest containing a rock warbler egg. From here, you can reach several more ledges with harvestable bird nests. Once finished, you can either climb down or use become ethereal again and drop to the first Falmer settlement near the Glacial Crevice exit.

Cross the bridge. Ahead is a flight of stairs ascending to the chantry courtyard, but before proceeding, turn to your left, where a rock outcropping beyond a lone stone arch holds an [elven greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Elven_Greatsword "Skyrim:Elven Greatsword"), two [flawless rubies](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Ruby "Skyrim:Flawless Ruby"), and a [flawless sapphire](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Sapphire "Skyrim:Flawless Sapphire"). Return to the bridge and head up the stairs into the courtyard dominated by a statue of Auri-El. The huge double doors beyond the two curved stairs are locked until you complete the pilgrimage ritual. To do so, empty your [initiate's ewer](/wiki/Skyrim:Initiate%27s_Ewer "Skyrim:Initiate's Ewer") into the basin at the top of the stairs behind Auri-El's statue, filling it with the water collected from the five wayshrines. The doors will then unlock and grant you access to the Inner Sanctum.

### Paragon Platform

The paragon platform, also referred to as the paragon portal, will allow you to open portals to a few otherwise inaccessible locations in the Forgotten Vale.

To find the paragon platform, go to the Wayshrine of Learning and turn northwest. Follow along the river until you see a path heading north up a series of stairs on the shore opposite the frost giant carrying the amethyst paragon. Partway up the stairs, once you are level with the top of the large waterfall, leave the path and head northwest along the river. On the near shore to the left is the paragon platform, and on the opposite shore is a frost giant carrying the sapphire paragon.

The platform uses the five different paragons to open portals to unique areas in the Forgotten Vale. The paragons are all carried by frost giants, as noted on the map below.

The [amethyst paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amethyst_Paragon "Skyrim:Amethyst Paragon") opens a portal to an otherwise inaccessible ledge in [Darkfall Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Grotto "Skyrim:Darkfall Grotto").
The [diamond paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Diamond_Paragon "Skyrim:Diamond Paragon") opens a portal to an otherwise inaccessible ledge in the [Glacial Crevice](/wiki/Skyrim:Glacial_Crevice "Skyrim:Glacial Crevice").
The [emerald paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Paragon "Skyrim:Emerald Paragon") opens a portal to [Forgotten Vale Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Overlook "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Overlook").
The [ruby paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Paragon "Skyrim:Ruby Paragon") opens a portal to [Forgotten Vale Forest](/wiki/Skyrim:Forgotten_Vale_Forest "Skyrim:Forgotten Vale Forest").
The [sapphire paragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Sapphire_Paragon "Skyrim:Sapphire Paragon") opens a portal to an otherwise inaccessible room in the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)").

## Notes

- [Auriel's Shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Auriel%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Auriel's Shield") can be obtained in Forgotten Vale Forest, and *[Unknown Book, Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:Unknown_Book,_Vol._II "Skyrim:Unknown Book, Vol. II")* can be obtained in Forgotten Vale Overlook.
- Unlike the vale itself and all other connected locations, the [Inner Sanctum](/wiki/Skyrim:Inner_Sanctum_(Vale) "Skyrim:Inner Sanctum (Vale)") doesn't respawn.
- While you are in the vale during the quest Touching the Sky, you will be unable to fast travel back to Skyrim. In order to leave the vale, you must go to the wayshrine inside the Inner Sanctum and take the portal to Darkfall Cave. From there, an exit passage will lead you back up to the cave mouth that returns to Skyrim. Once you have left by this method, you should be able to fast travel to and from the vale.
- If [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") is active, you may only rest in the vale if you bring a [campsite](/wiki/Skyrim:Camping "Skyrim:Camping") with you.

## Bugs

- Despite the vale being an open world area, you cannot summon [Arvak](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvak "Skyrim:Arvak") here.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130.0, fixes this bug.
- The portals here may not play their visual effects and may turn purple when you open them.
  - The [Official Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim:Special Edition Patch"), version 1.6.1130.0, fixes this bug.
- The items in some tents may have fallen through the tables and/or the bottom of the tents themselves, making recovering them difficult.
  - Using an area effect spell either inside or outside the affected tent offers the most likely chance of recovery.
- [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad")'s damage bonus against elves has no effect on the [Snow Elves](/wiki/Skyrim:Snow_Elf "Skyrim:Snow Elf") or [Frozen Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Frozen_Falmer "Skyrim:Frozen Falmer") here.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.
- Fast travel from Forgotten Vale may cause the game to hang on a darkened map screen. This may be caused by fast travel being disabled at certain places or points in the questline and not being properly enabled again. **?**

Forsaken Cave

**Forsaken Cave** is a medium-sized [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Draugr "Skyrim:Draugr") and leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains two zones: *[Forsaken Cave](#Forsaken_Cave)* and *[Forsaken Crypt](#Forsaken_Crypt)*.

Its [word wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall") teaches part of the [Marked for Death](/wiki/Skyrim:Marked_for_Death "Skyrim:Marked for Death") [dragon shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts").

## Related Quests

- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)")**: Retrieve a [legendary artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(item) "Skyrim:The White Phial (item)") to fulfill an old [alchemist's](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion "Skyrim:Nurelion") wish in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

### Exterior

You can find the cave by following the [River Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:River_Yorgrim "Skyrim:River Yorgrim") west from Windhelm, staying on the north shore. A leveled [creature](/wiki/Skyrim:Creatures "Skyrim:Creatures") guards the entrance, which is flanked by three [burial urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Burial_Urn "Skyrim:Burial Urn") and a patch of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"). There is also an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") a few feet away to the southwest.

### Forsaken Cave

Skeleton, chest, and sword

Upon entering, you will see an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in a cart in front of you, and a lootable skeleton lying beside it with a random [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Sword "Skyrim:Sword") and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel") next to it. Continuing on, you will find yourself in an ice tunnel which turns and descends to the northeast. At the bottom, the tunnel opens into a cavern where two leveled animals roam around. There are numerous large [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn") and burial urns found throughout these ruins. Opposite where you enter is a concealed door flanked by wooden walls. Behind the walls are a total of four burial urns. This door is your shortcut exit from the end of the dungeon, and cannot be opened from this side. If you return to these ruins after they have respawned, you will find this door still open.

To the west you will find an iron door flanked by two flights of stairs that lead to raised areas that contain nothing of interest. Through the door is a short corridor that leads to a stairwell with a wooden spiral staircase down. At the bottom is a corridor heading north, which after a couple turns opens into a wide corridor that has had a cave-in to your left and continues to the east. Partway along the corridor is a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") that activates a [dart trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Dart_Trap "Skyrim:Dart Trap") from a statue in front of you. At the foot of the statue is an unlocked chest, while around the next corner a draugr waits.

The corridor staggers to the right, then continues to the east. At the end of this section is another draugr and a cave-in, with a narrow corridor on your left. This leads to a catacomb area with two alcoves ahead on the right. The first alcove contains a burial urn flanked by an [ancient Nord helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Helmet "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Helmet") and a pair of [ancient Nord boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_Boots "Skyrim:Ancient Nord Boots"). The second alcove holds only a burial urn. The path turns to the west and descends two short flights of stairs, where a draugr patrols. At the bottom are more catacombs and a second draugr.

Flame spout trap

Turning left, there is a draugr slumbering in an alcove on your right, and a stone table containing four [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Mirror](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror")* in front of you. To your left, down a short flight of stairs is an adept-locked iron door leading to a circular room with two large urns and an unlocked chest. Heading west, there is another draugr in an alcove on the left, and another ancient Nord helmet on the ground to the right of you. Continuing to the west, you will pass four more iron ingots in another alcove on your right. Follow the path as it twists and turns, looting any dead [draugr](/wiki/Skyrim:Containers#Draugr "Skyrim:Containers") as you go. You will pass several draugr in alcoves that will rise as you approach. Keep going until you find a stone table on your left with two [gold ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot") on top; on the table is also a stone bowl containing five more easily missed gold ingots. Heading due east from the table and climbing over the rubble, you will find an unlocked chest. Keep following the path, looting and defeating any draugr as you go; there are two more draugr roaming the area. You will pass an alcove with two [steel ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Ingot "Skyrim:Steel Ingot") in an upper alcove. There are three [flame spout traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Flame_Spout_Trap "Skyrim:Flame Spout Trap") along the path, and another that is disabled due to being covered with rubble from a cave-in. Eventually you will come to a narrow corridor heading east. Just after it turns to the north, there is a pressure plate that activates a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") in front of you. At the end, the corridor opens into a room containing several sets of shelves, which contain eight [silver ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), and an [ancient Nord war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Nord_War_Axe "Skyrim:Ancient Nord War Axe"). At the end of the room is an iron door leading to [Forsaken Crypt](#Forsaken_Crypt).

### Forsaken Crypt

Start of the crypt

Upon entering this area, you will find yourself in a short corridor leading into a large room with an open walkway and a caged walkway both above you at different heights. On your right is a balcony overlooking this room. There is one draugr patrolling this room, and several sarcophagi around the corner, on a raised section under a walkway. Against the east wall are two sets of shelves containing two iron ingots, several [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), and [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), and one random potion each of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka"), and [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina"). To the right of the shelves is a corridor heading east, leading up a short flight of stairs then turning to the north and climbing another flight of stairs. At the end, you enter more catacombs, with a draugr patrolling and a sideboard in front of you containing a pair of ancient Nord boots and a random [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"). The path turns to the west, then south near some burial urns, then back to the west. Keep following it up a flight of stairs and out onto a walkway above the previous room; this crosses to the balcony, where a draugr will burst forth from one of the sarcophagi. There is an unlocked chest in front of another sarcophagus, while on your left, a set of shelves holds two silver ingots, a random healing potion, and a bowl. The path continues across another walkway to the north, and leads to an iron door that opens into a room with two leveled draugr and a [ceiling spikes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ceiling_Spikes "Skyrim:Ceiling Spikes") trap in the middle. There is an expert-locked iron door to the west, and an unlocked iron door in the southeast corner. To the east is a caved-in corridor, with a partially lowered gate in front. There are two tables in the room, each with a burial urn on top. Behind the expert-locked door is a small chamber with an unlocked chest. Passing through the unlocked iron door in the southeast corner, you climb some stairs and cross the caged walkway above the previous room heading south. At the end is a wide corridor with several statues on either side. There is a draugr patrolling this area, and a second in an alcove to the right of the second statue on the left. Around the corner to the north is another alcove on the right with another draugr, then a final draugr in another alcove on your left after turning to the west. There is an iron door in the west wall.

Curalmil

Opening this door will activate a set of [swinging blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Blades "Skyrim:Swinging Blades") in the corridor ahead that leads to the final room, where you can see a single sarcophagus. When you approach the sarcophagus, its boss occupant will burst forth and attack. The boss will be aided by four other draugr who are standing by the side walls of the room, one of which is leveled and can be up to an overlord in strength. On your first visit, the boss will be [Curalmil](/wiki/Skyrim:Curalmil "Skyrim:Curalmil"), while subsequent visits after the dungeon resets will bring forth a generic leveled draugr boss. The word wall which teaches part of the Marked for Death shout is behind the sarcophagus and up a flight of stairs. There is a boss chest in front of the word wall. Under the word wall is a corridor that leads to an ancient bowl if you are here on the quest [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)"). Activating the bowl will have you pour [Nurelion's mixture](/wiki/Skyrim:Nurelion%27s_Mixture "Skyrim:Nurelion's Mixture") into it, which lowers the stone wall in front of you and allows access to the final chamber containing the [Cracked White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Cracked_White_Phial "Skyrim:Cracked White Phial").

A hidden alchemy room

As you enter this chamber, you will see a sideboard on your left holding a bowl of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a bowl of six [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") flowers, two [orange dartwings](/wiki/Skyrim:Orange_Dartwing "Skyrim:Orange Dartwing"), a bowl of five [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), and three random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"). Against the south wall is a stone table holding a copy of the [Alchemy](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy "Skyrim:Alchemy") skill book *[A Game at Dinner](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Game_at_Dinner "Skyrim:A Game at Dinner")*, two burial urns and two [apothecary's satchels](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). In front on a raised section is a plinth holding the Cracked White Phial. To the north is another sideboard containing two more orange dartwings, a deathbell flower, a bowl of five chaurus eggs, a random poison, and a bowl containing a [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"). To the left is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with a sample of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), and opposite this is a set of shelves containing a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") flower, an orange dartwing, two random poisons, a bowl of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a bowl of ectoplasm, six [torchbug thoraxes](/wiki/Skyrim:Torchbug_Thorax "Skyrim:Torchbug Thorax") in a bowl, another sample of giant lichen, and a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts").

Back in the main chamber, there is an iron door in the southwest corner that leads up a flight of stairs to another iron door, which opens into a small room in Forsaken Cave. Pulling the lever on your right opens a hidden door that brings you back to the dungeon's entrance.

## Notes

- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), the *Forsaken Cave* zone will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- During The White Phial, the Phial can disappear if you leave the dungeon without taking it.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.4, fixes this bug.
- The ceiling spikes trap can cause you to clip through the ceiling and end up on the level above.
  - Reloading the game should resolve the issue.
- The ancient Nord boots and random helmet on a sideboard near the start of the crypt may not respawn with the rest of the ruin. **?**
- Although the lid blows off the dragon priest's sarcophagus when triggered, the boss draugr inside may not emerge until you approach him. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Forsaken Cave
- 

  Forsaken Crypt

## Overview
