Fort Amol

**Fort Amol** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southwest of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") initially occupied by [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Amol](#Fort_Amol)* and *[Fort Amol Prison](#Fort_Amol_Prison)*.

The fort will be taken over by the faction that wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Windhelm if you first clear it of warlocks (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") by taking Fort Amol for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

As you travel down the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"), a small stone cairn will mark the path to Fort Amol. Its walls are easily visible from the riverbank. Four hostile elemental mages are outside, in and around the courtyard. If you approach from the road, one will attack you before you even enter the fort. Two others may join the fray from inside the courtyard. A final mage can be found on top of the barracks performing some type of ritual. Corpses of slain [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") can be found throughout the fort exterior, as well as an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"). There is a chest and a [shrine of Julianos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Julianos "Skyrim:Shrines") next to the alchemy lab, however it is replaced by a smithing station if the quest Civil War has been completed. Another chest can be found in the eastern tower.

After you clear out the mages, Stormcloaks will retake the fort. If you follow the [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") Civil War questline, a battle will be fought here, after which the garrison will change to Imperial. If you are not aligned with the faction controlling the fort, they will consider you to be trespassing if you enter either of the two interior zones. However, if you are allied with the faction controlling the fort, you can get rest, food, and a horse here.

### Fort Amol

As you enter from the ground level in the courtyard, a mage will be standing in the next room. Any sound of battle with him will likely cause the other two mages from upstairs to join the fray. This can make for a very warm welcome. Be very wary of the fire mages, as they can do large amounts of damage very quickly, especially if carrying items such as a [staff of firebolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Firebolts "Skyrim:Staff of Firebolts"). The downstairs entrance room contains a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") by a fireplace, and a table holding a [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a dagger, and a set of blue mage robes. The room to the northwest hosts an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") and a large number of potions, [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"), and alchemical [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). A copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Catalogue of Armor Enchantments](/wiki/Skyrim:Catalogue_of_Armor_Enchantments "Skyrim:Catalogue of Armor Enchantments")* is lying on the cupboard along with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"). A locked chest can be found in the northwest corner on a wooden platform. The upstairs room contains some iron armor and weapons lying around, as well as two medium [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), three loose gold coins, various ingredients, a poison next to a bed in the northwest corner, and a second (unlocked) chest.

### Fort Amol Prison

The central guard chamber contains two mages that will attack as soon as they spot you. They are much tougher than the weaker ones in the courtyard. In this entry chamber, a scroll, a potion, and a [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") are on and near the central table, while two more leveled soul gems are on a set of shelves to the northeast. In the western corner, to the right of the two bookshelves, pick up or move the lantern inside the bucket to discover a *[Spell Tome: Bound Bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Bound_Bow "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Bound Bow")* underneath. Otherwise, the prison holds nothing of interest, not even lockpicking practice, since all the prison cells are already unlocked.

## Notes

- If you're aligned with the Imperials, after completing the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Amol "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Amol"):
  - The fort will be occupied by [Imperial soldiers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier"), as well as a [Fort Commander](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Commander "Skyrim:Fort Commander") who oversees the fort's operations.
  - A [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), an anvil, a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") will replace the shrine of Julianos.
- Earlier in the game's development, the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") was tied to the factions of the Civil War, and you seemingly chose a side before you could first encounter dragons. If you chose the Imperial Legion, [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") would send you with [Captain Metilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Metilius "Skyrim:Captain Metilius") to investigate reports of a dragon at [Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad"). If you instead joined the Stormcloaks, [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") would send you along with someone named Sifnar (this person might have been [Sifnar Ironkettle](/wiki/Skyrim:Sifnar_Ironkettle "Skyrim:Sifnar Ironkettle"), but the latter may have been named after the former) to investigate a similar disturbance at Fort Amol. Little evidence of this remains in the game's files, with only a few markers (`MQ104BSifnarCourtyardMarker1`), AI packages, and leftover scripts (`MQ104Script`) still referring to this iteration. The DialogueViews files hold two player-only topic lines that internally still refer to Sifar, `MQ00DragonbornSifnarB1` and `MQ00DragonbornSifnarB2`, which read *"I don't know what happened to me."* and *"I think you may be right."*, respectively. These are the same lines you can use when the unnamed [Whiterun guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") approaches and names you Dragonborn after you kill [Mirmulnir](/wiki/Skyrim:Mirmulnir "Skyrim:Mirmulnir") in the final version of the quest.
- Fort Amol also appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Amol "Arena:Amol")* and [ESO](/wiki/Online:Fort_Amol "Online:Fort Amol").

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  -  The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- When the Imperials occupy the fort, the alchemy bench will become embedded in a workbench. Similarly, there will be one chest embedded within another right next to it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug.
- The Stormcloak corpses and the ritual circle atop one of the towers will remain after the hostile mages are expelled.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- There was supposed to be an Amulet of Julianos near the shrine; however, it is incorrectly embedded within the shrine itself, and is not directly accessible.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug.
  - Explosive effects can dislodge it and make it accessible again.
- The Bound Bow spell tome may not be inside the bucket when you enter the prison after the Stormcloaks take over. **?**

## Maps

- 

  Fort Amol
- 

  Fort Amol Prison

A Fort Commander

The **Fort Commander** is available once a side in the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") has taken over a fort. If there is a Fort Commander's Quarters he will be found in them, if not he can be found inside the fort. Apart from his name he is a generic [Imperial soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") and has generic [Imperial soldier](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") dialogue.

Fort Dawnguard

**Fort Dawnguard** is a large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") which serves as the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)")'s base of operations.

[†](#note_Crafting)The alchemy lab, arcane enchanter, and forge are not initially present in the fort, but added during restorations to the fort just before the Prophet quest ends.

The fort is home to the ancient order of [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") hunters who guard the realm from the vampiric Volkihar clan. It is hidden in the east of [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), and can be used as a player home. It can only be reached via [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon").

The fort was built sometime in the [Second Era](/wiki/Lore:Second_Era "Lore:Second Era") by the Jarl of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") to contain his son, who had contracted vampirism. He hired a large mercenary band called the Dawnguard to guard his son. The threat of vampires was eventually disregarded by the people of Skyrim, and the fort was abandoned. [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran") is using the fort as a base of operations for his attempt to rebuild the Dawnguard and combat the rising threat of the vampires.

#### Dawnguard Questline

- **[Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(quest) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (quest)")**: Speak with the leader of the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
- **[Awakening](/wiki/Skyrim:Awakening "Skyrim:Awakening")**: Find out what the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan") are looking for.
- **[Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodline "Skyrim:Bloodline")**: Choose your side!
- **[Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)")**: Find and rescue [a Moth Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dexion_Evicus "Skyrim:Dexion Evicus") from the [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan").
- **[Chasing Echoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Chasing_Echoes "Skyrim:Chasing Echoes")**: Explore [Castle Volkihar](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar").
- **[Unseen Visions](/wiki/Skyrim:Unseen_Visions "Skyrim:Unseen Visions")**: Perform a ceremony to read the Elder Scroll.

#### Side Quests

- **[Ancient Technology](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Technology "Skyrim:Ancient Technology")**: Retrieve Dwemer schematics to improve technology for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Bolstering the Ranks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bolstering_the_Ranks "Skyrim:Bolstering the Ranks")**: Find [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") and recruit him into the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)").
- **[Cleansing Light](/wiki/Skyrim:Cleansing_Light "Skyrim:Cleansing Light")**: Kill the boss of a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") lair. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Destroying the Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Destroying_the_Dawnguard "Skyrim:Destroying the Dawnguard")**: Kill the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)") leaders.
- **[Hide and Seek](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(quest) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (quest)")**: Kill a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") masquerading as a citizen. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Lost Relic](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Relic "Skyrim:Lost Relic")**: Retrieve a relic of the original [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**: Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Rescue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue "Skyrim:Rescue")**: Rescue a victim from [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Fort Dawnguard

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| [Map of Fort Dawnguard interior](/wiki/File:SR-map-Fort_Dawnguard.jpg "Map of Fort Dawnguard interior") [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Dayspring Canyon")  [A](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon")  [Dead Drop Falls](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Drop_Falls "Dead Drop Falls")  [B](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Drop_Falls "Skyrim:Dead Drop Falls")  [Main Hall](/wiki/File:White_pog.png "Main Hall")  1  [Gunmar's Forge](/wiki/File:White_pog.png "Gunmar's Forge")  2  [Armored Troll enclosure](/wiki/File:White_pog.png "Armored Troll enclosure")  3  [Husky enclosure](/wiki/File:White_pog.png "Husky enclosure")  4  [Torture Room](/wiki/File:White_pog.png "Torture Room")  5  Map of Fort Dawnguard interior |  | Doors A: [Dayspring Canyon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dayspring_Canyon "Skyrim:Dayspring Canyon")  B: [Dead Drop Falls](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Drop_Falls "Skyrim:Dead Drop Falls") Rooms  1. Main Hall 2. Gunmar's Forge 3. Armored Troll enclosure 4. Husky enclosure 5. Torture Room |

The vestibule contains a [crossbow](/wiki/Skyrim:Crossbow "Skyrim:Crossbow"), eight [steel bolts](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Bolt "Skyrim:Steel Bolt"), and a [Dawnguard helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Helmet "Skyrim:Dawnguard Helmet") on wooden crates, six Dawnguard banners, a light source that gives off sunlight, and a random leveled two-handed weapon on a weapon rack. The kitchen contains a [cooking spit](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Spit "Skyrim:Cooking Spit") with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") beside it, four dead [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit "Skyrim:Rabbit") and two dead [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") above the fireplace, two Dawnguard banners on both sides of the fireplace, a bucket holding a broom in the corner, two [candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") on the floor, and two [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a [Dawnguard war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_War_Axe "Skyrim:Dawnguard War Axe") on the dining table. The area behind the kitchen has a table with two bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a coin purse, six loose septims, and a map of Skyrim with an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on it, another bottle of wine on a table behind it, and a bookshelf with copies of [Cats of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Cats_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Cats of Skyrim"), [Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Harvesting_Frostbite_Spider_Venom "Skyrim:Harvesting Frostbite Spider Venom"), and [Ode To The Tundrastriders](/wiki/Skyrim:Ode_To_The_Tundrastriders "Skyrim:Ode To The Tundrastriders"). The sleeping quarters contain pairs of [Dawnguard boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Boots "Skyrim:Dawnguard Boots") and [Dawnguard gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dawnguard Gauntlets"), eight steel bolts, copies of [The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars") and [The Wispmother](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wispmother "Skyrim:The Wispmother"), and [sliced goat cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Goat_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Goat Cheese"). The smithing area contains a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"), [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"), [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter"), a coin purse, a [Dwemer cog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"), and some [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") behind the smelter, two [bleeding crowns](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), two archery targets flanked by lit braziers, another crossbow, six steel bolts, a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"), four [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow"), three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), and a [potion of cure disease](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Cure_Disease "Skyrim:Potion of Cure Disease"). The enchanting room has an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab"), an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), two [troll skulls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), and another copy of The Aetherium Wars. The troll pen has raw meat and a [silverside perch](/wiki/Skyrim:Silverside_Perch "Skyrim:Silverside Perch"). The husky room has ten steel bolts and 14 [steel arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Arrow "Skyrim:Steel Arrow"), three combat dummies, two bleeding crowns, four [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), one [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap"), and the exit to [Dead Drop Falls](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Drop_Falls "Skyrim:Dead Drop Falls"). The area upstairs has a master bed, a weapon rack, a mannequin, a coin purse, four wardrobes, and a torture room with three iron ingots, a loose septim, a set of [torture tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Tools "Skyrim:Torture Tools"), another [torture tool](/wiki/Skyrim:Torture_Tool "Skyrim:Torture Tool")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), a hammer, a broom leaning behind a chair, a bucket with two iron daggers, blood splashes on the floor, and bloody bones scattered throughout.

There are three balconies on the roof of Fort Dawnguard, accessible from the fort itself. One of them has two more crossbows, 21 steel bolts, three Dawnguard war axes, a [Dawnguard warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Warhammer "Skyrim:Dawnguard Warhammer"), three steel arrows, two bed rolls, a small coin purse, a bottle of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), an [Amulet of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Talos "Skyrim:Amulet of Talos"), and copies of [The Talos Mistake](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Talos_Mistake "Skyrim:The Talos Mistake") and [2920, Morning Star, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Morning_Star,_v1 "Skyrim:2920, Morning Star, v1"). Another one has two more crossbows, 14 steel bolts, another Dawnguard war axe, another Dawnguard helmet, another pair of Dawnguard gauntlets, a [Scroll of Banish Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Banish_Daedra "Skyrim:Scroll of Banish Daedra"), two magicka potions, a bed roll, a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"), and a copy of [The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lusty_Argonian_Maid,_v1 "Skyrim:The Lusty Argonian Maid, v1"). The third has three more crossbows, 16 steel bolts, three more Dawnguard war axes, another Dawnguard warhammer, another pair of Dawnguard boots, a [Dawnguard shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_Shield "Skyrim:Dawnguard Shield"), another grindstone, another tanning rack, three Dawnguard banners around the tower, 13 steel arrows, a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), a small coin purse, a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), a bed roll, a magicka potion, [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"), [cooked beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooked_Beef "Skyrim:Cooked Beef"), a bowl of [beef stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Beef_Stew "Skyrim:Beef Stew"), and two bottles of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead").

## Notes

- Five members of the Dawnguard are available as [followers](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") after the Dawnguard version of the quest [Prophet](/wiki/Skyrim:Prophet_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Prophet (Dawnguard)") is completed. They are noted with the  icon in the NPC table above.
- The [All Forge](/wiki/Skyrim:All_Forge "Skyrim:All Forge")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") added by the [Myrwatch](/wiki/Skyrim:Myrwatch "Skyrim:Myrwatch") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") can be used to craft items usually restricted to Gunmar's forge.
- There are two war dogs in the dog pen in the northeast section of the fort, available as canine followers.
- You can buy armored [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") for 500 gold from [Gunmar](/wiki/Skyrim:Gunmar "Skyrim:Gunmar").
- All 3 merchants here benefit from the [Master Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Master_Trader "Skyrim:Master Trader") perk. You can invest with [Florentius Baenius](/wiki/Skyrim:Florentius_Baenius "Skyrim:Florentius Baenius") as well.
- There is a grindstone and tanning rack on the roof, reachable by climbing the west stairway inside and exiting at the top. These are technically in Dayspring Canyon, not part of Fort Dawnguard, though they can only be accessed via the fort.
- If you use the snow on the east side of the mountain behind the highest balcony, you can potentially use it to walk along the ledge and drop down to the two lower balconies, and scale the mountain to get to the rest of Dayspring Canyon without backtracking through the fort. Don't drop down too far, though, or you'll instantly die once you land.
- You can access [Dead Drop Falls](/wiki/Skyrim:Dead_Drop_Falls "Skyrim:Dead Drop Falls") through the southwest section of Fort Dawnguard. The entrance is between three combat mannequins and the armored husky paddock.
- If you become a vampire after siding with the Dawnguard in the Dawnguard questline, NPCs in the fort will refuse to speak to you until you [get yourself cured](/wiki/Skyrim:Rising_at_Dawn "Skyrim:Rising at Dawn").
- If you clip through the stone pillars in the enchanting area, you'll come across 3 merchant chests. Two of them are considered owned, but the third one isn't.
- If you have allied with the Dawnguard, [vampire scouts](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Scout "Skyrim:Vampire Scout") will occasionally appear near the fast travel arrival point to the fort.
- If you have allied with the Volkihar vampire clan, all the bodies of named NPCs killed during the quest Destroying the Dawnguard will never disappear.
- A similar-looking magna-geode stone with the same shape and appearance as [Meridia's Beacon](/wiki/Skyrim:Meridia%27s_Beacon "Skyrim:Meridia's Beacon") is found within Fort Dawnguard.

## Bugs

- When placing a weapon on the weapon rack in the master bedroom you won't be able to retrieve it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Dawnguard gear intended to be equipped on the nearby mannequin is mistakenly set to respawn, which causes the mannequin to duplicate the gear every time the cell resets.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 2.0.3, fixes this bug.
- The interior of Fort Dawnguard is not oriented correctly, meaning that the compass points south when entering and exiting.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- The tomes for the 3 spells you can only buy here ([Sun Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Fire "Skyrim:Sun Fire"), [Vampire's Bane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire%27s_Bane "Skyrim:Vampire's Bane"), and [Stendarr's Aura](/wiki/Skyrim:Stendarr%27s_Aura "Skyrim:Stendarr's Aura")) all use world and inventory art for [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") books, yet they are actually [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration") spells.
  -  The [Unofficial Dawnguard Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dawnguard_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dawnguard Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- There is a copy of the spell tome [Sun Fire](/wiki/Skyrim:Sun_Fire "Skyrim:Sun Fire") underneath the floor in the enchanting room.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.3, addresses this issue. The book has been moved to a shelf near the enchanting table.
- Although the fort is located within [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift"), crimes committed here may earn a bounty in [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"). **?**

Fort Dunstad

**Fort Dunstad** is a large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") south of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains four zones: *[Fort Dunstad](#Fort_Dunstad)*, *[Fort Dunstad Prison](#Fort_Dunstad_Prison)*, *[Fort Dunstad Commander's Quarters](#Fort_Dunstad_Commander.27s_Quarters)*, and *[The Stumbling Sabrecat](#The_Stumbling_Sabrecat)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Dawnstar if you first clear it of bandits.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Imperial)")**: Take Fort Dunstad for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Dunstad_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Dunstad (Stormcloaks)")**: Reclaim this fort for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The body of an unfortunate Dunmer [alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist "Skyrim:Alchemist") can be seen inside a cage hanging from a beam off one of the towers. A potion and three loose arrows are in a bucket on the roof of the section housing the Commander's Quarters; another bucket with arrows and a potion is at the top of the guard tower next to the southern gate.

### Fort Dunstad

The main entrance is at ground level. The interior features a large room, opening on the left to a spiral staircase bracing the tower. The tower itself has two levels built around a free-standing chimney (with harvestable [charred skeevers](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide")), and a latrine complete with buckets, reading material, and a potion of true shot on the second floor. A chest is also found on the second floor, to the right of the latrine. A trapdoor at the top of the stairs allows access to the ruined exterior. Underneath the hot coals in the middle of the second floor room is a trapdoor that requires a key, but no key for it exists, and in any case it leads nowhere. Before the fort undergoes its conversion due to the Civil War questline, five leveled bandits roam the place, most of them apparently engaged in [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") fighting in the big room downstairs by the ground level entrance; two iron cages and a small fenced arena have been set up for this purpose. This area is later repurposed as a dining hall and dormitory for the soldiers.

### Fort Dunstad Prison

Located in the northwest corner of the fort, the prison has two entrances: the main entrance at ground level, and another entrance over the stone walls. The door at ground level opens to a small set of stairs descending to a long hallway with an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks") leading to the first level of the tower. This floor contains two holding cells and a spike wall trap, activated by a lever mounted on the wall. One of the holding cells contains an apprentice-locked chest. A spiral staircase provides access to the second level, with four [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging near the top of the staircase. This level contains three more cells, an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs"), a large table holding a dead [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf_(NPC) "Skyrim:High Elf (NPC)"), a small table holding a poison and a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom") with some clutter, and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). A copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[2920, MidYear, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_MidYear,_v6 "Skyrim:2920, MidYear, v6")* can be found on a shelf next to the lab. An open wall cage between the alchemy lab and the doorway holds several healing potions. There's also another oil slick in this room. Up to two bandit chiefs can spawn here, and hostile skeevers are being held in the cells of both levels of the tower. Exiting using the ladder in this top floor room places you outside on the roof of the tower, where you will find a boss chest along with a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and two potions of resist cold next to an unoccupied chair. The corpse of the Dunmer alchemist hanging in the cage can be accessed from this position if you maneuver carefully, although it holds nothing of note.

### Fort Dunstad Commander's Quarters

The only entrance to the Commander's Quarters is above the stone battlements, on the south wall. To the left of the entrance is a small arch bridging the space where the fort's [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") is located. The interior comprises a small hallway connected to a bedroom on the right. An alchemy lab and four cupboards are in the hallway, but after starting the Civil War quests, a long table with a strategic map of Skyrim is added, and the lab is replaced by a large wooden chest. Also before the Civil War questline, a leveled bandit wizard spawns in the bedroom, which features a double bed, two cupboards, two end tables, and a dresser, while a total of ten potions and poisons, two bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"), a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and two loose gold coins can be found on the various shelves in the area.

### The Stumbling Sabrecat

This tavern is within the wooden stockade next to the stone battlements on the eastern side of the fort. For details on the location, see [The Stumbling Sabrecat](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Stumbling_Sabrecat "Skyrim:The Stumbling Sabrecat").

## Notes

- The skeevers kept by the bandits during their occupation of the fort are hostile to the bandits.

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.

## Maps

- 

  Fort Dunstad
- 

  Fort Dunstad Prison
- 

  Fort Dunstad Commander's Quarters

# Skyrim:Fort Fellhammer

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Fort Fellhammer ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Fellhammer)) | | |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |

Fort Fellhammer

**Fort Fellhammer** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") and [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron "Skyrim:Iron") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") south of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Fellhammer Garrison](#Fort_Fellhammer_Garrison)* and *[Fort Fellhammer Mines](#Fort_Fellhammer_Mines)*.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Jarl_-_Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Jarl - Caves)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir") by retrieving the [Helm of Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Helm_of_Winterhold "Skyrim:Helm of Winterhold").
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad").
- **[Striking the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Striking_the_Heart "Skyrim:Striking the Heart")**: Assassinate a leader of the Silver Hand.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The fort is south of Dawnstar, off the paved road which leads to [Fort Dunstad](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Dunstad "Skyrim:Fort Dunstad") to the southwest. After the road passes [Red Road Pass](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Road_Pass "Skyrim:Red Road Pass"), it turns east. At the point where it begins to turn westwards, a dirt path leads farther east to the fort. Five [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") plants and one [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") grow around the junction of the dirt path and the main road. A further five snowberry plants and one more blue mountain flower are found along the dirt path.

The fort is guarded by three bandits, who patrol the outer walls. The walls form a circular path from the left of the entrance all the way to the top of the garrison, though there is nothing up there. Part of the right-hand wall has collapsed, allowing for entry that way. There is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") beside the stairs to the left of the entrance. The expert-locked door to the [mines](#Fort_Fellhammer_Mines) (unlocked by the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fellhammer_Mine_Key "Skyrim:Fellhammer Mine Key") held by the bandit boss in the garrison) is on the ground level, and the door to the [garrison](#Fort_Fellhammer_Garrison) is on the first level.

### Fort Fellhammer Garrison

Bandit boss

The garrison is a small area split into two rooms: the main garrison bedroom, and a smaller storage or dining room. There is only one enemy here, though it is the boss of the dungeon. They spend all their time sitting in the chair in the smaller of the two rooms.

There are three beds in the main room, and a table, chair, and chest in the smaller room. To the right of the entrance, a [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") is growing through the stones, and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), and some books are on a ledge on the wall to the far left of the entrance. On the table in the small room is a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"), some food, and several bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and behind the door is a basket with two samples of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"). There are two plaques in the garrison: one weapon plaque opposite the entrance with an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and one shield plaque in the small room with two crossed [iron greatswords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") and a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield").

### Fort Fellhammer Mines

Dropping in on a bandit

The mines contain a large number of iron ore veins, ten in total. Just before the tunnel turns downwards, there is a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") on a wooden block and a cart to the left with four pieces of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore"). At the bottom of the slope is a hole with some [rotten planks](/wiki/Skyrim:Rotten_Planks "Skyrim:Rotten Planks") over it. Through the hole a bandit can be seen mining a vein. If you fall through the hole, you will need to traverse the mine backwards, though that would decrease the time to exit the mine. Past the hole, the path turns right and heads deeper into the ground. A bandit patrols along here. Just to the right before the corner is a [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown") fungus, with another behind the barrel to the left, and a third to the left after the tunnel has turned. There are two ore veins here, one to the left, and one straight ahead down a ramp.

There is an ore vein to the right just before the slope downwards, and a cart at the bottom with three pieces of iron ore. At the next corner there are two veins to the left, and one straight ahead. The tunnel turns to the right, and on a table there is a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")*, a [leather helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Helmet "Skyrim:Leather Helmet"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), and a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg").

To the left along the path after the table is another bleeding crown, and a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that makes some [boulders fall](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders") from the ceiling ahead. Not too far after that is the bandit observable from the hole above, with another bandit farther along. There is one vein with the first bandit, and three more by the last bandit, two on the left and another on the right. There is a barrel between the two left-hand veins that holds a [garnet](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Notes

- Killing the bandit boss clears the fort, but you may wish to avoid this, as it will force a 30-day waiting period for the ore veins to respawn. If you leave the boss alive, you can visit the mines every ten days for more iron ore, making the fort a prolific source of iron ore. Some quests that send you here only require an item to be retrieved, which can still be done without killing the boss, though the target chest is beside the boss.
- With the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, this dungeon is an excellent place to stock up on iron for [housebuilding](/wiki/Skyrim:Construction "Skyrim:Construction") purposes.

## Bugs

- Fast travelling here during [Purity of Revenge](/wiki/Skyrim:Purity_of_Revenge "Skyrim:Purity of Revenge") may automatically complete the optional objective to wipe out the [Silver Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Hand "Skyrim:Silver Hand") members at [Driftshade Refuge](/wiki/Skyrim:Driftshade_Refuge "Skyrim:Driftshade Refuge"), though they may not actually be dead when you arrive there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. The bandits at Fort Fellhammer all had a script attached to them when they never needed one.

## Maps

- 

  Fort Fellhammer Garrison
- 

  Fort Fellhammer Mines

# Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Fort Frostmoth ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Fort+Frostmoth)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Fort_Frostmoth "Lore:Fort Frostmoth")) | | |

| # of [Ruby Geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby "Skyrim:Ruby") | 3 |

Fort Frostmoth

**Fort Frostmoth** is a small [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") south of [Highpoint Tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Highpoint_Tower "Skyrim:Highpoint Tower") and northeast of [Hrodulf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Hrodulf%27s_House "Skyrim:Hrodulf's House") occupied by [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") and [General Falx Carius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Falx_Carius "Skyrim:General Falx Carius").

For historical information on Fort Frostmoth, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Fort_Frostmoth "Lore:Fort Frostmoth") and *[History of Raven Rock, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._I "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. I")*.

## Related Quests

- **[March of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:March_of_the_Dead "Skyrim:March of the Dead")**: Stop the [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") attacks on [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

A small dock patrolled by an [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") is south of the fort, with a submerged broken boat holding three mead barrels. Two flights of stairs ascend to the north. At the top of the second flight, to the east is a tower, and to the west is another flight of stairs. The tower is guarded by an ash spawn, and contains a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") and a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") among the ash at the bottom of a few stairs.

The third flight of stairs ascends to the outer wall of the fort, with an archway in the wall to the north. Passing through the archway into the courtyard will cause two ash spawn to rise from the middle of the courtyard, and you will hear [General Falx Carius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Falx_Carius "Skyrim:General Falx Carius") alert the guards to your presence. A third ash spawn patrols the wall above you, and a fourth ash spawn is on the roof of the northeast tower. You can climb the spiral staircase in the tower to reach the roof, but it contains nothing of interest.

The courtyard has a thick covering of ash, in which a pair of empty stables and several archery targets and sparring dummies are partly buried. To the west is a building with two towers and an unlocked door in the middle. To the north is another building with a single tower to the right and a key-locked door to the left.

### Fort Frostmoth

The unlocked door leads into an entry area, with a small room to the north and a short north-south corridor to the west. As you move west, an ash spawn will rise in front of you in the corridor. The room contains a table and two chairs, one mostly buried in ash and unusable, and two random potions of [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), or [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on the floor near the table. Past the room and to the north in the corridor, a broken wall to the west allows access to another room. Near the northwest corner of the room is a usable bed. Near the southwest corner is one of three partly buried unusable beds, with a [horse hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Hide "Skyrim:Horse Hide"), a knapsack, and an adept-locked chest among the ash around the bed. Along the east wall is a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt"), a sideboard holding a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and a food barrel. In the southeast corner is a door which opens to the previous corridor, with an ash spawn just outside the door.

Opposite the door and just south of the entrance is a storage alcove. Along the north wall of the alcove is a row of six weapon racks, with an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") in one of the racks and a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword") on the floor. Along the east wall is a set of shelves holding three [imperial helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet"), two pairs of [imperial bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Bracers"), two pairs of [imperial light bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Bracers "Skyrim:Imperial Light Bracers"), two pairs of [imperial boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Boots"), and two pairs of [imperial light boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Boots "Skyrim:Imperial Light Boots"). To the right of the shelves is another set of shelves holding an [imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor") cuirass, an imperial helmet, an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). Along the south wall is a third set of shelves holding a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"), three books, three [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox"). To the right of the shelves is a food barrel.

To the south is a doorway to a circular room with a wooden ramp ascending to a ladder and a trapdoor exit in the ceiling. Next to the ladder is a small round table holding a leveled bow and a quiver of arrows. Along the east wall are two sacks, two pieces of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood"), a bench, a [banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor") cuirass on the floor in front of the bench, and a set of shelves holding two random potions and a deer pelt. Beneath the ramp is another piece of firewood. Along the west wall is a straw bale with a sack on top, a sample of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") on the floor, a bench, and a set of shelves holding four books.

Exiting through the trapdoor leads to the roof of the building's south tower, with an empty wooden platform nearby and two ash spawn on guard. A stone bridge crosses to the north tower, where another wooden platform holds a chest. It is possible to use the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") from the roof of the north tower to reach the roof of the other building to the northeast, and from there climb onto the roof of that building's tower. On the tower roof is an empty wooden platform, a trapdoor, and a leveled [heavy armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet") and a random enchanted [cuirass](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") next to the trapdoor. The trapdoor serves as a shortcut to the final confrontation with General Carius.

Returning to the first corridor inside the west building's unlocked entrance, a flight of stairs to the north descends to a room with a master-locked cell door ahead and two ash spawn to the right. In the southwest corner is an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") and a quiver of arrows. Along the west wall is a doorway blocked by cobwebs. In the northwest corner is a patch of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungus. To the right of the locked door are two sacks and a fish barrel. Around a corner to the northeast are three more sacks and a crate, with a caved-in alcove to the left containing *[A Letter to Selina IV](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Letter_to_Selina_IV "Skyrim:A Letter to Selina IV")*, the lootable skeleton of [Maximian Axius](/wiki/Skyrim:Maximian_Axius "Skyrim:Maximian Axius"), and a knapsack containing his three previous letters *[A Letter to Selina I](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Letter_to_Selina_I "Skyrim:A Letter to Selina I")*, *[II](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Letter_to_Selina_II "Skyrim:A Letter to Selina II")*, and *[III](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Letter_to_Selina_III "Skyrim:A Letter to Selina III")*. Along the east wall is a key-locked door. In the northeast corner are six pieces of firewood that have fallen out of an overturned cart. Along the north wall is a partly collapsed tunnel leading down.

Beyond the webbed doorway to the west is another partly collapsed tunnel leading down. At the bottom are several unusual [spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiders "Skyrim:Spiders"). When killed, any that aren't albino are destroyed. The bodies of the [albino spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider "Skyrim:Albino Spider") can be looted for [albino spider pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Albino Spider Pod") and [damaged albino spider pods](/wiki/Skyrim:Damaged_Albino_Spider_Pod "Skyrim:Damaged Albino Spider Pod"), which can be used to create [spider scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Scrolls "Skyrim:Spider Scrolls") in [White Ridge Barrow](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Ridge_Barrow "Skyrim:White Ridge Barrow"). At the bottom of the tunnel is a cavern containing six albino spider eggs which can be looted for both types of pods. In the southeast corner is a [heart stone deposit](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone_Deposit "Skyrim:Heart Stone Deposit") and a [ruby geode](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruby_Geode "Skyrim:Ruby Geode"). In the southwest corner, a lower partly flooded path runs along the west wall, with a second heart stone deposit and a second ruby geode on the wall. To the north is a short dead-end tunnel containing two more albino spider eggs, with a third ruby geode east of the tunnel entrance.

Returning to the previous room, beyond the master-locked door to the north is a storeroom featuring two sets of shelves on either side of a barrel containing eight portions of [moon sugar](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Sugar "Skyrim:Moon Sugar"). The shelves hold eight bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), five bottles of [Cyrodilic brandy](/wiki/Skyrim:Cyrodilic_Brandy "Skyrim:Cyrodilic Brandy"), six bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), eight [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), two bottles of [spiced wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiced_Wine "Skyrim:Spiced Wine"), and five bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). To the right of the shelves is a boss-level chest. In the northeast corner are two mead barrels.

Returning again to the previous room, the tunnel descending to the north leads to a corridor lined with two rows of coffins, five of which can be looted for [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), bones, low-quality clothing, or a few [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). A pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") is next to the lower coffin on the right. At the end of the corridor is an east-west corridor lined with more coffins, with an ash spawn to the west. Along the north wall opposite the first corridor is an unlootable coffin with two random potions of healing, magicka, or stamina on top. To the east, the six coffins on either side are all lootable. An [iron ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and a leather strip are next to the bottom coffin on the left, and a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") is next to the bottom coffin on the right. Past the coffins is a cave-in.

To the west, the six coffins on either side are all lootable. An [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), a bowl of [glow dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Glow_Dust "Skyrim:Glow Dust"), and a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") are next to the upper coffins on the right. Past the coffins is a doorway to a large room lined with twelve coffins, nine of which are lootable, with two more lootable coffins stacked in the middle. A [pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl "Skyrim:Pearl") in a metal bowl and three iron daggers are next to the middle lower coffin along the south wall. A random potion and a leveled one-handed enchanted sword are in a fallen open coffin along the west wall, with a chest behind the coffin. A bottle of Nord mead in a metal bowl and a sample of wheat are next to the left upper coffin along the north wall. An apothecary's satchel and [Ildari's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ildari%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ildari's Journal") are on top of the two stacked coffins in the middle of the room, with a knapsack containing the [Fort Frostmoth key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Frostmoth_Key "Skyrim:Fort Frostmoth Key") and other loot next to the coffins.

Returning once again to the previous room, the door to the east requires the key from the knapsack. Beyond the door, a long flight of stairs ascends to a room with a damaged stone pillar surrounded by wooden supports. Behind the pillar to the left is General Carius, who wields the unique [Champion's Cudgel](/wiki/Skyrim:Champion%27s_Cudgel "Skyrim:Champion's Cudgel"). Attacking him will cause three ash spawn to rise around the room. Along the west wall is a cupboard holding nine books and a troll skull. In the northwest corner is a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing") on a partly buried table. In the northeast corner are two bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") on the floor and a garlic braid hanging from a rack. Along the east wall is a large doorway to a circular room containing three usable chairs, a small table in the middle holding a rare [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(weapon) "Skyrim:Knife (weapon)") weapon, a cupboard along the east wall, a boss-level chest to the southeast, and a ladder and a trapdoor exit in the ceiling along the south wall. The cupboard holds a set of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"), seven books, a random potion of magicka, and a random potion of healing, magicka, or stamina. Along the south wall in the previous room is a key-locked door. Exiting through the trapdoor leads to the roof of the north building's tower. Exiting through the key-locked door leads to the courtyard.

## Notes

- [Fort Frostmoth](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Fort_Frostmoth "Bloodmoon:Fort Frostmoth") previously appeared in [Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon"), when it was still an Imperial fort.
