Fort Greenwall

**Fort Greenwall** is a large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") north-northwest of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains four zones: *[Fort Greenwall](#Fort_Greenwall)*, *[Fort Greenwall Prison](#Fort_Greenwall_Prison)*, *[Fort Greenwall Captain's Quarters](#Fort_Greenwall_Captain.27s_Quarters)*, and *[Greenwall Cave](#Greenwall_Cave)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Riften if you first clear it of bandits (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Imperial)")**: Take Fort Greenwall for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Greenwall_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Greenwall (Stormcloaks)")**: Reclaim this fort for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Walkthrough

Both the exterior and interiors are significantly different depending on whether the fort is held by bandits or soldiers.

#### When Held by Bandits

The fort straddles the road from Riften to Windhelm, with barricades in front of arches that lead through the fort's courtyard. There are up to seven [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") patrolling the walls of the fort, including one at the top of the tower. Most are archers carrying daggers for melee fighting. There is a large covered well in the courtyard, which serves as an entrance to *[Greenwall Cave](#Greenwall_Cave)*. On the ground level at the southwestern end of the fort is a covered [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") area with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench"). Just northeast of the forge is a stable for a single [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). To the left of the stable is a wooden flight of stairs up to the top of the wall. From there, heading southwest brings you to the main entrance to *[Fort Greenwall Captain's Quarters](#Fort_Greenwall_Captain.27s_Quarters)*. There is also a wooden scaffold with stairs up to the area above the quarters, where a trapdoor with a leveled lock can be found. From there, there is a bridge that leads to the top of the tower, which features a campfire with a pot hanging over it and a single bandit.

To the right of the forge area is a door opening into *[Fort Greenwall Prison](#Fort_Greenwall_Prison)*, while to the northeast is an entrance to *[Fort Greenwall](#Fort_Greenwall)*. There are stone stairs up to the top of the wall to the left of this entrance. To the left from the top of the stairs is the bottom of the tower, which has a bucket containing a few [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") and a typical spiral stairwell leading up to the roof previously visited. To the right from the top of the stairs is a second entrance to *Fort Greenwall*, with a wooden lookout tower above.

#### When Held by Soldiers

The fort straddles the road from Riften to Windhelm, with barricades in front of arches that lead through the fort's courtyard. There are a total of three [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") or seven [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") patrolling the walls of the fort. Unless you have joined their side, they will warn you several times to move on and that you are trespassing before growing tired of your presence and attacking. There is a large covered well in the courtyard, which serves as an entrance to *[Greenwall Cave](#Greenwall_Cave)*. On the ground level at the southwestern end of the fort is a covered [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") area with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") holding an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). Just northeast of the forge is a stable with a single [horse](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse "Skyrim:Horse"). To the left of the stable is a wooden flight of stairs up to the top of the wall. From there, heading southwest brings you to the main entrance to *[Fort Greenwall Captain's Quarters](#Fort_Greenwall_Captain.27s_Quarters)*. There is also a wooden scaffold with stairs up to the area above the quarters, where a trapdoor with a leveled lock can be found. From there, there is a bridge that leads to the top of the tower, which features a campfire with a pot hanging over it.

To the right of the forge area is a door opening into *[Fort Greenwall Prison](#Fort_Greenwall_Prison)*, while to the northeast is an entrance to *[Fort Greenwall](#Fort_Greenwall)*. There are stone stairs up to the top of the wall to the left this entrance. To the left from the top of the stairs is the bottom of the tower, which has a bucket containing a few [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") and a typical spiral stairwell leading up to the roof previously visited. To the right from the top of the stairs is a second entrance to *Fort Greenwall*, with a wooden lookout tower above.

#### When Held by Bandits

When the bandits hold the fort, the ground level entrance leads down some stairs into a room with a single bandit standing behind a pillar. There are exits to the northeast, southwest, and down a flight of stairs against the northwest wall. There are six empty weapon racks on your right when entering. The center of the room has two carts, sacks, barrels, and an empty chest along with the bodies of two dead [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit"), all in a heap. Against the southeast wall are two sets of shelves holding two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). To the northeast is a cage containing the body of an [alchemist](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemist "Skyrim:Alchemist") and a [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poisons "Skyrim:Poisons"). In the northern corner is an apprentice-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"). Beside the stairs against the north wall is a table holding a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and a brazier on a stand with two [baked potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") cooking on top.

To the southwest is an area with a single bandit either working at a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") or standing around complaining to themselves. Next to the grindstone is a row of twelve empty weapon racks. Against the rear wall is a table holding four quivers of iron arrows, a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow"), and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). To the northwest are two practice areas, one with two archery targets and a practice dummy, and the other with a practice dummy and three more empty weapon racks.

The stairs against the northwest wall lead down to a large kitchen and storeroom, with a bandit standing beside a pillar in the middle. On the left as you enter are two stacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, with several wheels of cheese among the first stack, and baskets of [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") among the second stack. On the right is a rack holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding clutter, with a wall-mounted cage to the left containing a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a piece of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), a piece of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). Farther to the left on this wall is a sideboard holding two bottles of Nord mead. In the eastern corner is a large fireplace, with a dead [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton_(dead) "Skyrim:Breton (dead)") lying in front of it, and two burnt corpses on the fire that can be looted. There are bones littering the floor, and two more sets of shelves around the room.

To the northeast from the main room is a corridor with a small empty room to the left, and a set of empty shelves opposite. A doorway to the north leads into a circular room, with a single bandit standing around. In the center is a campfire, with a pair of pots hanging over it. One of the pots contains a random [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). There are two empty sets of shelves against the southwest wall, an unowned hay pile to the northwest, and a third set of shelves to the north holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), an iron dagger, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). There is a second unowned hay pile against the east wall.

To the northeast in the corridor outside this room is a flight of wide stone stairs spiraling up, with a bandit patrolling up and down them. At the top, against the outer wall is a row of four empty weapon racks. A doorway to the southwest leads into a room with a campfire in the middle and wooden benches against the side walls. There is a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), a drum, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") by the benches. To the southwest is a wooden door leading back outside. The door brings you out at the northeastern end of the fort, beneath a wooden lookout tower.

#### When Held by Soldiers

When the soldiers hold the fort, the ground level entrance leads down some stairs into a large dining room filled with several wooden tables and benches and two sets of shelves. Between the tables and shelves there are a total of four bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), three bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), three portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a salt pile, and several pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). On the southeast wall, at the bottom of the entrance stairs is a row of six weapon racks holding [long bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") if the fort is held by the Stormcloaks or [Imperial bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Bow "Skyrim:Imperial Bow") if the fort is held by the Legion. There are exits to the northeast, southwest, and down a flight of stairs against the northwest wall.

To the southwest is an area with a single soldier working on the [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"). Against the rear wall is a table holding four quivers of iron arrows and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). To the northwest are two practice areas, one with two archery targets, and the other with a practice dummy. There are a total of nine weapon racks in this area holding several long bows or Imperial bows and a selection of [iron weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Weapons "Skyrim:Iron Weapons") or [Imperial swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). There are two food sacks on the floor in the middle of the room.

The stairs against the northwest wall lead down to a large kitchen and storeroom. On the left as you enter are two stacks of [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels, with several wheels of cheese among the first stack, and baskets of [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") among the second stack. On the right is a rack holding two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding clutter, with a wall-mounted cage to the left containing a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"), a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), a piece of [giant lichen](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Lichen "Skyrim:Giant Lichen"), a piece of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a sprig of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), and a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"). To the left of the wall cage, hanging from the ceiling is a bunch of [dried elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Dried_Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Dried Elves Ear"). Farther to the left on this wall is a sideboard holding two bottles of Nord mead. There are two garlic braids and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") hanging from the ceiling by the southeast wall and by a pillar in the center of the room. In the eastern corner is a large fireplace, with two pots hanging in front holding two baked potatoes. By the pillar, the sideboard holds two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, several pieces of bread, and a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")*.

To the northeast from the main room is a corridor with a small empty room to the left, and a set of shelves opposite holding a selection of [Stormcloak helmets](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Helmet "Skyrim:Stormcloak Helmet"), [fur boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Boots "Skyrim:Fur Boots"), and [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Fur_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Fur Gauntlets"), or [Imperial armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Armor "Skyrim:Imperial Armor"). A doorway to the north leads into a room which has partially caved in, and is a dormitory with eight soldiers sleeping in unowned single beds. There are two sets of shelves against the southwest wall that hold pieces of the relevant faction [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor"). A third set of shelves holds a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), an iron dagger, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"). There is also a wooden table and chairs, a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack"), and two [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"); one chest has a leveled lock and is partially buried under rubble, while the other chest is unlocked. On the table is a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a bulb of garlic, and a piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"). Several of the beds are buried under masonry or straw, but all can be used to sleep in.

To the northeast in the corridor outside this room is a flight of wide stone stairs spiraling up. At the top, against the outer wall is a row of four more weapon racks holding a selection of [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"). A doorway to the southwest leads into a room set out as a lecture room, with a lectern facing several rows of wooden benches. On the lectern is a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), an iron dagger, and two common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books"). Among the benches are two knapsacks, a Stormcloak helmet and an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe"), or an [Imperial helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Helmet") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield"). The door brings you out at the northeastern end of the fort, beneath a wooden lookout tower.

#### When Held by Bandits

The entrance to the prison is on the ground level of the fort, at the southwestern end of the fort near the forge. Entering leads directly into an L-shaped corridor, with one corridor heading southwest and the other heading northwest. The northwest corridor leads past two sets of shelves, one holding clutter with a knapsack beside it, and the other holding a selection of pieces of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"). A wooden door to the right opens into a small storeroom that has mostly caved in, containing a row of six empty weapon racks on the wall and a few food barrels. To the southwest, the corridor has openings on the south wall where you can see down to a room below, with a flight of stone stairs at the end leading down into the room. There are two bandits in this room patrolling up and down a further flight of stairs. To the left beneath the openings is a set of shelves holding ragged clothes and footwraps for the prisoners.

At the bottom of the stairs to the northeast, there are multiple layers of thick cobwebs that need to be hacked or burnt through. There are three [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider") in the corridor at the bottom. At the northwestern end of the corridor is a level-locked door that opens into a small room containing an unlocked chest, an empty set of shelves, and a set of working shackles on the floor. The corridor continues to the southeast passing the prison cells, which are laid out down the corridor three to each side. All apart from one contain bedrolls, while the first cell on the left has a single bed and a table and chair, presumably for a higher class of prisoner. Some of the cells are blocked by more thick cobwebs, and there are several unlootable egg sacs along the corridor. At the far end of the corridor is a dead bandit and a couple of unlootable desiccated corpses on the ground. The end room on the right contains another dead bandit, and doesn't seem to be a cell, as there is no cell door. The room is littered with human bones and unlootable egg sacs.

Returning upstairs and passing the room leading to the cells, on the southeast wall is another row of six empty weapon racks. The corridor turns here and climbs a flight of stairs to the northeast. At the top is a wooden door leading to *Fort Greenwall Captain's Quarters*.

#### When Held by Soldiers

The entrance to the prison is on the ground level of the fort, at the southwestern end of the fort near the forge. Entering leads directly into an L-shaped corridor, with one corridor heading southwest and the other heading northwest. The northwest corridor leads past two sets of shelves, one holding clutter with a knapsack beside it, and the other holding a selection of pieces of iron armor. A wooden door to the right opens into a small storeroom that has mostly caved in, containing a row of six empty weapon racks on the wall and a few food barrels. To the southwest, the corridor has openings on the south wall where you can see down to a room below, with a flight of stone stairs at the end leading down into the room. There is a soldier sitting at a table in this room. On the table is a baked potato, and behind the table on a stone shelf on the northwest wall, beneath the openings, are four common books, a small coin purse, and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"). To the left beneath the openings is a set of shelves holding ragged clothes and footwraps for the prisoners.

At the bottom of the stairs to the northeast, there may be another soldier. At the northwestern end of the corridor is an adept-locked door that opens into a small room containing an unlocked chest, an empty set of shelves, and a set of working shackles on the floor. The corridor continues to the southeast passing the prison cells, which are laid out down the corridor three to each side. All apart from one contain bedrolls, while the first cell on the left has a single bed and a table and chair, presumably for a higher class of prisoner. The end room on the right seems to be a torture chamber instead of a cell, as there is no cell door. The room contains a chair in the center soaked in blood along with the floor. On the chair are a couple [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips") and an iron dagger. The room is littered with human bones, and has a headman's block with a woodcutter's axe beside it next to the wall.

Returning upstairs and passing the room leading to the cells, on the southeast wall is another row of six empty weapon racks. The corridor turns here and climbs a flight of stairs to the northeast. At the top is a wooden door leading to *Fort Greenwall Captain's Quarters*.

#### When Held by Bandits

There are three entrances to the captain's quarters: a door and a trapdoor from outside, and the entrance from the prison. The main door is above the covered forge area in the courtyard. It leads into a corridor to the left of the entrance from the prison, which is down a ramp to the right. The zone contains a bandit chief and possibly one other bandit. Around the corner to the northwest is a corridor with two sets of shelves holding four common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") and five bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and a dresser with a [Shrine of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrines") and an iron dagger on top. At the end is an area with a large fireplace, a ladder leading to a trapdoor with a leveled lock, an unowned single bed, and a set of shelves holding five common books and a random [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"). On the floor by the bed is a woodcutter's axe. To the northeast is a small room containing an unlocked boss chest, with a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")* on the floor. To the left of the chest is a table holding a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat"), two loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a medium coin purse. To the right, against the southeast wall is a narrow table holding a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") and five more loose septims.

#### When Held by Soldiers

There are three entrances to the captain's quarters: a door and a trapdoor from outside, and the entrance from the prison. The main door is above the covered forge area in the courtyard. It leads into a corridor to the left of the entrance from the prison, which is down a ramp to the right. Around the corner to the northwest is a corridor with two sets of shelves and a dresser holding a total of six bottles of wine, an iron dagger, four common books, and several items of clutter. The walls are decorated with the relevant faction banners. At the end is an area with a large fireplace, a ladder leading to a trapdoor with a leveled lock, and a table holding a tactical map of [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") showing the current progress of the civil war, a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), and several common books. On the floor by the fire is an iron battleaxe and a woodcutter's axe. The commander will either be sitting at this table studying the map or sleeping in a room to the northeast. The bedroom contains a large double bed, with an end table to the left holding a small coin purse and two loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). A set of shelves to the left of the bed holds a set of [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes"), a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots"), a couple pairs of random [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Gauntlets "Skyrim:Gauntlets"), two common books, and a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Mace Etiquette](/wiki/Skyrim:Mace_Etiquette "Skyrim:Mace Etiquette")*. A dresser to the right of the bed holds five more loose septims and contains a selection of clothes inside. Behind the door is an unlocked boss chest.}}

### Greenwall Cave

Entrance to Greenwall Cave

Greenwall Cave

Greenwall Cave, which is not connected to any of the fort's three interior zones, is accessible from the fort's exterior area. There is one entrance inside the fort's walls (the covered well), and one outside. The cave is a good source of [glowing mushrooms](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"). The entrance via the well is down a ladder.

Underwater below the well, there is the [corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpse "Skyrim:Corpse") of a soldier, a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter "Skyrim:Letter") which explains who he was, two bottles of alto wine, three bottles of wine, six bottles of Nord mead, and an unlocked chest. If you wait long enough within the cave, the corpse will slowly float to the surface. A [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(creature) "Skyrim:Salmon (creature)") can be found swimming in the deep water here. To the northeast is a gate with a leveled lock, which leads to a descending path and partially flooded tunnel ending at the second entrance. This entrance is northeast of the fort.

## Notes

- To the east of Greenwall Cave's main entrance (the one exterior to the fort), there is a caged [wolf](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf "Skyrim:Wolf"). When freed, two [Trappers](/wiki/Skyrim:Trapper "Skyrim:Trapper") will proceed to attack you, with the wolf siding with you against them. If the wolf manages to survive the fight, it will be friendly, and will remain in the cage area.
- During the related Civil War quest, there will be many more soldiers.
- Fort Greenwall also [appears](/wiki/Online:Fort_Greenwall "Online:Fort Greenwall") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- On the left edge of the fireplace is the tip and bottom of the handle of a second iron battleaxe (as if it is under the fireplace), but you are unable to interact with it. **?**
- If you clear the fort of bandits prior to starting the Civil War questline, when the fort respawns, the interior items and room content will change to those as if the fort were occupied by Stormcloaks, but there are no soldiers either inside or outside the fort. Only a single horse will appear near the stable. **?**

Fort Greymoor

**Fort Greymoor** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Greymoor](#Fort_Greymoor)* and *[Fort Greymoor Prison](#Fort_Greymoor_Prison)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Whiterun if you first clear it of bandits (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Related Quests

- **[Kill Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis")**: Kill [Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Agnis "Skyrim:Agnis") in Fort Greymoor.

### Exterior

The fort is crumbling and part of the missing sections of wall have been replaced by log palisades. The main entrance to the courtyard is past two rows of barricades arranged in half circles around the arch forming the entrance from the southeast. To the left of the entrance when viewed from outside of the fort is a small cage hanging from a beam; it contains a dead [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). You can loot this bandit either by standing under and jumping or by dropping from above. There are two bandits on guard on the wall over the entrance with three more spread around the walls and courtyard.

There are practice dummies set up to imitate guards on the walls around the outer wall of the fort.

There are two stables near where the eastern tower used to stand and between the first of these and the wall is an unlocked chest. To the north of the stables is a wooden hut with a blacksmith's [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") and [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") inside and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") on the side next to a wagon wheel. In front of the forge is a log table with a pile of firewood underneath. Opposite the arched entrance is a short flight of stairs up to a raised area with a set of wooden double doors leading to the interior of the fort. There is a fire to the left and a couple of barrels in the corner farther to the left. To the right is a boarded over well. To the left of the northern tower is a double flight of wooden stairs up to another wall connecting this tower with another to the west. There is a doorway leading inside where there is a fire with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") and a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") next to it and a crate with two loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. There are barrels, crates and a sack in this area as well as an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the right of the second doorway. The second doorway leads to the top of the main part of the fort.

On your right is a flight of stairs up to the top of another tower. A bandit is on guard here and a small round table and chair. On the table is a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") and a couple of coins that may have fallen to the floor. A dummy is holding a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") that can taken.

Continuing along the top of the main part of the fort, there is a trapdoor entrance behind some rubble by a large wooden structure leading up to a lookout platform. There is a second flight of stairs back down to a barrel containing ingredients with a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") lying on the ground. Heading southeast along the wall, there are stairs down and up, past another dummy guard to the tower in the southern corner of the fort. There is another trapdoor here that leads into the prison. This completes the circuit of the outer wall of the fort.

### Fort Greymoor

A

B

C

D

E

F

G

Fort Greymoor

Entering through the main double doors (**E** on map) will bring you straight to a crossroads with rooms to the southwest, northwest and northeast. To the southwest is a dining room with four long wooden tables holding three bottles of Nord mead, three [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), and a [goat cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). There is a large fireplace to the north of the room with a copy of *[Argonian Account, Book 1](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian_Account,_Book_1 "Skyrim:Argonian Account, Book 1")* on the floor and an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") on the mantle over the fire. To the southeast is a short corridor leading to an unlocked wooden door to *[Fort Greymoor Prison](#Fort_Greymoor_Prison)* (**F** on map); there is an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks") on the floor here. To the left of the door are some small cages, and a couple of barrels are to the right. To the south of the dining room is an opening to a wide spiraling stairway leading up to the right. On your left is an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") on the floor, with an iron helmet nearby. At the top of the stairway there is a circular room above the dining room. A bandit wanders here, and three practice dummies are set up around the room. To the northeast is a ladder to a trapdoor in the ceiling leading outside (**G** on map), and directly opposite against the wall is an unlocked boss chest (**B** on map). To the southeast is an open door leading to a bedroom with a [corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Corpse "Skyrim:Corpse") of an Imperial soldier, and between the door and ladder is a lectern holding a copy of the [Light Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Light_Armor "Skyrim:Light Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Rislav The Righteous](/wiki/Skyrim:Rislav_The_Righteous "Skyrim:Rislav The Righteous")* (**C** on map).

Inside the bedroom are an empty sideboard and table, an unowned double bed, and a bookcase containing a [red apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), a random pair of boots, and copies of *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*, *[Brief History of the Empire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v2 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v2")*, *[The Wolf Queen, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v3 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v3")*, *[A Dance in Fire, v4](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v4 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v4")*, *[The Song of Pelinal, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v2 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v2")*, and *[The Hope of the Redoran](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Hope_of_the_Redoran "Skyrim:The Hope of the Redoran")*.

The short corridor to the northwest from the main entrance has twelve weapon racks, with six on each side holding two iron swords and two [Imperial swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Sword "Skyrim:Imperial Sword"). This leads to a room dominated by a large cage containing two burnt corpses; a magic-using bandit is looking at a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") on a table to your left as you enter. Under the table is a novice-locked chest. Behind the cage is a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), and on a table against the wall to the northwest are a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a random [regeneration potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"), a small coin purse, four loose coins, and a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick").

Through a doorway to the west are what appears to be the latrines, with three stalls with loose stone walls between each. On one of these walls is an [Imperial light helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Light_Helmet "Skyrim:Imperial Light Helmet"). There is a wide flight of stairs spiraling down opposite. At the bottom through a doorway is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that activates a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap. In the room behind are a dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever") and a short corridor heading to the northwest, which leads to a corridor being used as a storage area with two more dead skeevers and three [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") scattered on the ground. On your left are two sets of shelves containing seven sacks, a pair of leather boots, a [potion of the defender](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Defender "Skyrim:Potion of the Defender"), a [potion of the warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Warrior "Skyrim:Potion of the Warrior"), and a [potion of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), with two more sacks between the two sets of shelves. Straight ahead is a partially flooded corridor leading to a sewer pipe and exit that leads outside (**D** on map) to the northwest of the fort.

On your right is a platform with barrels and an adept-locked chest underneath. There are four more sets of shelves on top of the platform containing a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [wolf pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Wolf_Pelt "Skyrim:Wolf Pelt"), three sacks, a small coin purse, two [woodcutter's axes](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), ten bottles of Nord mead, a pair of leather boots, and a lockpick. There are four more bottles of Nord mead on the ground beside them. To the left of the platform is a doorway to wide spiraling stairs leading up, and to the left of this is a firewood pile with a woodcutter's axe on a wooden block.

There is a bandit patrolling these stairs and a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer") found partway up. At the top are several straw bales and a doorway into the kitchen area. The corridor to the northeast of the main entrance leads to the same kitchen area, with a bandit guard and [Agnis](/wiki/Skyrim:Agnis "Skyrim:Agnis") (**A** on map) if you are here for the relevant [quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_Agnis "Skyrim:Kill Agnis"). On your left as you enter this room is a large fireplace with a spit hanging in front of it with three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") in a pot on the spit. To the right is a door to a storage room with three sets of shelves containing a random [illusion potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Potion of Illusion"), a random [healer potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Healer "Skyrim:Potion of the Healer"), a random [enhanced stamina potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Enhanced Stamina"), and a potion of minor healing. In the center of the kitchen are two long wooden tables laid end to end with a whole [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)"), an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), and four pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"). To the southeast is a door leading to a bedroom with a single bed, a dresser with a copy of *[A Dance in Fire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v1 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v1")*, and a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") on a wooden plate on top. To the right is a table with a practice dummy and iron dagger. Against the southeast wall is a bookcase containing a random strength potion and copies of *[Brief History of the Empire, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Brief_History_of_the_Empire,_v1 "Skyrim:Brief History of the Empire, v1")*, *[Beggar Prince](/wiki/Skyrim:Beggar_Prince "Skyrim:Beggar Prince")*, *[The Song of Pelinal, v6](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Song_of_Pelinal,_v6 "Skyrim:The Song of Pelinal, v6")*, *[The Monomyth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Monomyth "Skyrim:The Monomyth")*, and *The Wolf Queen, v3*.

### Fort Greymoor Prison

A

B

C

Fort Greymoor Prison

You enter into a circular room with a bear trap right by the door (**B** on map). There are several small cages and one larger apprentice-locked cage. Inside the cage are a dead [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") and a [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") on a wooden plate. There is a long wooden table in the center of the room with a bottle of wine, an iron dagger, and a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") in a wooden bowl on the table. To the northwest is a door to *[Fort Greymoor](#Fort_Greymoor)* (**A** on map) with a pair of random boots beside it. On the west side of the room is a ladder to the trapdoor in the ceiling that leads to the top of the tower (**C** on map). At the rear of the room is an opening leading to a wide spiraling stone stairway with a bandit patrolling up and down. To the right of the opening is a small round wooden table with a medium coin purse, two loose coins, and an iron dagger on top.

You can hear a bandit talking to themselves at the bottom of the stairs. Through a doorway there are a set of shelves full of worthless clothing and a doorway to the northeast to the cells. There are six cells all containing bedrolls, three on each side of a central corridor. On the left, the first is unlocked with a dead hunter inside, and the second and third are empty. On the right, the first is empty, the second is novice-locked and has a dead [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") inside, and the third is master-locked, but contains nothing. The corridor then turns to the east, where there is a bandit with their back to you inspecting a dead [troll](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll") on a table. Be careful to avoid the [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling. On the table with the troll are an iron dagger, two lockpicks, and a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"). Under the table is a bear trap, and to the left is an unlocked chest. In the northern corner are two small empty cages hanging from the ceiling. In the middle of the northeast wall at head height is a level-locked chest on the wall containing a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and leveled poison.

## Notes

- After clearing the fort of bandits, the exterior chests will be disabled when you leave the area.
- If you have cleared the fort of bandits but have not completed the quest [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun") for the Imperials or Stormcloaks, only the external bandits will respawn. The interior will respawn, but not the bandits.
- If you have cleared the fort of bandits and have completed the quest Battle for Whiterun, the Imperial or Stormcloak soldiers will not be hostile toward you.
- Many internal names and an unused key indicate the fort was originally known as **Fort Blackmoor**, which appears in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")* as the village [Black Moor](/wiki/Arena:Black_Moor "Arena:Black Moor").

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.

# Skyrim:Fort Hraggstad

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Fort Hraggstad ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Hraggstad)) | | |
| # of Zones | 2 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"); either [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") | |

Fort Hraggstad

**Fort Hraggstad** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Hraggstad](#Fort_Hraggstad)* and *[Fort Hraggstad Prison](#Fort_Hraggstad_Prison)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") if you first clear it of bandits and/or complete the quest [Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion") (see [bugs](#Bugs)).

## Related Quests

- **[Joining the Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Joining_the_Legion "Skyrim:Joining the Legion")**: Prove yourself worthy to join the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[The Battle for Fort Hraggstad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Hraggstad")**: Prepare for the final assault on [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") by taking this fort for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").
- **[More Than You Can Chew](/wiki/Skyrim:More_Than_You_Can_Chew "Skyrim:More Than You Can Chew")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Netch Leather Armor"): Obtain the secrets of crafting with [netch leather](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather "Skyrim:Netch Leather") from a tribe of [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling").

### Exterior

The sizable courtyard and walls are patrolled by up to seven [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). A [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") is along the southwestern wall, with an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to its left. On your right as you pass the arch into the courtyard is an empty stable, with several food barrels found around the courtyard. On top of the two intact towers are random, possibly enchanted [bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") and quivers of [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") on tables, with the top of the tallest tower also having a [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow").

### Fort Hraggstad

As soon as you enter, unless your sneak skill is very high, you are likely to be confronted by a lone bandit in the first room, standing in front of the fireplace directly opposite the entrance. However, even the sounds from a loud battle with him are unlikely to reach the ears of the next bandit upstairs, so you can generally deal with the two bandits one at a time. To the left of the fireplace is a cupboard holding clutter, a garlic bulb in a wooden bowl, and three common books, while leaning against the fireplace is a woodcutter's axe. To the right of the fireplace is a doorway leading further into the fort, and in the northeast corner is a wooden table with [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), helmet, [sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), and battleaxe all on top.

With the [Netch Leather Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Netch_Leather_Armor "Skyrim:Netch Leather Armor") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, there is an additional locked chest here which can only be opened with a key obtainable during the quest [More Than You Can Chew](/wiki/Skyrim:More_Than_You_Can_Chew "Skyrim:More Than You Can Chew").

Through the doorway is a cart at the bottom of a flight of stairs, containing an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"), a long bow, iron gauntlets, and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"). Climbing the stairs leads to a large room, with a bandit leaning against the wall, and the [bandit chief](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit_Chief "Skyrim:Bandit Chief") at the back of the room in an area being used as sleeping quarters. The front half of the room is being used for storage, with several food barrels under a wooden structure in the northwestern corner. On this structure is an adept-locked chest and a small wooden table holding three potions of minor healing and some foodstuffs. Against the north wall are two sets of shelves containing three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), some food, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), an iron sword, and eight common books. Opposite the shelves is another wooden structure, with a food barrel and a table holding a small mead barrel and three potatoes.

There is a raised section in the middle of the room with a small wooden table holding two bottles of wine. Against the south wall is a single bed and a dresser. On the dresser are three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a bulb of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), and some bread and cheese. In front of this is an end table with a gourd on top, and against the north wall is another single bed and another table with a [leg of goat roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat_Roast "Skyrim:Leg of Goat Roast") and a loaf of bread on top.

The western end of the room contains four more single beds, an unlocked chest, and a table holding a tactical map of Skyrim which the bandit chief was studying, a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes"), a garlic bulb, a gourd, an iron helmet, and a copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Gold Ribbon of Merit](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Gold_Ribbon_of_Merit "Skyrim:The Gold Ribbon of Merit")*. Against the north wall, between two of the beds, is a cupboard holding an iron helmet. Between the other two beds against the southern wall are an end table and a table with a set of iron armor, iron gauntlets, and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") on top, while leaning against the end table is an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword"), with a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") next to the nearest bed. None of the beds in the fort are owned.

### Fort Hraggstad Prison

Upon entering, you are in a room with a bandit roaming about and a second bandit sitting at a table to the left. On the table is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"). There are a couple wooden benches and a set of shelves holding only clutter behind the table, with a [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") on top of the shelves. Against the northeast wall, almost opposite the entrance, is a second set of shelves holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"), [iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") or [banded iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Banded Iron Armor"), [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"), and an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet"). There is a door leading downstairs in the southeast corner.

At the bottom of the stairs is a room containing a set of shelves full of more clutter against the northeast wall, and a small wooden table in the southeast corner with a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") on top. To the southwest are stairs down to the cells, which are guarded by another bandit. There are a total of seven cells, with four against the southwest wall, and three against the northeast wall. All of the cells are empty and unlocked. On your left is a table holding an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") and a common book. Behind the table is a chair, and against the southeast wall is an unlocked chest to the right of two sets of shelves holding several pieces of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese as well as clutter.

## Notes

- Earlier in the game's development, the quest [Dragon Rising](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Rising "Skyrim:Dragon Rising") was tied to the factions of the Civil War, and you seemingly chose a side before you could first encounter dragons. If you chose the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") would send you with [Captain Metilius](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Metilius "Skyrim:Captain Metilius") to investigate reports of a dragon at Fort Hraggstad. If you instead joined the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"), [Ulfric](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") would send you along with someone named Sifnar (this person might have been [Sifnar Ironkettle](/wiki/Skyrim:Sifnar_Ironkettle "Skyrim:Sifnar Ironkettle"), but the latter may have been named after the former) to investigate a similar disturbance at [Fort Amol](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Amol "Skyrim:Fort Amol"). Little evidence of this remains in the game's files, with only a few markers (`MQ104FortHraggstadMoveToMarker`), AI packages, and leftover scripts (`MQ104Script`) still referring to this iteration. The DialogueViews files hold dialogue for General Tullius and Captain Metilius that are not viewable in the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit") in the final game's files.

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- The exterior weapons and the bandit chest aren't properly linked to enable their parent markers.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Fort Kastav

## Overview

Fort Kastav

**Fort Kastav** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") south of [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold") initially occupied by [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Kastav Prison](#Fort_Kastav_Prison)* and *[Fort Kastav Captain's Quarters](#Fort_Kastav_Captain.27s_Quarters)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Winterhold if you first clear it of warlocks and skeletons.

## Related Quests

- **[Rescue from Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Kastav")**: Take Fort Kastav for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and rescue the prisoners within. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Kastav](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Kastav "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Kastav")**: Reclaim this fort for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

Fort Kastav is situated in a mountain pass which it spans almost completely, leaving only enough room for the [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun")-Winterhold road. The exterior of the fort is quite impressive, making use of the natural features of the mountain, and boasting many lookout platforms and an extensive ramp system. Skeletons patrol the walls, and another skeleton watches from a lookout post, while two powerful mages will emerge and attack if the skeletons raise the alarm. When approaching from the road, either use the main entrance into the grounds for a direct assault, or the platform ramps in the eastern corner for a more stealthy approach. Once inside the walls, find a small shed that contains an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") and a potion.

The prison section is on the ground level of the fort, and the Captain's Quarters are on the second level; each has a main door entry. The fort boasts a tower that forms a third level, which can be accessed via a ladder in the Captain's Quarters or by jumping up the nearby mountain slope. The prison can also be accessed via a trapdoor outside the fort, by a snowy ledge near the western wall.

### Fort Kastav Prison

If entering the prison through the main doors, you will begin on a staircase landing guarded by a [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). The landing extends onto wings to the right and left, but holds nothing of value. Down the stairs is the lobby and an illuminated area with a table, shelves, and an unlocked chest. The shelf holds a potion and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). A [Fort Kastav Prison key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Kastav_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Fort Kastav Prison Key") is on the table. Across from the table is another shelf holding assorted weaponry, and a leveled weapon is on the adjacent weapons rack.

The double wooden doors to the left of the table lead down to the main prison area, where a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and a skeleton are waiting. The guard's area is on the upper level, and provides a view from above into each prisoners' cell below. There are five prisoner cells at the bottom of the stairs, and each is opened with the prison key. However, there is little of note in the cell area, aside from the style of the prison cells themselves, and a serving of dog meat in each. Rather, explore the guard's area. The shelf immediately to the left of the doors contains a potion and various alchemy ingredients. An unlocked chest is on the far side of the room on the south wall. A second fort prison key can be found on the table, or on the floor after becoming displaced by the necromancer.

Back in the lobby, the open storage room on the west wall features a weapon on a weapon plaque mounted to the right of a door. The door leads to a ladder back up to the exterior of the fort. Exiting here will place you just outside the fort to the southwest, overlooking the main road. There is no access to the Captain's Quarters from the prison.

### Fort Kastav Captain's Quarters

From the main doors into the Captain's Quarters, you will see a table with a bottle each of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and a shelf with a selection of [goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel") and [eidar](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel") cheeses. The ruined storage area at the bottom of the stairs holds an unlocked chest, but little else of note. To the left of the main doors is a raised area serving as the captain's bedroom. Here you will find a small table with a [scroll of Conjure Frost Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Frost_Atronach "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Frost Atronach") and an apothecary's satchel. An unlocked chest is at the foot of the bed, and an end table holds a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(book) "Skyrim:Warrior (book)")*. A ladder next to the bed leads up and out to the fort's tower. A sacrificial altar is on the tower, and holds a dagger, a [scroll of Conjure Familiar](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Conjure_Familiar "Skyrim:Scroll of Conjure Familiar"), a sample each of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts") and [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), and a bowl containing some loose gold, a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg"), and a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower.

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [warlocks](/wiki/Skyrim:Warlock "Skyrim:Warlock") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- The trapdoor on the tower leading from the Captain's Quarters appears to be levitating.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

Fort Neugrad

**Fort Neugrad** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Falkreath](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath "Skyrim:Falkreath") initially occupied by [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Neugrad](#Fort_Neugrad)* and *[Fort Neugrad Prison](#Fort_Neugrad_Prison)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Falkreath if you first clear it of bandits.

## Related Quests

- **[Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad")**: Rescue [Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") soldiers from the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") and capture the fort. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Neugrad")**: Retake Fort Neugrad for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

After the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") gain control of the fort, the walls and fortifications will be repaired, a stable and [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge") area will be built in the courtyard, and a new selection of chests will be scattered about.

### Fort Neugrad

While the bandits occupy the fort, a boss-level bandit leader will be waiting in the southeast room upstairs. He will ignore you until you open his door. He holds a [Fort Neugrad library key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad_Library_Key "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad Library Key"), which opens an otherwise pickable lock on the south side of the dining hall downstairs. Inside is a hostile mage by the name of [Brandish](/wiki/Skyrim:Brandish "Skyrim:Brandish").

After the Imperials or Stormcloaks gain control of the fort, the interior will be partially renovated to show the occupation, and a new selection of chests will be scattered about, replacing the previous bandit boss chests.

Regardless of faction ownership of the fort:

- In the room downstairs you can find a copy of *[Jornibret's Last Dance](/wiki/Skyrim:Jornibret%27s_Last_Dance "Skyrim:Jornibret's Last Dance")*
- Upstairs, in the commander's room to the southeast, you can find a copy of *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")*
- Two chests with adept-level locks
- A variety of items, styled after the current residents of the fort (bandits or Imperial soldiers)

### Fort Neugrad Prison

While the bandits occupy the fort, there are no prison cells in the area, but only wine barrels and shelves containing clutter.

After the Imperials or Stormcloaks gain control of the fort, the lowest level of the prison will have some cells to hold prisoners of the opposite faction.

Regardless of faction ownership of the fort:

- There is an adept-locked chest in the water close to the southeast entrance
- In the room after descending the stairs but before descending down to the prison cells, there is an apprentice-locked chest behind the shelves to your right as you leave the room
- In the prison room, you can find a copy of *An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim*
- In the prison room during the quest [Rescue from Fort Neugrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Rescue_from_Fort_Neugrad "Skyrim:Rescue from Fort Neugrad"), the [Fort Neugrad Prison key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad Prison Key") is on a barrel close to the passage from the prison room into the caves

## Notes

- The nearby lake contains a hidden entrance into the prison. Just outside this underwater entrance, there is a half-overturned sunken rowboat with a treasure chest inside.
- The upstairs exit from the fort to the tower on top contains a locked chest with a [treasure map](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Neugrad_Treasure_Map "Skyrim:Fort Neugrad Treasure Map") inside; the treasure is across the lake, behind some rocks [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Neugrad+Treasure+Chest&zoom=16&legacy=true). Going clockwise around the lake from there also nets you two [gold ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein").
- The Imperial or Stormcloak garrison will react to you as a trespasser inside the fort and prison unless you are a member of their faction, but as long as you keep moving, you'll be free to loot items without consequence. However, if you are allied with the faction controlling the fort, you can get rest, food, and a borrowable horse in the fort.

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  -  The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- The chest referred to in the treasure map is sometimes absent; reading the map should spawn the chest, but does not. This bug is most likely due to the scripting errors in [version 1.2](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.2 "Skyrim:Patch") of the official patch.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.3, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Fort Neugrad
- 

  Fort Neugrad Prison

# Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk

## Overview
