Fort Snowhawk

**Fort Snowhawk** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") west of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") initially occupied by [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains two zones: *[Fort Snowhawk](#Fort_Snowhawk)* and *[Fort Snowhawk Prison](#Fort_Snowhawk_Prison)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Morthal if you first clear it of necromancers and skeletons.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Imperial)")**: Retake Fort Snowhawk for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Snowhawk_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Snowhawk (Stormcloaks)")**: Take this fort for the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

The courtyards outside the fort are quite confusing, with many small interconnected areas with arches and flights of stairs leading to different levels. You can tackle this eroding stronghold in a number of ways: by storming the front gate, slipping in through the hole in the southeast wall, or leaping over any of the crumbling battlements. The main arch leading into the courtyard is to the south, with several barricades in front, and the main entrance into the fort opposite. A host of [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and their [skeletal minions](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") defend the fort's exterior. There are numerous [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels around the fort as well as a [deathbell](/wiki/Skyrim:Deathbell "Skyrim:Deathbell") and [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush growing in the courtyard and several places where the walls have crumbled that have been reinforced with wooden palisades. The western quadrant includes two gated stables, while the eastern quadrant has a covered well, with a wooden table beside it and two [long bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and a quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on top. Opposite the table are two archery targets and a practice dummy. To the left of these is the entrance to *[Fort Snowhawk Prison](#Fort_Snowhawk_Prison)* with an alternative ground-level entrance to the interior of the fort opposite. Beside the well is a flight of stairs up, with a [pressure plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate") at the top, that doesn't appear to have any effect, with a campfire and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") hanging over it nearby. There is also another table here with an [imperial shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Shield "Skyrim:Imperial Shield") on top, regardless of who controls the fort. A third entrance to the interior of the fort can be found on an upper level to the north. A ruined tower is in the northeastern corner of the fort with an expert-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") among the masonry, take care as it can be a bit tricky getting back out, especially if overencumbered. You'll need to jump onto the chest then jump out or fast travel if no enemies are around.

### Fort Snowhawk

The main entrance to the south leads into a wide passage with a wooden door opposite that is barred from the other side and stairs leading up to the left and down to the right. Care is needed when climbing the stairs to the left as there is a [frost rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Rune "Skyrim:Frost Rune") trap at the bottom of the stairs that leads to the upper entrance which is guarded by two skeletons. Beside the entrance is a cupboard with a [Scroll of Circle of Protection](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Circle_of_Protection "Skyrim:Scroll of Circle of Protection"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal") and a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") on the shelves. Beside the cupboard is a ladder to a trapdoor out on top of the main tower, there is nothing out there apart from the view. Backtracking down the stairs, to the right of the entrance is a cupboard with a random empty [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a set of [black mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Black Mage Robes"), and four common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") including *[An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:An_Explorer%27s_Guide_to_Skyrim "Skyrim:An Explorer's Guide to Skyrim")* which may add several places to your main map, unless you have already found them. By the top of the stairs leading down is a barrel of [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). At the bottom a flooded passage heads to the northeast past a junction, with a decrepit kitchen on the right and a short passage on the left that ends after a couple of paces because it has been boarded up. Ahead is a flight of stairs up to a wooden gate with a button on the right that lowers it. The kitchen contains a wardrobe, a set of shelves holding two [potions of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"). Beside the shelves is a cupboard that holds only [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"), but with a random [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe") on the floor in front. Against the side wall is a wooden table with a random [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") stabbed into it and two [charred skeever hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") on a plate on top, while hanging above are two bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"). In the eastern corner is an alcove containing an adept-locked chest.

Beyond the wooden gate is a large room containing seven unowned single beds. There are double doors opposite leading outside at ground-level opposite the entrance to the prison. There are small counters either side of the passage, with [sabre cat pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Pelt "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Pelt") on the one and a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and two bunches of dried elves ear hanging from racks over the other. There is dresser against the southeast wall with a *[Spell Tome: Candlelight](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Candlelight "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Candlelight")* on top. In the southern and western corners are stairs leading up to a balcony over the passage, with two doors leading off of it.

The lower of the two leads to a two-level room containing a level necromancer and several crafting stations. There is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") opposite the door with a small unit beside it, a counter against the northeast wall, a cupboard in the corner and a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") in front. There are stairs leading up to the upper level, where there a total of five sets of shelves, an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") and a long wooden table. On the unit, shelves and counter are a total of; two [butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing"), two [blue butterfly wings](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Blue Butterfly Wing"), a bowl of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), two [taproots](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot"), a sample of [scaly pholiota](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaly_Pholiota "Skyrim:Scaly Pholiota"), a bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton"), a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch"), a sample of [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), a sample of [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), a random potion of magicka, a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka"), two sets of black mages robes, three bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), three bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulb, a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), twenty-nine books, including a copy of *[The Aetherium Wars](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Aetherium_Wars "Skyrim:The Aetherium Wars")*, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a sprig of snowberries, several cheese wheels, an iron mace, a potion of minor healing, a potion of minor stamina, and two food sacks. On the table is a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer%27s_Letter "Skyrim:Necromancer's Letter") that explains what happened at the fort recently and where the dead [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") came from, a copy of [Fort Snowhawk quarters key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Snowhawk_Quarters_Key "Skyrim:Fort Snowhawk Quarters Key") and a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Dance in Fire, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dance_in_Fire,_v2 "Skyrim:A Dance in Fire, v2")*. There is a [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") banner hanging above the shelves even when the fort is held by the necromancers.

There is also a door to the southeast leading into a passage that leads from the other door on the previous balcony toward the southwest. The passage contains two more sets of shelves separated by a wooden table with a small unit opposite, these hold in total; four loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a sample of bleeding crown, a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), two bowls of [ectoplasm](/wiki/Skyrim:Ectoplasm "Skyrim:Ectoplasm"), a sample of [mudcrab chitin](/wiki/Skyrim:Mudcrab_Chitin "Skyrim:Mudcrab Chitin"), two bunches of lavender, a [nightshade](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightshade "Skyrim:Nightshade") flower, a bowl of bone meal and six more common books. At the end of the passage are two doors; one expert-locked in the front and an unlocked one on the left, that leads into a bedroom containing a leveled necromancer unless you've already dealt with them. The bedroom also contains an unowned double bed in the eastern corner with a wooden table to the left and an apprentice-locked chest at the foot of the bed. On the table are two deathbell flowers, a *[Spell Tome: Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tome:_Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Spell Tome: Raise Zombie")*, three common books and another copy of the Fort Snowhawk quarters key. There is a dresser and wardrobe in the room both containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and behind the door a small shelf with an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") and two pieces of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root").

Through the expert-locked door, which is opened using the key taken from the bedroom and crafting room, is a large round room with an altar in the center and the boss leveled necromancer wandering around it. There is a skeleton lying on the altar and a random [one-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:One-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:One-Handed Weapons") on the altar. An unlocked boss chest is against the wall to the southeast, with a random [warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Warhammer "Skyrim:Warhammer") beside it on the floor. There are a total of four sets of shelves around the room holding a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine, twenty-four more books, a sprig of snowberries, two random soul gems; one filled, one empty and several food sacks. To the southwest is a door barred from this side, with a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") on the floor in front. This opens opposite the main exit from the fort.

### Fort Snowhawk Prison

You may find the prison deserted. The entrance leads directly into a room that has suffered quite extensive damage from a cave-in. There are two torture racks among the masonry and behind these is a warhammer randomly chosen from a leveled list, and farther back, in an area which can be reached with a bit of jumping, is a set of shelves that have fallen flat that holds two random [potions](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), a random empty soul gem, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and some ruined books. On your right when entering is a blood-soaked table with the corpse of a bandit and a random empty soul gem on top. Beside this is a cupboard with two random soul gems; one empty, one filled, and a [scroll of Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Scroll of Raise Zombie") on the shelves and another medium coin purse hidden behind. A doorway to the northeast has an [elemental rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Traps#Elemental_Runes "Skyrim:Traps") in front of it.

Through the doorway is another blood-soaked table with a bowl of bone meal and an Orcish mace on top. Hanging above are two small cages, one contains a skeleton and the other another dead bandit, both of which can be looted. There are curved stairs leading down to the right. At the bottom is a large fireplace with an apprentice-locked chest beside it and a cupboard to the right of that holding another random empty soul gem, a random potion of magicka, a random [potion of resist element](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Resist_Fire "Skyrim:Potion of Resist Fire"), a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide") and a food sack. A long wooden table and chair are to the left of the passage leading to the cell, on top of which is a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), a random [weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"), a copy of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")* and a small coin purse. Along the passage there is an arcane enchanter in a large cell with a torture rack and masses of human bones and opposite is an empty cell. At the end of the passage another cell on the left contains an unlocked chest, a cell containing the bodies of two bandits lying on hay piles and a third cell door with a tunnel behind leading to an alternative exit. There are a number of fungi along the tunnel and a ledge that stops you from using this as an entrance. Take care dropping off the ledge as there are four [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on the lower level as well as the corpse of another bandit. There are a total of four bleeding crown, six [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") and two [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi.

## Notes

- It is very possible for the necromancers to exit an area as you're entering it or to flee from battle (via a loading screen door). In some cases, one leaves but when you follow there will be more than one.
- The main tower has three entrances. The top door contains two skeletons, the middle door (front entrance) contains a magic trap and a necromancer, and the lowest door (across from the prison door) contains a necromancer and a skeleton.
- Fort Snowhawk also [appears](/wiki/Arena:Snowhawk "Arena:Snowhawk") as a settlement in *[Arena](/wiki/Arena:Arena "Arena:Arena")*, and is mentioned in *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*. For historical information, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Snowhawk "Lore:Snowhawk").

## Bugs

- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [necromancers](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.

# Skyrim:Fort Sungard

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Fort.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Fort.png) | Military Fort: Fort Sungard ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Fort+Sungard)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Fort_Sungard "Lore:Fort Sungard")) | | |
| # of Zones | 5 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"); either [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Soldier "Skyrim:Imperial Soldier") or [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloak_Soldier "Skyrim:Stormcloak Soldier") | |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")* *[Last Scabbard of Akrash](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash")* | |

| FortSungard01, FortSungard02, FortSungard03, FortSungard04, FortSungard05 | |

Fort Sungard

**Fort Sungard** is a large [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east-southeast of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") initially occupied by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains five zones: *[Fort Sungard Muster](#Fort_Sungard_Muster)*, *[Fort Sungard Shrine](#Fort_Sungard_Shrine)*, *[Fort Sungard Annex](#Fort_Sungard_Annex)*, *[Fort Sungard Tower](#Fort_Sungard_Tower)*, and *[Fort Sungard Oubliette](#Fort_Sungard_Oubliette)*.

The fort will be taken over by whoever wins the [Civil War](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"), or by the faction currently holding Markarth if you first clear it of Forsworn.

## Related Quests

- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Imperial) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Imperial)")**: Retake Fort Sungard for the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Battle_for_Fort_Sungard_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:The Battle for Fort Sungard (Stormcloaks)")**: Take this fort in the name of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Skilled Apprenticeship](/wiki/Skyrim:Skilled_Apprenticeship "Skyrim:Skilled Apprenticeship")**: Retrieve a [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash") for [Ghorza gra-Bagol](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorza_gra-Bagol "Skyrim:Ghorza gra-Bagol").

### Exterior

The fort is strategically located atop a small mountain at the crossroads between [the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach"), [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold"), and [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold"), with the plains to the north offering the easiest approach. Initially the fort will be occupied by [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), but the building interiors are entirely free of them, making exploration easy. Although there are several stealthy and covert methods to enter the interior of this fortress, the most likely route of entrance is the exterior gate. By default, the exterior of the fortress will be teeming with Forsworn, although this will be the only location in the fort inhabited by them. The Forsworn will be replaced by soldiers of the faction currently controlling Markarth if the Forsworn are killed, or if The Reach changes hands during the civil war, it will be automatically retaken by the new regime. The route leading up to the main gate is scattered with wooden towers and defenses, and a melee warrior can easily get overwhelmed by the Forsworn here. The next tier (middle tier) of the battlements only has two defenders, who guard *[Fort Sungard Muster](#Fort_Sungard_Muster)*. The highest tier is guarded by three Forsworn. Up here there are a couple doors to *[Fort Sungard Tower](#Fort_Sungard_Tower)* and a door to *[Fort Sungard Annex](#Fort_Sungard_Annex)*. There is little loot in this area of Fort Sungard, aside from a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") to the right of the fort's main gate.

**Occupants**

- 5 leveled archer Forsworn (two are guarding the front gate, one is on the middle tier, two are on the highest tier)
- 3 leveled melee Forsworn (one is guarding the front gate, one is on the middle tier, one is on the highest tier)

### Fort Sungard Muster

The Muster is largely the living and eating quarters for the fort. The top level makes up the sleeping area, leading down into the kitchen and dining area, before ending on the lowest level in the pantry. There are three entrances into this area. The pantry exit is a small grate that allows for access between the exterior and interior of the fort's walls. The living area contains exits to the roofs and courtyard of the Fort. There is a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill book *[Last Scabbard of Akrash](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash")* on the highest level at the end of hall on a table with a few ingots. This is the copy Ghorza will point you to in the [related quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Skilled_Apprenticeship "Skyrim:Skilled Apprenticeship"). Weapon racks on either side hold assorted bows and greatswords. Leveled armor boots will appear behind the weapons, including [Creation Club](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") content depending on what has been installed. Other than that, there are only loose [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), a stray [charred skeever hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Charred_Skeever_Hide "Skyrim:Charred Skeever Hide") in the pantry, and a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot") in the kitchen on the bottom shelf of a wooden bench in the center of the room.

**Treasure**

- The [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") skill book *[Last Scabbard of Akrash](/wiki/Skyrim:Last_Scabbard_of_Akrash "Skyrim:Last Scabbard of Akrash")* on the highest level at the end of the hall on a table.
- Several chests in the sleeping area on the highest level.

**Other**

- A cooking pot in the kitchen down the stairs from the sleeping area.

### Fort Sungard Shrine

The Shrine is a small area of the fort with only two rooms. The bottom room is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with a few stray alchemy [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). The top room has a shrine. If the fort is controlled by the Forsworn, the shrine is a [Shrine of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Shrine of Kynareth"); if Imperials control the fort, it is a [Shrine of Akatosh](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Akatosh "Skyrim:Shrine of Akatosh"); if Stormcloaks control the fort, it is a [Shrine of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrines#Shrine_of_Talos "Skyrim:Shrines"). Aside from that, there is only an adept-locked strong box sitting on the hay bales near the alchemy lab.

**Treasure**

- A strong box on the haystack next to the alchemy table.

**Other**

- A shrine on the upper floor, which will be dedicated to Kynareth if Forsworn occupy the castle, Akatosh if the Imperials control the fort, or Talos if the Stormcloaks are the occupiers.
- An alchemy lab on the lower floor.

### Fort Sungard Annex

The Annex is the armory of the fort and contains a few floors with stray [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") and [weapons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weapons "Skyrim:Weapons"). At the top is the entrance to the fort, while going deeper leads past a jail cell and ultimately to an officer's office and bedroom. The exit at the bottom will lead to a small smithing area on a porch that overlooks Whiterun Hold.

**Treasure**

- On top of the chimney in the first room stands a bucket with a random war axe lying on it and a random potion hidden inside the bucket.
- Two chests in the officer's office and bedroom.
- A key to Fort Sungard Jail on the officer's table.
- A [Scroll of Call to Arms](/wiki/Skyrim:Scroll_of_Call_to_Arms "Skyrim:Scroll of Call to Arms") under the officer's table.

**Other**

- A forge, grindstone, and workbench on the balcony that overlooks Whiterun.

### Fort Sungard Tower

The Tower is a four-story building with several exits to various levels of the fort. The bottom level leads to *[Fort Sungard Oubliette](#Fort_Sungard_Oubliette)*, the second level leads to the courtyard, the third level leads to the fort rooftops, and the top level leads to the tower's roof itself. A cart on the second level has two [moonstone ores](/wiki/Skyrim:Moonstone_Ore "Skyrim:Moonstone Ore") lying on it.

**Treasure**

- Two moonstone ores in a cart on the second level.
- Two leveled potions of any variety on a table, in the room with no door on the second level.
- A chest next to the shelf between the two spiral staircases on the second level.

### Fort Sungard Oubliette

The Oubliette is the jail tower of the fort. A ladder leads to the top of the tower, and a secret exit can be found on the bottom. The cells on the main floor are empty, but on the bottom floor there is a large drop down that can potentially kill very low level players. A bandit prisoner discovered this fact when he was cast into the oubliette and was crushed by the fall.

**Treasure**

- In the chamber after the large fall, next to the bandit corpse, are the [Pickpocket](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") skill book *[Guide to Better Thieving](/wiki/Skyrim:Guide_to_Better_Thieving "Skyrim:Guide to Better Thieving")* and a [Fort Sungard Jail Key](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Sungard_Jail_Key "Skyrim:Fort Sungard Jail Key"). A few [lockpicks](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") are scattered around the corpse and the locked door out of the area.

## Notes

- A [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Note_(Serpent%27s_Bluff) "Skyrim:Forsworn Note (Serpent's Bluff)") urging the Forsworn to hasten the taking of the fort is found in the tent with the boss chest at [Serpent's Bluff Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Serpent%27s_Bluff_Redoubt "Skyrim:Serpent's Bluff Redoubt").
- If you open the local map at the crossroads east of the fort, the area will be called "Granite Hill". [Granite Hill](/wiki/Lore:Granite_Hill "Lore:Granite Hill") was to be a village in [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") that was omitted from the final game, similar to [Heljarchen](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn#Notes "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") in [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). It is referenced in the game files, one of [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") [Siddgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Siddgeir "Skyrim:Siddgeir")'s conversations with his [steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steward "Skyrim:Steward") [Nenya](/wiki/Skyrim:Nenya "Skyrim:Nenya"), and in the book *[Holdings of Jarl Gjalund](/wiki/Skyrim:Holdings_of_Jarl_Gjalund "Skyrim:Holdings of Jarl Gjalund")*.
- The fort is very near [Hendraheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hendraheim_(place) "Skyrim:Hendraheim (place)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club"), which is to the southwest on the other side of the road.

## Bugs

- When exiting to the smithing balcony of the Annex, your follower may become trapped there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
  - You can fast travel with Fort Sungard as the destination to solve this.
  - If fast travel is not an option and you have a horse with you, you can use your horse to "push" your follower off the broken part of the smithing balcony. You can then have them follow you down the mountain and push them again onto the ground.
- The grindstone in the Annex may not be interactable.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.1, fixes this bug.
- If this is not the first [Civil War Fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts#Civil_War_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") you clear, after clearing it of [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"), soldiers will never garrison and enemies respawn instead. This is due to a hidden quest not ending after clearing the first Civil War Fort. See this [talk](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Fort_Hraggstad "Skyrim talk:Fort Hraggstad") section for info.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
  - The console command `resetquest CWFortObserver` can be used to reset the hidden quest, then clear the fort again. Repeat this for every Civil War Fort you want to be garrisoned.
- The 3 jail doors and frames are grossly oversized, causing them to clip through the fort structures when opened.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.1, fixes this bug.
- The Muster had a pair of fish racks set up to hold weapons, plus some shields stuck to the walls. All of these objects could easily be knocked down from various causes and turn the entire arrangement into a big mess.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.1, addresses this issue. Some invisible weapon and shield racks have been created to resolve this and keep the items from being knocked around needlessly.
- A Forsworn may spawn inside the Shrine, making it impossible to reach or kill them.
  - This can be remedied by standing to the left of the door and casting [rune spells](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") onto the lip part of the shrine.
- As you exit the Oubliette, you may encounter a group of three Forsworn who are not hostile, even if you haven't completed [No One Escapes Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:No_One_Escapes_Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:No One Escapes Cidhna Mine") in favor of the Forsworn. If you interact with them, they will simply say greetings and other random replies.
- Interacting with the cooking pot in the Muster will leave you standing on a foot of thin air as you enter the cooking menu and the animation begins, due to the pot being set up too high in the fireplace. **?**

Roadside Ruins

## Quick Walkthrough

1. You filled the Cup of Fortune.
2. Find a bed and sleep.
3. Read the note placed in your inventory while you slept.
4. choose the side and the way you do the job

### The Cup of Fortune

Go to sleep

After filling the cup labeled "Fortune", you will need to find a bed and sleep. There is a convenient bedroll nearby with a quest marker. Go to sleep and after awakening, you will receive a letter [Rogue's Job Offer](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue%27s_Job_Offer "Skyrim:Rogue's Job Offer") and a Spiked Vial in your inventory. Read the letter, you will learn of a High Elf named [Cuinanthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Cuinanthil "Skyrim:Cuinanthil") who is a rich mark begging to be robbed. Cuinanthil has just arrived in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") with his ever-present Dark Elf bodyguard [Inimoro](/wiki/Skyrim:Inimoro "Skyrim:Inimoro"). The rogue lets you know the treasure is being hidden somewhere in the Reach and lays out a plan to get to it. You find out the bodyguard has a weakness for Sujamma, a drink from his homeland. At this point two optional different objects appear, you can finish the quest in two ways.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Side with Cuinanthil** Steps  1. Inform Cuinanthil of the rogue's intentions. 2. Meet Cuinanthil in the Markarth Warrens. 3. Talk to Cuinanthil and get a small reward.   If your speech skill passes the [very hard](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech#Very_Hard "Skyrim:Speech") level, you can choose to find Cuinanthil in Marharth and talk him into believing someone is trying to rob him, he then will walk towards [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"), once inside The Warrens, you'll see Cuinanthil's guard [Inimoro](/wiki/Skyrim:Inimoro "Skyrim:Inimoro") kill a man named [Ernanthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ernanthil "Skyrim:Ernanthil"), you can find [Ernanthil's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ernanthil%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Ernanthil's Journal") within his inventory, revealing he's Cuinanthil's brother, but he got nothing from his father's will, so he seeks to fetch the treasure from his brother. There's also a note [On the Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:On_the_Bittercup "Skyrim:On the Bittercup") and the special potion [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup_Items#Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup Items") found on Ernanthil's body. There's also a courier's corpse besides Ernanthil's body.  You can drink Bittercup to permanently increase the greater of health, magicka or stamina stats by 20 points and decreases the lesser by 20 points. You can then speak with Cuinanthil to complete the quest, he will thank you and hand over 300 gold as a reward. Once complete the quest, you can kill Cuinanthil to get the [Key to Eslaf's room](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup_Items#Keys "Skyrim:Bittercup Items"). You can then access the room and take all of the treasure within, which includes a unique [Master's Transmute](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration_Spells#Master.27s_Transmute "Skyrim:Alteration Spells") spell tome. | **Side with Ernanthil** Steps  1. Create a Spiked Sujamma beverage. You may have to travel to Solstheim to get some. 2. Travel to Markarth and convince the owner of the Silver-Blood Inn to sell your beverage. This will make the bodyguard sick. 3. Pickpocket the mark, and steal the family Seal (ring). 4. Impersonate a courier. 5. Defeat the bodyguard. 6. Follow the mark to the treasure hiding place. 7. Defeat the mark.   The first thing you need to do is create a Spiked Sujamma drink to poison the bodyguard. One of the items left in your inventory is a vial of spiked poison. Sujamma is not sold by any of the traders in Skyrim so you may have to go to Solstheim to get some. After acquiring the Sujamma, go to a cookpot and mix the spiked vial with the Sujamma. Silver Blood Inn Cuinanthil and his bodyguard  Once you have the spiked drink head to Markarth and talk to the owner of the Silver-Blood Inn and convince him to sell your Sujamma. Your dialogue choices will include several price options to persuade him to buy your drink, or you can just give to him at no cost. He won't refuse free Sujamma so you will always have that option if your Speech skills are not high enough. Cuinanthil and his bodyguard will roam around the inn. The bodyguard will stay close to Cuinanthil at all times.  At some point he will take a break and drink the Spiked Sujamma and begin to get violently sick. He will remain this way for a long period of time. While the bodyguard is down, find and pickpocket the ring seal from Cuinanthil. Depending on how long it takes you to pickpocket Cuinanthil, the bodyguard will soon recover after you have successfully stolen the ring seal. Head out of the inn and follow the quest marker to the [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens") and enter the door.   I've been looking for you... The dead courier  Follow the quest marker into the Warrens until you come to the body of a dead courier. Read the [Rogue's Instructions](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue%27s_Instructions "Skyrim:Rogue's Instructions") nearby. They tell you to seal the letter with the ring, dress as the courier, and deliver the fake letter back to Cuinanthil. A [Letter from Cuinanthil's Steward](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Cuinanthil%27s_Steward "Skyrim:Letter from Cuinanthil's Steward") is made. Be sure to remove all your armor and disguise yourself as the courier. Seal the fake letter and head back to the inn. When you return to Cuinanthil, you must select the dialogue options that all couriers say in order to fool Cuinanthil.  Bodyguard in trouble  Say, "I've been looking for you..." and then, "Got something I'm supposed to deliver - your hands only." Cuinanthil will accept your ruse and read the letter. Then he accuses his bodyguard of wrongdoing. The bodyguard will start to fight city guards and civilians trying to escape his fate. You will get a quest update to help the guards kill the bodyguard. Once the bodyguard is dead, Cuinanthil will run out of the inn to check on his treasure. You are to follow him.   Hidden in plain sight The vault  Cuinanthil has taken you back to the Warrens, to a hidden vault deep in the squalor of the derelict district. Follow him into the vault area. While inside you will get a quest update to confront Cuinanthil. At this point the mysterious rogue will enter the vault behind you and confront Cuinanthil too. They will fight until Cuinanthil is dead. You will realize after reading Cuinanthil's journal that the two are brothers fighting over a large family fortune. Speak to [Ernanthil](/wiki/Skyrim:Ernanthil "Skyrim:Ernanthil") and, as a reward, you will get 1000 gold and a note [On the Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:On_the_Bittercup "Skyrim:On the Bittercup") and a special potion [Bittercup](/wiki/Skyrim:Bittercup_Items#Bittercup "Skyrim:Bittercup Items"). Killing Ernanthil is allowed after finishing the dialogue. You can steal all the loot at this point. |

## Notes

- The Spiked Vial uses the same model as the [Pest Poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Pest_Poison "Skyrim:Pest Poison") from the quest [Dampened Spirits](/wiki/Skyrim:Dampened_Spirits "Skyrim:Dampened Spirits").
- There are two variants of the "Rogue's Instructions" found on the dead courier in the Warrens. Each variant is gender dependent.
- The copy of the Unique "Master Transmute" spell tome is found within the large chest in the hidden vault.

## Bugs

- If you side with Ernanthil and assist the guards in killing Inimoro, you may receive a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:WIKill04RewardLetter "Skyrim:WIKill04RewardLetter") from Cuinanthil thanking you for killing Inimoro. You will get a [miscellaneous objective](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Quests "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Quests") to speak to Cuinanthil for a reward, which is impossible to complete as he will be hostile towards you while still alive. **?**
  - Using the console commands `setav aggression 0` and `stopcombat` on Cuinanthil will allow you to speak with him.

## Quest Stages

| Fortunate Son (ccKRTSSE001\_QuestFortune) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | After performing a ritual at the Roadside Ruins, I've woken up to find a letter on my person. I should read the letter to see what it's about. *Objective 10:* Read the Rogue's Job Offer |
| 20 |  | After performing a ritual at the Roadside Ruins, I've woken up to find a letter on my person. The letter was from a mysterious rogue, about a job in Markarth robbing a wealthy High Elf. *Objective 20:* Steal the ring seal from Cuinanthil  *Objective 40:* (Optional) Inform Cuinanthil of the rogue's intentions  *Objective 1:* (Optional) Mix a bottle of Spiked Sujamma at a cooking station |
| 1 |  | After performing a ritual at the Roadside Ruins, I've woken up to find a letter on my person. The letter was from a mysterious rogue, about a job in Markarth robbing a wealthy High Elf. To make the job simpler, I've crafted a bottle of spiked sujamma to give to the innkeeper. *Objective 30:* (Optional) Convince the inn's owners to sell your sujamma |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccKRTSSE001_QuestFortune stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccKRTSSE001_QuestFortune`.

# Skyrim:Four Shields Tavern

## Overview

Exterior of the Tavern

**Four Shields Tavern** is an inn in the village of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") in [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar"). It is the only building on the eastern side of the road through Dragon Bridge.

[Faida](/wiki/Skyrim:Faida "Skyrim:Faida") is the proprietor, and [Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") works there while learning the innkeeper trade, hoping to eventually establish her own inn.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Aldepius](/wiki/Skyrim:Aldepius "Skyrim:Aldepius") [CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier")  [Faida](/wiki/Skyrim:Faida "Skyrim:Faida") [Innkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Inns "Innkeeper") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") [Food and Drink](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Food and Drink")  [Varnius Junius](/wiki/Skyrim:Varnius_Junius "Skyrim:Varnius Junius")\* |

\* Varnius will only be present after his [petition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Man_Who_Cried_Wolf "Skyrim:The Man Who Cried Wolf") has been heard at the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace").

## Related Quests

- **[A False Front](/wiki/Skyrim:A_False_Front_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:A False Front (Stormcloaks)")**: Find and deliver some forged documents to the [Imperials](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion").
- **[Over the Edge](/wiki/Skyrim:Over_the_Edge "Skyrim:Over the Edge")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Steel_Soldier "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Steel Soldier"): A criminal has sensed his past catching up with him.

## Four Shields Tavern

Like all inns in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") the entrance leads directly into the common room, which has a fire pit down the middle of the room. There are five long wooden tables and benches against the side walls with a selection of bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") as well as a few loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") on all the tables. The left-hand table against the north wall also has a flower basket containing two [pine thrush eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") and a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), while the table in the southwestern corner also has several pieces of cheese and two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak") on it. There are several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels around the room, including one that is a fish barrel.

The counter is in front of the west wall and has a bottle of alto wine and several pieces of cheese on top. Underneath can be found a [steel warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Warhammer "Skyrim:Steel Warhammer"), three small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, fourteen bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), five loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") and a copy of *[Of Fjori and Holgeir](/wiki/Skyrim:Of_Fjori_and_Holgeir "Skyrim:Of Fjori and Holgeir")*. Along the west wall are five large vats with three racks hanging from the ceiling holding ten [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and six [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), with two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of dried [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") also hanging from the ceiling. There are three doorways off of this room, one to the north and two to the south. There is a set of shelves on either side of the doorway to the north holding two bottles of alto wine, six bottles of wine, seven bottles of Nord mead, four loaves of bread and three bunches of elves ear.

The bedroom to the north is the largest and can be rented for 10 septims per day. It contains a single bed in the northwestern corner, with two dressers along the north wall both containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") and having a bottle of alto wine, a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), three bottles of Nord mead, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on top of them. There is a large coin purse to the right of these, in the northeast corner with a few food sacks in a pile on the floor in front. Against the east wall is an unlocked long [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), while against the south wall is a square wooden table and chair with a [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") and [bowl](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl") on the table.

The left-hand bedroom to the south has an owned single bed in the southeastern corner, an unlocked chest at the foot of the bed, a round wooden table with a bottle of [Black-Briar mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Black-Briar_Mead "Skyrim:Black-Briar Mead") on top and a tall wardrobe against the east wall with copies of *[The Oblivion Crisis](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Oblivion_Crisis "Skyrim:The Oblivion Crisis")* and *[The "Madmen" of the Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_%22Madmen%22_of_the_Reach "Skyrim:The \"Madmen\" of the Reach")* on top. The other bedroom has an owned single bed in the southwestern corner, a chest at the foot of the bed, a round wooden table and chair next to the bed and a dresser against the west wall containing more clothes.

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Faida's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be [pickpocketed](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickpocket "Skyrim:Pickpocket") or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

## Bugs

- [Julienne Lylvieve](/wiki/Skyrim:Julienne_Lylvieve "Skyrim:Julienne Lylvieve") was meant to be Faida's backup for the Four Shields Tavern, but isn't because there is no backup alias.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Four Skull Lookout

## Overview

| [Ore Veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Mining "Skyrim:Mining") | |

Four Skull Lookout

**Four Skull Lookout** is a small [outdoor Nordic ruin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic_Dwellings "Skyrim:Nordic Dwellings") south of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit").

It is one of the three ruins visited for the quest [Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell"). With the [Divine Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, the named bandits [Eigorn](/wiki/Skyrim:Eigorn "Skyrim:Eigorn"), [Oren](/wiki/Skyrim:Oren "Skyrim:Oren"), [Remy](/wiki/Skyrim:Remy "Skyrim:Remy"), and [Viparth](/wiki/Skyrim:Viparth "Skyrim:Viparth") can be found here. They are in possession of the Crusader's Relics.

## Related Quests

- **[Destruction Ritual Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction_Ritual_Spell "Skyrim:Destruction Ritual Spell")**: Learn the most powerful [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction") spells Skyrim has to offer.
- **[Relics of the Crusader](/wiki/Skyrim:Relics_of_the_Crusader "Skyrim:Relics of the Crusader")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Divine_Crusader "Skyrim:Divine Crusader"): Reclaim the holy relics of Pelinal Whitestrake.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

The easiest approach to the ruin is from the [Red Eagle Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Eagle_Redoubt "Skyrim:Red Eagle Redoubt") lower camp (before the ascent). The ruin consists of a single room with open doorways to the northwest and southeast. It contains a single unlocked chest containing [leveled loot](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists "Skyrim:Leveled Lists") next to a campfire, with a searchable pot hanging over it and two unowned bedrolls around it. Next to one of these are an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword") and [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield"). Outside, in front of the northwestern doorway, is a pedestal, with a chair off to the left. It is the home of three bandits: a warrior, archer, and wizard.

There are three [juniper trees](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") around the ruin, and a birds' nest containing a [pine thrush egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Pine_Thrush_Egg "Skyrim:Pine Thrush Egg") lodged against the southwestern side of the ruin. One [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") plant can be found to the left of the southeastern doorway. Nearby is a leveled animal that may get drawn into any battle with the bandits.

## Notes

- Directly west of the ruin, on a promontory toward the cliff, a [shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar") can be found along with minor loot including a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe"), a couple of rolls of paper, several loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), and a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse").
- A [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") can be found among the rocks just in front of the pedestal.
- The bandits do not seem to respawn.[*verification needed — See [discussion](/wiki/Skyrim_talk:Four_Skull_Lookout "Skyrim talk:Four Skull Lookout")*]
- Four Skull Lookout also [appears](/wiki/Online:Four_Skull_Lookout "Online:Four Skull Lookout") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionReach](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach "Skyrim:CrimeFactionReach"); [MS02VictimsFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MS02VictimsFaction "Skyrim:MS02VictimsFaction"); [MarkarthKlepprFrabbiFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthKlepprFrabbiFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthKlepprFrabbiFaction"); [MarkarthNaiveFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthNaiveFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthNaiveFaction"); [MarkarthSilverBloodInnFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthSilverBloodInnFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthSilverBloodInnFaction"); [MarkarthSilverBloodInnWorkerFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:MarkarthSilverBloodInnWorkerFaction "Skyrim:MarkarthSilverBloodInnWorkerFaction"); [ServicesMarkarthSilverFishInn](/wiki/Skyrim:ServicesMarkarthSilverFishInn "Skyrim:ServicesMarkarthSilverFishInn"); [TownMarkarthFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction "Skyrim:TownMarkarthFaction") | | |

Frabbi

**Frabbi** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [food vendor](/wiki/Skyrim:Food_Vendor "Skyrim:Food Vendor") who works in the [Silver-Blood Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver-Blood_Inn "Skyrim:Silver-Blood Inn") in the city of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). Her husband is [Kleppr](/wiki/Skyrim:Kleppr "Skyrim:Kleppr") and they have a daughter, [Hroki](/wiki/Skyrim:Hroki "Skyrim:Hroki"), and a son, [Hreinn](/wiki/Skyrim:Hreinn "Skyrim:Hreinn"). She has an acerbic relationship with her husband, though she will [dislike](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") you if you kill him. She is also available for information during [The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy"). If Kleppr dies, Frabbi will take over all innkeeper services at the Silver-Blood Inn, including renting out beds and giving rumors.

She was supposed to sleep from midnight to 8am, but a [bug](#Bugs) prevents her from doing so. She spends the rest of the day working in the inn. She can be found leaning on the wall, sweeping the floor, as well as warming herself near the hearth.

Frabbi wears a set of barkeep [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#0005b6a1 "Skyrim:Clothes") and [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Shoes#0005b6a0 "Skyrim:Shoes"), and carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), some [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"), and the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Margret%27s_Room "Skyrim:Key to Margret's Room") to [Margret](/wiki/Skyrim:Margret "Skyrim:Margret")'s room.

## Related Quests

- **[The Forsworn Conspiracy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Forsworn_Conspiracy "Skyrim:The Forsworn Conspiracy")**: Investigate a murder in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") to discover a sinister plot surrounding the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

While in the Silver-Blood Inn, she will greet you with:

:   *"Unlike my husband Kleppr, I watch after our guests."*
:   *"Now you just tell me if you need something."*
:   *"You come right to me if you find an unwashed floor or lumpy bed."*
:   *"I'll bend Kleppr's ear if there's anything wrong with a room you rent."*
:   *"Isn't my son Hreinn such a good worker? Not like his father at all...."*

If Kleppr is dead:

:   *"My worthless husband is gone, so I run the inn now."*
:   *"I can't believe the mess Kleppr left things in. I have twice the work with him gone."*

When spoken to:

:   **Where can I learn more about magic?**
:   *"Magic? Got no good use for that here. Mages keep to their [College](/wiki/Skyrim:College_of_Winterhold_(place) "Skyrim:College of Winterhold (place)") in [Winterhold](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold "Skyrim:Winterhold"). Go bother them. Wish the Jarl's wizard would up and leave with ya."*

When asked for rumors:

:   *"[Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") the beggar got himself kicked out the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella"). Caused quite the ruckus."*
:   *"They say that something happened in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)"). [Brother Verulus](/wiki/Skyrim:Brother_Verulus "Skyrim:Brother Verulus") has the whole place closed."*
:   *"A witchhunter from the Priesthood of Stendarr is in town. He's asking a lot of questions about that old [abandoned house](/wiki/Skyrim:Abandoned_House "Skyrim:Abandoned House")."*

When you part ways with her:

:   *"I should remind Kleppr to clean this place up."*
:   *"Bye, now."*

### The Forsworn Conspiracy

During The Forsworn Conspiracy, you are to find out why a woman named [Margret](/wiki/Skyrim:Margret "Skyrim:Margret") was attacked in the local marketplace. You are told that she stayed in the Silver-Blood Inn, where either Kleppr or Frabbi can be of help in the investigation. Should you ask Frabbi if Margret stayed in the inn:

:   *"Ah, yes. Rented the nicest room we had for a whole month."*

If Margret survived the attack, Frabbi will continue:

:   *"I think she's sitting by the fire. Poor girl."*

If not, she will instead say:

:   *"Best we all forget about her. Bad luck to talk about the dead in Markarth."*

:   **Do you have the key to Margret's room?**
:   *"Of course. But I can't just hand that over. Privacy, after all."*

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **I won't tell anyone. Promise.** **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Well, you seem like the honest sort. Here you are."* **Failed**:*"Right. You adventuring types would never go into a room just to steal everything."* | | | | **Passed**: Continue investigation **Failed**: Nothing |
| **Maybe I could rent the room?** **(Bribe)** | **Passed**:*"Well, I guess Margret isn't around to complain. It's yours."* **Failed**:*"Sorry. Margret might be dead, but the room's rented."* | | | | **Passed**: Continue investigation **Failed**: Nothing |
| **Hand the key over. Now.** **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**:*"All right. I don't want any trouble. It's yours."* **Failed**:*"Are you serious? I say more threatening words to my husband."* | | | | **Passed**: Continue investigation **Failed**: Nothing |
| Never mind, then. | Did you need anything else? | | | | Nothing |

## Conversations

Even while they're working, Frabbi and Kleppr's exchanges are rife with sarcasm and hostility. One case is when he overhears her telling you, *"Unlike my husband Kleppr, I watch after our guests."*, as he will yell, *"What was that you said, venomous wife of mine?"* She will yell back, *"Nothing, you pig-headed oaf!"* Similarly, when you enter the kitchen or take a seat, Kleppr will call her to serve you a drink: *"Frabbi, a customer needs a drink!"* She will approach you to offer you a beverage, but not before she snaps at him: *"Too lazy to give him*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *a drink yourself? Oaf."* At other times, they will throw snide remarks at each other:

**Frabbi**: *"All the wood furniture in this inn is rotting to the core. Do you know why that is, Kleppr?"*
**Kleppr**: *"I don't know, my darling wife. I assume you're going to tell me?"*
**Frabbi**: *"It's rotten because the wood is cheap and its*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *soaked with ale! Now we'll have to replace all the furniture before bugs set in."*
**Kleppr**: *"Don't worry, my love. Just show the bugs your adoring face, and they'll scurry away in complete fear in no time."*
**Frabbi**: *"You're an idiot, Kleppr. Why did I ever marry you?"*
**Kleppr**: *"Not a day goes by I don't ask that question myself, my dear."*

**Kleppr**: *"Frabbi, my dear loving wife, could you please clean out our guest rooms?"*
**Frabbi**: *"Clean the rooms yourself Kleppr. It's not like you do anything important around here."*
**Kleppr**: *"No, just check in the guests and manage the coin and keep a roof over your head. No, nothing important."*

**Frabbi**: *"Kleppr, you idiot! Can't you do anything right?"*
**Kleppr**: *"What? What did I do this time? I was just standing here!"*
**Frabbi**: *"You were just standing there when you were supposed to be serving drinks to our customers!"*
**Kleppr**: *"Shouldn't you be helping me then, wife of mine? Sharing my problems? Being my better half?"*
**Frabbi**: *"I am your better half. And your better half is telling you to stop being an idiot and serve the customers their drinks!"*

However, she is much more amicable towards her son Hreinn, doting on him:

**Frabbi**: *"How are your chores coming, son?"*
**Hreinn**: *"I've been cleaning up spills and there is fresh linen for the rooms."*
**Frabbi**: *"Aren't you wonderful! Why can't your father be more like you and your sister?"*
**Hreinn**: *"Are you going to walk over to father and start hitting him again?"*
**Frabbi**: *"No, not right now. Maybe later, if I'm still upset."*

Meanwhile, Kleppr denies that they bicker so often:

**Hreinn**: *"Father, why do you and mother fight so much?"*
**Kleppr**: *"We don't fight, son. We, um, talk. Loudly."*
**Hreinn**: *"Will I need to talk so loudly with my wife when I get married?"*
**Kleppr**: *"[Dibella's](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella") Heart, son, I hope not."*

## Notes

- If both Kleppr and Frabbi die, Hreinn was supposed to take over as innkeeper. If Hreinn were to die, Hroki would take over as innkeeper. Surprisingly, if they all died, [Rhiada](/wiki/Skyrim:Rhiada "Skyrim:Rhiada") will take over the Silver-Blood Inn, though she will remain in [the Treasury House](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Treasury_House "Skyrim:The Treasury House").

## Bugs

- According to her packages, Frabbi was meant to sleep from midnight to 8am in the inn, but she will not.[*verification needed — Why doesn't the package activate?*] **?**

Fralia Gray-Mane

**Fralia Gray-Mane** is an [elderly](/wiki/Skyrim:Elder "Skyrim:Elder") [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker") living in [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"). She is the wife of the famous blacksmith [Eorlund Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Eorlund_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Eorlund Gray-Mane"), and the mother of [Avulstein](/wiki/Skyrim:Avulstein_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Avulstein Gray-Mane"), [Thorald](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane"), and [Olfina](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfina_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Olfina Gray-Mane"). During the day she runs a stall at the Whiterun market, where she sells tools, weapons and other minor trinkets. Contrary to the claims of [Olfrid](/wiki/Skyrim:Olfrid_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Olfrid Battle-Born") and [Idolaf Battle-Born](/wiki/Skyrim:Idolaf_Battle-Born "Skyrim:Idolaf Battle-Born"), she believes that her missing son Thorald is still alive, and will pay you if you [investigate this matter](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action").

She visits the [Temple of Kynareth](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Kynareth "Skyrim:Temple of Kynareth") at 5am, staying there until 7am before returning to her house. While at home, she can be found eating, sleeping, or relaxing. At 8am she heads to the local marketplace to work at her stall until 6pm, when she goes home to do the cooking.

Fralia wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"), and a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat#000209aa "Skyrim:Hat"). She is equipped with a [Skyforge steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Dagger"), and carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Key to House Gray-Mane") to [the clan's house](/wiki/Skyrim:House_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:House Gray-Mane"), as well as a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Missing In Action](/wiki/Skyrim:Missing_In_Action "Skyrim:Missing In Action")**: Rescue a [missing Stormcloak supporter](/wiki/Skyrim:Thorald_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Thorald Gray-Mane") from the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor").

## Dialogue

Her greetings:

:   *"Bits and baubles for sale, all crafted by the best blacksmith in Skyrim."*
:   *"My Eorlund is the finest blacksmith in Skyrim, and that's not just a wife's boasting."*
:   *"I can't stand those braggart Battle-Borns. They think they're the gods' gift to Whiterun."*
:   *"Eorlund and I... we both miss our son terribly. Thorald... he went missing, fighting the Imperials."*
:   *"Everyone thinks Thorald is dead. But not me. I know my boy is alive out there. Somewhere..."*
:   *"I...I miss our son terribly, especially since Eorlund died. Thorald... he went missing, fighting the Imperials."* **(Eorlund is dead)**
:   *"Never much cared for that [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater") myself. He was in the [Empire's](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") pocket, so to speak."* **(If Stormcloaks control Whiterun)**
:   *"If only you could help bring my son back to me."*

Topics:

:   **Who's the best blacksmith in Skyrim?**
:   *"I can tell you're new around here, askin' a question like that. My husband Eorlund tends the [Skyforge](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge "Skyrim:Skyforge") up at [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr"), the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") mead hall. There's no finer smith in the nine holds. You should ask him about his work. It's the only subject that'll get him talking. Well, that and maybe those stuck-up, dung-sniffing Battle-Borns."*
:   **The Battle-Borns?**
:   *"Don't even get me started on that lot. They put on airs like they're somethin' special. Sure, they've got money, but they ain't got a shred of honor between 'em. Gray-Mane. Now that's a name fills you with pride. We've got roots in Whiterun. We've got history."*
:   **Where's Jorrvaskr?**
:   *"Head up the steps from the market an' look to your right. Can't miss it."*

However, you will not hear her comment on the Battle-Born clan if Eorlund is dead but she will still give you directions to Jorrvaskr:

:   **Who's the best blacksmith in Skyrim?**
:   *"Curse you for bringing up that bitter memory. Not long ago it was my husband Eorlund. There was no finer smith in the nine holds. Now he's dead and gone and the Skyforge of Jorrvaskr lies cold."*

If the stormcloaks control Whiterun:

:   **Are you pleased to see the Stormcloaks in charge?**
:   *"Pleased enough, I suppose. At least they appreciate the ways and traditions of the Nord people. Can't say I ever much liked the idea of the Empire telling us what to do an' how to do it."*

Her goodbyes:

:   *"If you need any jewelry, just let me know."*
:   *"You take care of yourself, now."*

When she is operating her stall, she will promote her jewelry to passersby:

:   *"Bits and baubles for sale, all crafted by the best blacksmith in Skyrim."*
:   *"Come see my collection of Gray-Mane's finest trinkets! You'll not find their like in all Tamriel!"*
:   *"Shiny trinkets for your good lady! All crafted by the great Eorlund Gray-Mane himself!"*

### Missing In Action

*"What of Thorald? Is he nothing? So don't talk to me about suffering!"*

Said feud may unfold at the Whiterun marketplace:

**Olfrid**: *"Foolish old woman! You know nothing! Nothing of our struggles, our suffering!"*
**Fralia**: *"Nothing? And what of my son? Hmm? What of Thorald? Is he nothing? So don't talk to me about suffering!"*
**Idolaf**: *"Your son chose his side, and he chose poorly. And now he's gone. Such is the way of war. The sooner you accept his loss, the better."*
**Fralia**: *"I will never accept his death! My son still lives. I feel it in my heart. So tell me, Battle-Borns, where is he? Where are you holding my Thorald?"*
**Olfrid**: *"Do you believe this old hag? 'Holding him'? Why I've got him in my cellar. He's my prisoner. Face it, cow! Your stupid son is dead! He died a Stormcloak traitor. And you... you best keep your mouth shut before you suffer the same."*
**Idolaf**: *"Come on, father. There's nothing more to be said here."*

If you speak to her after this:

:   *"All I can think about is my son, my Thorald... they say that he was killed, but I know better. I know my son is alive! Those Battle-Born... they're in with the Imperials. They know it too, and yet they lie to my very face!"*

:   :   **How do you know they're lying?**
    :   *"It's not wise to discuss it here. Please, if you truly wish to help, meet me at my home. I'll tell you the whole story."*

:   :   **How can you be sure your son is alive?**
    :   *"I just... I just know it. I can feel it in my heart. You have to believe me. Please, visit me at my home. I can tell you the whole story."*

You will need to meet her at her house to discuss this any further. Otherwise, if you attempt to ask her about her missing son. she will refuse to answer:

:   *"Please, let's speak privately."*
:   **Can you tell me more about your missing son?**
:   *"Not here. Let's speak at my home, where we can be alone, unwatched."*

When the two of you enter House Gray-Mane, she will say:

:   *"Welcome to our home."*

A Nord man will run up to you, armed with a battleaxe and asking her:

:   **Avulstein:** *"Mother, what's the meaning of this? Who have you brought into our home?"*
:   **Fralia**: *"Avulstein, put that down! He's/She's here to help us find Thorald!"*
:   **Avulstein**: *"All right, mother."*
:   **Fralia**: *"I can't take any more of this. No weapons, please. Let's just talk."*
:   **Avulstein**: *"We can't trust anyone! Who knows what they'll do if they find me here. How do we know he's/she's not spying for the Battle-Born? This was foolish!"*

You can ask Fralia more questions:

:   **Can you tell me anything else about what's going on?**
:   *"Thorald's disappearance has been hard on all of us, but Avulstein has taken it badly. He's afraid of being taken as well, so he hasn't left the house. All he talks about is Thorald. Please, help Avulstein if you can. Something has to be done, or we're all going to lose our minds."*

:   **How can you be sure Thorald is still alive?**
:   *"He's my son. I just... I feel it in my heart. You'd understand if you had children."*

:   **Why do you think the Battle-Borns are involved?**
:   *"It's hardly a secret that they have ties to the Empire, and hate anyone who speaks out against it. Thorald did worse. He took action against the Empire, and the Battle-Borns knew it."*

Now speak to Avulstein to hear what he wants: proof that Thorald is imprisoned somewhere. Once you have [such proof](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Missive_(Battle-Born) "Skyrim:Imperial Missive (Battle-Born)"), you can optionally show it to Fralia, who will be overjoyed:

:   *"I knew he wasn't gone, I just knew it! Please, get that to Avulstein right away."*

After delivering the proof to Avulstein, she can be found worrying about Thorald:

:   *"Please tell me you have news of my son."*

From the Imperial missive, you know Thorald is being held at [Northwatch Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Northwatch_Keep "Skyrim:Northwatch Keep"). Rescue him from the clutches of the [Thalmor](/wiki/Skyrim:Thalmor "Skyrim:Thalmor"). He will express his utmost gratitude for saving his life, but he still fears for his own safety. He plans to join the Stormcloaks as Whiterun is no longer safe for him and his brother.

Now that Thorald is safe, bring the good news to an eager Fralia:

:   **Thorald is safe.**
:   *"Is he? You've saved him?! I must see him at once!"*
:   **I'm afraid he's not here. He didn't think it was safe to return.**
:   *"What? After all this, I can't even see him? How... How do I know you're telling me the truth, and not just what I want to hear?"*
:   **He said to tell you to "suffer the winter's cold wind."**
:   *"'...for it bears aloft next summer's seeds.' That's my boy. So it's true, then. For now, it's enough to know that he's alive. I can find peace in that. Thank you, dear friend. You've given me back my son."*

If Eorlund is alive, she will reward you with an enchanted weapon:

:   *"I'd had Eorlund forge this for Thorald. It was to be a present for his return. I suppose he can't have it now. Why don't you take it? We can always make another for the day when this war ends and Thorald can come home."*

If he is dead, she will instead hand you some leveled gold:

:   *"With Eorlund gone, I'm afraid I can't offer you much in the way of thanks. But please, take this. It's the least I can do."*

From now on, you can hear Fralia speak highly of her son:

:   *"Oh, I always knew my Thorald was alive. Ain't a man in Skyrim who can keep a Gray-Mane down."*

:   **Have you heard from your sons?**
:   *"No, nor do I expect to. Would be too dangerous for now. It's enough for me to know that they're out there somewhere, and together again."*

## Conversations

While she tends her stall, she will chat with her customers:

**[Ysolda](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysolda "Skyrim:Ysolda")**: *"Fralia, do you ever deal with the Khajiit at all? I'm sure they would love to trade in your husband's steel."*
**Fralia**: *"Plenty of people here that need Eorlund's craftsmanship, my dear. We've never had any reason to deal with those caravans of theirs."*

**[Lillith](/wiki/Skyrim:Lillith_Maiden-Loom "Skyrim:Lillith Maiden-Loom")**: *"Hello, Fralia dear."*
**Fralia**: *"Lillith - always a pleasure. Just browsing, or were you looking for something particular?"*
**Lillith**: *"Funny you should ask. I'm in the market for a new locket. Something in polished silver, maybe. Big enough to hold, say, a folded-up letter?"*
**Fralia**: *"Ahhh, I see. I think I know just what you need. I don't have anything like that here now, but my Eorlund - he can make you one right quick. When I get home, I'll have him start on it right away. Come back to pick it up in, oh... three days?"*
**Lillith**: *"Perfect, my dear. Absolutely perfect. I'll see you then."*

She will occasionally run into her husband, who will barely say much:

**Fralia**: *"Eorlund, dearest, are you hungry? Would you like me to fix you something?"*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*
**Fralia**: *"A venison pie, maybe? With a nice cup of mulled mead?"*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*

**Fralia**: *"When will you be makin' some more jewelry, love? Some silver lockets and amulets would fetch a nice price at the stand."*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*
**Fralia**: *"Wonderful, dear. Thank you."*
**Eorlund**: *"Hrm."*

## Notes

- When you ask him for a sword, Eorlund will comment, *"A blade! It will be as sharp as Fralia's tongue!"* He was also supposed to admit, *"My poor Fralia thinks Thorald's still alive, but I know better."* However, the condition for this line is incorrectly set to stage 1000 of [In My Time Of Need](/wiki/Skyrim:In_My_Time_Of_Need "Skyrim:In My Time Of Need"), meaning it cannot be heard.
- If Avulstein is dead, Thorald was intended to say, *"I don't dare return to Whiterun. But my mother... She'll need some consolation. Tell her... tell her to suffer the winter's cold wind, for it bears aloft next summer's seeds. She'll understand."* If asked about Thorald after the quest, Fralia was also supposed to reply, '*No, nor do I expect to. Would be too dangerous for now. It's enough for me to know that he's out there somewhere, and not locked up like an animal in a cage."* As Avulstein is essential, these lines cannot normally be heard.

## Bugs

- Fralia has no sleep package, making it impossible for her to do so.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- Fralia's merchant chest is owned by [Anoriath](/wiki/Skyrim:Anoriath "Skyrim:Anoriath") instead of her.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Her conversations with Lilith and Ysolda may still take place if Eorlund is dead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.6, fixes this bug.
